(77) 'janalokAdiH' ityatra tu janatyAgena janAkhyalokasyaiva pratipattayarthaM lokashabdaprayoga iti j~neyam | janalokAdirityatra tatpuruSho bahuvrIhishcha vivakShitaH | tushabdo visheShArthaH | tathA cha 'madhyamAt' viShNoH prasAdAt janalokasyAdirmaharlokaH janatapolokAdireva vA bhavati na muktiH | 'muktidastu' uttamaprasAda eva prakIrtito vR^iddhaiH, na tvanyAviti yojanA | tathA cha karmAdinA bhagavatprasAdasiddhAvapi 
tasyAnuttamatvAt j~nAnasAdhyasyaivottamatvAt anuttamena svargAdimAtrasiddhAvapi mokShAsiddheH tatsAdhanaprasAdAya j~nAnamapekShitamiti bhAvaH | na chAtra "IyustrIn karmaNA lokAn j~nAnenaiva taduttarAn" iti vAkyavirodhaH shaN^kyaH, tasya maharlokasthAkR^itakabhAgaviShayatvAt, asya cha punarAvartyabhAgaviShayatvAt, 'sAmAnyadarshanAllokAH' iti pramANabalena j~nAnashabdasya svabimbaviShayayogyAparokSha- vyatiriktasAmAnyAvatArA- dyaparokShaviShayatvAt, tasya cha shravaNAdibhirityatra hyAdipadena grahaNAdvA; nyAyAmR^itoktarItyA j~nAnadvAreti sheShakaraNAdvA; evakArasyAyogavyavachChedArthatvAdvA na virodhaH |
(78) nanvastUttamaprasAdAya j~nAnApekShA, tathApi "karmaNA j~nAnamAtanoti" ityAdeH karmAdinAspi j~nAnaM bhavatIti na tadarthaM jij~nAsA kartavyA "AtmA" iti vAkyesnyaniShedhAbhAvAdityAshaN^kAM prakR^itapramANasheSheNa pariharati - 'shravaNaM' iti | atra evakArasya dvirgrahaNaM sarvatra sambandhaj~nApanAya | te cha shravaNAdInAM kAryasAdhane anyasAhitya- nirAsaktAH, "naraM cha nArAyaNameva" ityAdAviva anabhimatakarmAdivyAvartakAshcha | dvayordvayossamuchchaye 'cha' shabdau | 'tathA' shabda upamAyAm | 'tathaiva cha' iti nipAtasamudAyo vA | bhaktigrahaNaM prasaN^gAt dR^iShTAntArthaM vA |
(79) tathA cha 'j~nAnasampattau' aparokShaj~nAnaprAptau yathA bhaktistathA shravaNAdyeva sAdhanaM, nAnyatkarmAdItyarthaH | kA gatistarhi "karmaNA j~nAnamAtanoti" ityAdivachanasyetyata Aha - 'pradhAnaM' iti | shravaNAdi pradhAnaM sAdhanaM 'anyat' apradhAnamityeva 'iShyate' abhyupeyate prAmANikaiH, na tvanyat sAdhanameva neti yojanA | apradhAnasAdhanaviShayaM karmAdivachanamiti bhAvaH |
(80) viparItaM kiM na syAdityata Aha - 'na cha' iti | chashabdospyarthaH | tathA cha 'etAni' shravaNAdIni 'vinA kashchit' api adhikArI 'kutashchana' karmAdessataH 'j~nAnaM nApa' evametAni shravaNAdIni santichet kutashcha karmAdervinA j~nAnaM nApeti neti yojanA | tathA cha nirapekShAnvayavyatirekAbhyAM shravaNAdyeva j~nAne pradhAnaM sAkShAtsAdhanaM, karmAdi tu tadabhAvAt pAramparyeNa sAdhanamiti na vaiparItyamiti bhAvaH | 'nAradIye' 'yata uktaM' iti sheShaH | asya 'ato "yato nArAyaNa" ityAdinoktaM yuktaM' ityupaskR^itavAkyenAnvayaH | 'yato nArAyaNa' ityanena jij~nAsAyAH nirviShayatvashaN^kAnirAsAya prayuktaH sautro brahmashabdo nArAyaNapara iti vyAkhyAtaH |
(81) nanu nArAyaNaprasAdamR^ite na mokShashchet tarhi tajjij~nAsaiva kartavyA na brahmajij~nAsA | na cha vAchyaM 
nArAyaNa eva brahmapadena vivakShitaH sUtrakR^iteti, brahmashabdasya bahvarthatvena sUtrakAravivakShAvisheShasya durj~neyatvAdityata Aha - 'brahma' iti | mukhya iti sheShaH | chaH 'anekArthospi brahmashabdaH' iti apyarthe, yata ityarthe cha | tathA cha brahmashabdasyAnekArthatvespi yataH saH viShNAveva mukhyaH ato mukhyAmukhyayormukhyasyaiva grAhyatvAt sa eva sUtrakAra- vivakShito j~nAyata iti yojanA | atra shabdAntaraM vihAya viShNushabdaprayogeNa tachChabdagatAnAM vargapaà¤¼JNchamaShaShThachaturthAnAM NaShavAnAM saN^khyArekhAlekhanena sUtrANAM chatuShShaShTyuttarapaJNchashatasaN^khyoktA bhavati | yadvA - 
deshataH kAlatashchaiva guNatashchApi pUrtitaH |
viShNau brahmeti nAmaitanmukhyatonyatra na kvachit ||
ityaitareyabhAShyokteH deshakAlaguNAparichChedarUpatrividhapUrtivAchakabrahmashabdavyAkhyAnAya tAdR^ishaviShNushabdaprayogaH| TIkAyAM tu - atra viShNugrahaNena "saviShNurAha hi | taM brahmetyAchakShate" ityanyonyAvyavahitasUtradvayakaraNAnantarameva brahmamI- mAMsAyAH vyAsenArabdhatvAdetadavyavahitadevamImAMsAntyasUtradvaye brahmatvena nArAyaNasyaiva prakR^itatvaM sUchayatIti prayojanA- ntaramuktam | tattvapradIpespyetadeva 'yashcha devatAmImAMsAnte "viShNureva hi tat shrutestaM brahmetyAchakShate" iti sarvadevottamatvena pratij~nAto brahmatvena choktaH, sa eva brahmashabdenottaramImAMsAyAM vichAryatvenochyate' iti pAThabhedenoktam|
(82) brahmashabdasyAnyatrApi rUDhatvAdrUDhereva mukhyavR^ittitvAtkutossau viShNAveva mukhya ityata Aha - 'yaM' iti| 'brahmashabdashcha' ityAdi atrApi sambadhyate | cho yadyapItyAdyarthe | hishabdo yata ityarthe | shrutirAheti sheShaH | tathA cha yadyapi brahmashabdosnyatra rUDhaH, tathApi 'shrutiH' "yamanta" ityAdikA yataH kavInAM mate 'tadeva paramaM brahma' ityAhuriti prayogabAhulyarUpAM rUDhimAha, ato brahmashabdo viShNAveva paramamukhya ityarthaH | anyatrAj~narUDheH  vidvadrUDheratimukhyatvA- diti bhAvaH | yamantassamudre iti vAkyam -
yadoShadhIbhiH puruShAn pashUMshcha vivesha bhUtAni charAcharANi |
ataH paraM nAnyadaNIyasaM hi parAtparaM yanmahato mahAntam ||
yadekamavyaktamanantarUpaM vishvaM purANaM tamasaH parastAt ||
iti vAkyena saha vyAkhyAtaM viShNutattvanirNayaTIkAyAm | tathA hi - 'yamantassamudre' vibhakttayarthesvyayIbhAvaH samudrasyAntassthitaM 'kavayo' j~nAninaH 'avayanti' IShadeva jAnanti, yasmin 'tadakShare' avij~neyatvarUpapUrvavisheShaNa- vishiShTe prasiddhe vA avinAshini 'parame' prajA adhInAH santi |
(83) 'jagataH prasUtI' prasUtirjanayitrI mUlaprakR^itirlakShmIH 'yato' yasmAt prasUtA utpannA, sR^iShTau 
abhimukhI- babhUveti vA, yachcha yadvastu 'toyena' tattajjIvakarmaNA svavIryeNa vA, toyashabdoktAmbUpalakShitairbhUtairvA 'bhUmyAM' pR^ithivyAdiShu lokeShu 'jIvAn vyasasarja' vividhaM sasarja |
(84)-(85) yachcha 'oShadhIbhiH' sahitAn 'puruShAn pashUMshcha charAcharANi bhUtAni' preraNAya 'vivesha' | 'charAcharANi bhUtAni' ityanenaiva siddhe yaj~nAN^gatvAdinA vishiShTAnAM vrIhyoShadhInAM grahaNAya punarvachanam | 'ataH' yasmAt 'paraM' atishayena 'anyat' vastu 'aNIyasaM' aNIyo nAsti, yachcha 'parAtparaM' utkR^iShTAdutkR^iShTaM 'mahato' mahatparimANAdapi 'mahAntaM' mahat, 'yadekaM' kevalaM 'avyaktaM' svaprasAdaM vinA atIndriyaM 'vishvaM pUrNaM tamasaH' prakR^iteraj~nAnAdvA 'parastAt' atikramya sthitaM 'tadevartaM' yathArthaj~nAnarUpaM 'tadu' tadeva 'satyaM' j~nAnapUrvakriyAvat 'tadeva kavInAM' mate 'paramaM' mukhyaM 'brahma' ityAhuriti | atra 'tadakShare' iti shrutipAThaH | 'yadakShare' iti kvachitpAThe yasminnityadhyAhAro na kAryaH | 'vyasasarja' iti prAyikaH shrutipAThaH |  'vyachasarja' ityapi kvachitpaThanti | atra sakArasya chakArAdeshaH ChAndasaH | AdyapakShespi vi A sasarjetyavayavavibhAgaH tatrAN^o hrasvatvaM ChAndasaM bahulagraha- NAt | "indrA varuNa vAmaham" iti shrutau NakArAtparasyAkArasya yathA hrasvatvaM tadvaditi nArAyaNapaNDitA- chAryoktiH| "vyasasarja visasarja bahulagrahaNAt" iti prameyadIpoktirapi hrasvAbhiprAyikaiva | kechittu liTyaDAgamaH ChAndaso bahulagrahaNAditi prameyadIpArthamAhuH | tadAryoktAtpakShAntaram | padmanAbhatIrthakR^itatattvanirNayaTIkAyAM nyAyaratnAvalyAM tu 'vayanti' iti vichChidya 'tadakShare' ityeva cha paThitvA, "yaM puruShaM samudresntaH kavayo vayanti vAJNChanti tadakShare yasmin tasmin akShare nAshavarjite parame prajAstadAdhArAH tiShThanti, jagataH prasUtI jagajjanayitrI prakR^itiH yataH prasUtA prAdurbhUtA satI toyena itaramishritena jIvAn dehavattvena vyasasarja visR^iShTavatI" ityekAnvayena "tadeva tAtparyaviShayIbhUtatvAdR^itaM tadevAbAdhitarUpatvAtsatyaM tadeva kavInAmabhimataM paraM brahma" ityartha uktaH | nArAyaNapaNDitAryakR^itau tattvamaà¤¼JNjaryAmapi 'tadakShare' iti paThitvA "yamavayanti avagachChanti yasmiMstasmin akShare prajAH santi yataH prasUtA parAdhInavisheShaM prAptA shrIH toyena karmaNA jIvAn bhUmyAM prakR^ityAM vyasasarja" ityanvayena "tadevartaM shashvadekaprakAraM satyaM sAdhu guNapUrNaM" ityartha uktaH |
(86) nanu 'tadeva' iti vAkye tachChabdena kuto viShNunishchayaH? samudrasthatvaliN^gAditi chet - na, tasya rudrAdAvapi kathaJNchitsambhavAdityato niravakAshaviShNushruterevetyAha - 'tannaH' iti | 'iti vachanAdviShNureva' 'tatra' "tadeva" iti shrutau tachChabdena 'uchyate' iti nishichIyata ityarthaH | hishabdaH prasiddhau | atra 'tannaH' ityekadeshagrahaNena "nArAyaNAya vidmahe vAsudevAya dhImahi, tanno viShNuH prachodayAt" iti samagravAkyaM gR^ihyate | dvitIyArthe chaturthyau | tathA cha yasmAt vayaM nArAyaNaM 'vidmahe' jAnImahe yatashcha taM vAsudevaM 'dhImahi' dhyAyemahi 'tat' tasmAt 'naH' asmAn 'tat' shubhaM prati 'viShNuH 
prachodayAt' prerayatviti shrutyarthaH |
(87) yadyuttaravAkye viShNushabdashravaNAdviShNurevAtroktaM brahma, tarhi 'tanno rudraH' ityAdItara- shabdashravaNAt rudrAderapi mukhyabrahmatA prAptetyata Aha - 'na cha' iti | chashabdaH samuchchaye | tathA cha 'itarashabdAt' rudrAdivAchaka- shabdabalAttasya rudrAderapi tasya mukhyabrahmatvasya 'prAptirna' ityarthaH |
(88) kuta ityatastatprApakashabdAnAM viShNAveva mukhyatvAditi hetUpaskArabhipretya tasyAsiddhiparihArAya viShNormukhyataH sarvanAmavAchyatve shrutimAha - 'nAmAni' iti | 'shruteH' iti kvachitpaJNchamyantapAThaH | prathamAntapAThe yatosta iti sheShaH | asya 'na cha' ityanenAnvayaH | 'yat' yasmAt 'anR^itasya' R^itabhinnasya viShNvitarasya lokasya jagataH 'sarvaM' nAmapravR^ittinimittaM 'AvirAsIt' abhUt tasmAdutpattimatpravR^ittinimittavattvAt 'vishvA' vishvAni sarvANi 'nAmAni' 'loke' rudrAdijagati 'abhi' mukhyataH vAchakatayA 'na santi' ityarthaH |
(89) tarhi kasmin tAni mukhyAnItyata Aha 'nAmAni' iti | vaishabdosvadhAraNe | paramamiti hetugarbhavisheShaNam | tathA cha 'sarvANi nAmAni' 'yaM' 'A' mukhyato vAchakatvena 'vishanti' 'taM paramaM' deshakAlAbhyAmaparichChinnapravR^ittinimittaM 'viShNuM vai' vadanti vidvAMsa ityarthaH | tattvapradIpe tu - 'vishvA' vishvAni 'nAmAni loke' abhito 'na santi' mukhyato na santi mukhyato na lokavAchakAni 'yat' yasmAt, yataH puruShAt 'anR^itasya' viShNvanyasya jagato janmalayAdikaM sarvaM 'AvirAsIt', yaM cha vAchakatvena 'nAmAni A' samantAt 'vishanti', 'taM' ha 'viShNuM' uttamaM vadantItyartha uktaH | etatpakShe yachChabdasyAvR^ittiH | dvitIyAdipAdatrayasya hetu- samarpakatvam | pakShadvayespi viShNushabdo bhinnakramaH |
(90) nanu yathA viShNoH shrutyantarasiddhasarvanAmatvenAtroktaM brahmatvaM siddhyati tathA rudrAdInAmapi viShNvAdishabdavAchyatvena atroktaM brahmatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha - 'yaH' iti | 'ityevashabdAt' iti itivAkyasyaivashabdAt 'anyeShAM' rudrAdInAM 'sarvanAmatA' viShNvAdisarvashabdavAchyatvaM netyarthaH | sarvanAmatetyanantaraM - yata evamataH 'tanno viShNuH' (mahAnA.3-16) ityAdau nAnyeShAM prAptiH ata eva na brahmatvaM teShAmiti vAkyasheShaH | 'yo' bhagavAn 'eka eva devAnAM' brahmAdInAM 'nAmadhAH' - vishvapAshabdavadayaM shabdaH - nAmadhArakaH na tvanyespi 'taM prashnaM' praShTAraM 'anyA' anyAni 'bhuvanA' bhuvanAni lokAH 'saMyanti' saMyAnti mokShe pralaye cheti shrutyarthaH |
(91) nanvatrApi yachChabdena viShNuriti kutaH? vishvakarmeti shrutibalAdasya sUktAkhyaprakaraNasya vishvakarmAdyanyaparatayA tadgatayachChabdasyApi tatparatvauchityAdityata Aha - 'ajasya' iti | 'hi' yasmAt iti vAkye 'viShNoH liN^gaM' padmanAbhatvAkhyamasAdhAraNo dharmaH shrutaH tasmAdyachChabdodito viShNurevetyanvayaH | 
utsargato liN^gAt shruteH prAbalyespi sAvakAshAyA vishvakarmashruteH niravakAshaliN^gena bAdhopapatteriti bhAvaH | shrutyarthastu - 'ajasya' ajanyasya puruShasya 'nAbhau ekaM' vastu 'arpitaM' udbhUtam | 'yasmin vishvAni bhuvanAni' sarve chaturdashalokAH 'adhitasthuH' adhiShThitAH iti |
(92) nAbhyarpitaM padmAdanyatkiM na syAdityata Aha - 'na cha' iti | chaH samuchchaye | prasiddhaM viShNunAbhisthatvena prasiddhaM padmAkhyArthaM 'vinAsnyosrtho' na yujyate, prasiddhibAdhAdityarthaH | vishvakarmashruti- vatpadmanAbhatvaliN^gamapyanyasya kiM na syAdityato vAssha - 'na cha' iti | padmanAbhatvena prasiddhapadArthaM bhagavantaM vinA 'anyaH' padmanAbho na yujyate prasiddhibAdhAdityarthaH |
(93) na kevalaM prasiddhibalAdevaitachChrutyuktaM padmaM padmanAbhashcha harirityavasIyate, kintu 'ajasya' iti shrutestadubhayabodhakatvena smR^ityanugR^ihItatvAchchetyAha - 'ajasya' iti | iti shruterityanvayaH | tathA cha 'ajasya nAbhAviti shruteH' sakAshAt 'lokasAraM' lokAdhArabhUtaM 'puShkaraM' padmaM 'abhUt' iti j~nAyate |
(94) 'tasmai vyastasamastavishvavibhUtaye' vishvasya jagato vibhUtayaH sR^iShTyAdyaShTakaM jIvAdau vyastAH vistR^itAH jaDAdau samastAH saMkShiptAH vishvavibhUtayo yenAsau vyastasamastavishvavibhUtistasmai 'lokakartre' lokasvAmine 'viShNave namaH' ityarthaH | tattvapradIpe tu - samastavishvavibhUtayo yena vyastA sa vyastasamastavishvavibhUtiH | atha vA vyastAH samastA vishvavibhUtayo yeneti dvedhA vyAkhyAtam | tatra divitIyaM TIkAyAM vivR^itam | pUrvArdhe viShNuvAchaka- shabdAbhAvAduttarArdhodAharaNam | 'iti cha skAnde' iti chashabdo bhinnakrameNa 'uktaM' ityadhyAhR^itapadena sambadhyate | yata evamataH 'ajasya' ityuktaM padmameva, padmanAbhashcha harireveti vAkyasheShaH | na kevalaM prasiddhibAdhAditi chArthaH |
(95) yadA niravakAshaliN^gamAtraM shrutibAdhakaM tadA kimu vAchyaM samAkhyAyuktaM taditi bhAvenAha - 'para' iti| idaM chAvartate, 'viShNureva' ityAdikamatrApi sambadhyate | tathA cha yataH vishvakarmasUkte "paro divA para enA pR^ithivyA paro devebhirasurairyadasti" iti yA AkhyA uktiH tasyAH samA samAnA 'paro divA' ityevaMrUpa 'shrutau' AmbhR^iNIsUkte asti atospi 'viShNureva' vishvakarmasUktodita ityarthaH |
(96) nanu samAkhyAshrutAvapi viShNuH kuto vAchya ityata Aha - 'yaM' iti | itItyanantaraM vAkyenetyubhayatra sheShaH | 'paro divA' ityetatsamastamanenApi yojyam | atra samAkhyAshrutAvityekaM padam| tathA cha yasmAt 'paro divA' iti samAkhyAshrutau metyAkhyA mAkhyA tayA sahitA samAkhyA "prakR^itirvAva samAsamA" (mAdhyandinashrutiH) iti shrutau samAsamatvokteH 'nAmaikadeshe' iti nyAyena samAbhidhAvA, ahamiti prakR^itA lakShmIH "yaM" ityAdivAkyena brahmAdInAM svAdhInatvamuktvA "mama yonirapsvantaH samudre" 
iti vAkyena "paro divA" ityuktaM viShNuM svakAraNatvena samudrasthatvena chAha, tasmAdviShNureva samAkhyAshrutipratipAdya ityarthaH|  uktvetyanena lakShmIkAraNaM brahmAdyanyatamaM kiM na syAditi shaN^kA vAritA | shrutau 'divA' ityAdi tR^itIyA paJNchamyarthe | tathA cha - 'divaH' 'shriyaH' 'paraH' 'enA' etasyAH bhUmyAshcha 'paraH' uttamaH | 'devebhiH' 'devebhyaH' 'asuraiH' asurebhyashcha 'paraH' uttamaH | kiM bahunA - 'yadasti' tasmAtsarvasmAdapi paraH | sa viShNuH dyAvApR^ithivIbhyAM paraH | ahaM tu 'mahinA' mahimnA 'etAvatI' parimitA babhUva | ahametAvatI yathoktaprakArA mahimnA nAtosdhiketi vA shrutyarthaH | ahamiti labdhapadena lakShmIruchyate, etatsUktapravartikAyAH AmbhR^iNyAH lakShmIrUpatvAt | tathA cha - ahaM 'yaM yaM' rudrapadayogyaM jIvaM 'ugraM' rudraM kartuM 'kAmaye' ichCheyaM 'taM taM' ugraM kR^iNomi karomi | evaM tattatpadayogyaM yaM yaM 'brahmANaM' 'R^iShiM' 'sumedhAM' sumedhasaM vA kartuM kAmaye taM taM tathA karomItyarthaH | shiShTavAkyArthaH "patyurasAmaJNjasyAt" (bra.sU. 2-2-37) ityadhikaraNe vakShyate |
(97) tathAspi mama na svatantryamityaha - 'mama' iti | 'mama' 'yoniH' kAraNaM 'samudre apsu' apAm 'antaH' tiShThati | tasyAdhikyaM kampasvarArthaH | patinAma na grAhyamiti bhAvena nArAyaNa ityanuktvA tadartha- bodhanAyaivamuktiH |
(98) nanvatra samudrastho rudraH kiM na syAt 'tapyamAnAya salile' iti bhAratokteH na cha ramAdhInatoktivirodhaH, ugrashabdena kasyachitkrUrasya grahaNasambhavAdityata Aha - 'ugra' iti | bhavedityubhayatra sheShaH | tathA cha atrogra ityukto rudra eva bhavet, tathA samudresntassthito nArAyaNa eva bhavet, iti pratij~nAvAkyadvayArthaH | tatra hetumAha - 'prasiddhatvAt' iti | 'asyArthasya' rudre ugrashabdavAchyatvarUpArthasya prasiddhatvAt, "ugraH kapardI" ityAdikoshaprasiddhatvAt, ugrashabdena rudrashabdArthasya krauryasya j~nApitatvAchchetyarthaH | rudro raudra ugra ityeteShAmekA- rthatvAditi bhAvaH | evaM samudrashAyitvarUpArthasya "mahodadhishayosntakaH" ityAdiviShNusahasranAmaprasiddhatvAt samudres- ntaHsthatvakathanena "Apo nArAH" iti smR^itisiddhanArashabdoditodakAshrayatvarUpanArAyaNashabdArthasya 'sUchitatvAchcha' ityarthaH |
(99) nanu prasiddhyAdisadbhAvespi tatparityAgenAnyasvIkAre kiM bAdhakamityata Aha - 'na cha' 
iti| arthasyetyetadvipariNAmenAtra sambadhyate | tathA cha cho yatosyamarthaH 'prasiddhaH' ato 'avirodhe' pramANavirodhAbhAve 'na parityajyate' na tyajyata ityarthaH, prasiddhArthasya virodhaikApodyatvAt, anyathA prasiddhibAdhAditi bhAvaH | "AkAshA- deva samutpadyante" (ChAM. u. 1-9-1.) "janitota viShNoH" (R^i.saM. 9-97-5.) "nakirindratvaduttaraH" (R^i. 4-30-1.) ityAdau vyabhichAravAraNAyAvirodha iti | nanu virodhAbhAvossiddhaH, yatostra yadi rudro lakShmya- dhInatayograpadenochyate tarhi "vishvAdhiko rudraH" ityAdishrutivirodhaH syAt atostra tatparityAgo yukta ityata Aha - 'ukta' iti | karaNavyutpattyA nyAyaH pramANam | tathA cha - yato "nAmAni vishvA" (bhAllaveyashrutiH) ityAdyu- ktAgamena, taduktotpattimatpravR^ittinimittavattvAdyanumAnena, chashabdasamuchchitaiH "vede rAmAyaNe chaiva" iti vakShyamANa- pramANaishcha sAdhakaiH 'shrutayo' "vishvAdhiko rudraH" (mahAnA. 10-3.) ityAdyAgamAH radrAdipadAnAM viShNuvAchitva- mAshritya vA, vishvo vAyuH adhiko yasmAdvishvAdhika ityarthAshrayaNena vA 'etameva' viShNumeva 'vadanti' tAtparyataH prAdhAnyena bodhayanti ityavagamyate | ato na "vishvAdhikaH" ityAdishrutivirodha iti yojanA |
(100) shrutInAM viShNvekavAchitve smR^itiM chAha - 'vede' iti | viShNureva 'vede rAmAyaNe cha purANe tathA bhArate' |
(101) kiM bahunA 'sarvatra' sarvagrantheShu 'gIyate' pratipAdyate | teShvapi na bhAge, kintvAdau madhye ante cha, karmAdikANDatrayespi, upakramopasaMhArayoravAntaraprakaraNeShu cha, sarvatra prativAkyaM pratipadaM pratyakSharaM cha mukhyataH pratipAdyata ityarthaH |
(102) 'veda' iti vachanasya khilAkhilapArijAtAkhyaharivaMshabhAgatrayagatatvasUchanAya 'harivaMsheShu' iti bahuvachanam | harivaMsheShvityanantaraM 'yaduktaM' iti sheShaH, tasyAto na virodha iti, harivaMsheShUktanyAyena uktarItyA iti vAsnvayaH | nanu pramANavirodhAbhAvossiddhaH, yataH shrutivirodhAbhAvespyasti pAshupatAdishAstravirodhaH, tatra rudrAdInAM sarvottamatvasya sarvakAraNatvasya chokteH ityata Aha - 'na cha' iti| chospyarthaH na kevalaM shrutivirodhAbhAvaH, apitarhItaravirodhospi neti | 'asyArthasya' iti vartate |
(103) kuta ityata teShAM mohArthaM kR^itatvAditi hetvadhyAhAramabhipretya tasyAsiddhiM pramANodAharaNena nirAha - 'eSha' iti | rudraM prati viShNuvAkyametat | muhyatesnena jana iti 'moho' naTanaM vaà¤¼JNchanaM vA | 'moho' mohakAraNamanAdikarmavAsanArupamiti tattvapradIptokterapyayamevArthaH, mohakashAstramiti vyAsatIrthIyokteH | na cha asya 'na mohashAstrasya vaktA viShNurAshaN^kyaH, "ajasyAvakrachetasaH" (ka.u. 5-1.) iti hi shrutiH' iti tattvapradIpavirodhaH shaN^kyaH asatAmityabhiprAyAt | 
vidyamAnAkArAchChAdanenAvidyamAnAkArapradarshanaM naTanam | avidyamAnakathanaM vaJNchanam | sR^ijAmItyuttamapuruShaprayogAdahamiti kartA labhyate | chashabdaH kriyAkartR^isamuchchaye | 'pUrvashrutasyaitachChabdasya pashchAt shruto yachChabdo visheShaNam' iti  nyAyadIpokteH ya eSha iti yojanA | tathA cha ahaM 'mohaM sR^ijAmi' karomi | 'ya eSha' mohaH 'janAn mohayiShyati' aj~nAnamithyAj~nAnAdikaM prApayiShyati |
(104) parabAdhakatvAt bAhuH prANyaN^gaM, mahAn bAhuryasya saH, tasya sambuddhiH he 'mahAbAho' shatrubAdhakAN^gayukta 'rudra' 'tvaM cha' mohaM sR^ija 'mohashAstrANi' cha 'kAraya' kuru, dadhIchyAdibhishcha kAraya| he 'mahAbhuja' mahAbhakShaka mahAkuTileti vA he rudra |
(105) teShviti sheShaH tathA cha - 'teShu' mohashAstreShu 'atathyAni' kvApyavidyamAnAni liN^gamUlAnveShaNAdIni 'vitathyAni' vyadhikaraNatvena vidyamAnAni viShNuniShThAni vAyuniShThAni vA rudrAdiniShThatayochyamAnAni sarvottamatva- sarvasvAtantryaviShabhakShaNAdIni 'darshayasva' pratipAdayeti yAvat | 
(106) 'mAm AtmAnam' ityuddeshyadvitIyAntam | parasparasamuchchaye chashabdau | tathA cha lokeShu 'AtmAnaM' svAtmAnamuddishya 'prakAshaM' prasiddhiM 'kuru' | na kevalametAvat, kintu 'mAm' uddishya 'aprakAsham' aprasiddhiM cha kurvItyarthaH | kechittu - prakAshossyAstIti prakAshamiti arshaAdyajantatvamAshritya uddeshyadvitIyAnAshrayaNena prakAshaM prasiddhamiti vyAchakShate |
(107) 'vArAhavachanAt' ityasyetareShAM mohArthaM kR^itatvAvagamAditi  hetumukhena 'na chetara' iti pratij~nAvAkyenAnvayaH | liN^gamUlAnveShaNakathA tu - pUrvaM jagatkartR^itvaviShaye viShNuviriJNchayorvivAdosbhUt ahameva jagataH kartA na mattosnyaH iti | etasminnantare tayorgarvavinAshAya tanmadhye kiJNchana liN^gamudabhUt | tau tat dR^iShTvA sarvadevasannidhau parasparaM samayaM chakratuH | tatra brahmA viShNumAha - avayormadhyessya liN^gasya yosntamAdiM cha gachChati sa bhavedadhiko loke, lokakartA cha sa prabhuH | tasmAddhe viShNo tvaM liN^gasya mUlagaveShaNAyAdhastAdvraja, ahamantagaveShaNAya UrdhvaM gamiShyAmi iti | evaM tau samayaM kR^itvA mArgamANau nirgatau | tatra viShNurvarAha- rUpeNAdhastAdgaveShituM yayau | vANIjAnistu haMsarUpeNordhvaM yayo | atha punarviShNuH svasthAnaM samAgatya sarvadevasannidhau ahaM liN^gasyAdimadrAkShamiti satyam Aha | brahmAspi samAgatya ahamantamadrAkShamiti ChadmanA mR^iShA Aha | atha liN^garUpI maheshvaraH tayorvachaH shrutvA he viShNo yatastvaM satyamevAvochaH ataH tava loke matsamA pUjA bhaviShyati | brahmaNastu netyuvAcha | tato brahmA he rudra mamAnR^itoktikR^itAparAdhastvayA kShantavya ityAha | tato rudro na mama vacho mithyA bhaviShyati | tathAspi 
tvaM mithyoktikR^itadoShaparihArArthaM gandhamAdanagiriM vraja | tatra kratUn kuruShva| tatastava shrautasmArtakarmasveva pUjA bhaviShyati | na tu devAlayAdiShvityuktvAsntaradhIyatetyAdirUpA skAndapurANasthA| nanu tathAspyasyArthasya skAndabrahmavaivartAdipurANavirodhassyAt, teShAM shivabrahmAdipAramyaviShayatvAdityata Aha - 'shaive cha' iti | chashabdospyarthassamuchchaye, yadyapItyAdyarthe cha - 'shaive' shivotkarShaparespIti 'skAnde' vachanAditya- nuShaN^gadyotakashcha | evamuttaratrApi |
(108) - (109) he 'achyuta' 'yadaiva' yadi cha tvameva sarvathA 'parAN^mukho' bhavasi anugrahaM cha karoShi 'tadA' tarhi 'brahmeshAnAdayaH surAH' shvapachAdapi shvAnaM pachatIti shvapacho nIchaH tasmAdapi 'kaShTatvaM' kleshayuktatvaM kaShTaM vA 'yAntyeva' ityarthaH | asya tarkatvAttasya viparyayaparyavasAne brahmAdInAM viShNvadhInatvam atyantatadanugrahapAtratvaM cha siddhyatIti na pramANavirodhaH | itishabdasya 'iti skAnde' ityanvayaH |
(110) - (112) 'brAhme' brahmaviShaye | atra 'aham' iti chaturmukha uchyate | 'yadvat' iti shravaNAt 'tadvat' iti labhyate | chashabdau samuchchayArthau | 'asmAbhiH' ityatra shivashchAnye cha ahaM cha vayaM tairityekasheShaH | tathA cha yadyapi vayaM 'tachChaktyekAMshabhAginaH' tasyAchyutasya yA shaktiH sAmarthyaM tasyaikAMshabhAgino na bhavAmaH tathAspi 'yadvat' yathA 'bAlaH krIDanakaiH' krIDAsAdhanapadArthaiH 'krIDate' 'tadvat' tathA 'achyuto' harirapi 'asmAbhiH' karaNaiH 'krIDate' sR^iShTyAdikrIDAM karotItyarthaH | punarna chetyuktiH tAtparyArthA, 'nA' puruSha iti vA | itishabdasya iti brahmavaivarte ityanvayaH | 'skAnde' 'brahmavaivarte' ityanayoH 'vachanAt' itipadadvArA 'na chetaragranthavirodhaH' ityanenAnvayaH | tathA cha teShAM shaivAditvespi na virodhitvam, tatrAspi viShNUttamatvAderapyuktyA svavirodhena shivAdyutkarShesprAmANyAt | na cha viparItaM kiM na syAditi vAchyam, shivAdyutkarShAdeH shaivAdipurANeShvevAsAdhAraNyena prAptatvAt, tatraiva viShNUtkarShoktau tatra prAmANyasya shivAdyutkarShAdAvaprAmANyasya cha nishchayena vaiparItyAyogAt | tasmAtpAshupatAdiparikalpitashivAdyuttamatva- paripATI darshanabhAShayA teShUpanyasyata iti na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH |
(113) tathApi viShNUttamatvarUdrAdhamatvayorvaiShNavagranthavirodhosstItyata Aha - 'na cha' iti | samuchchaye chashabdaH | tathA cha - 'vaiShNaveShu' viShNuviShayapurANAdiShvapi 'tathA' viShNoranyasyottamatvamuktaM na, ata eva 'tathA' shaivavat sarvottamatvAdhamatvaviShaye virodho netyarthaH, yena svavirodhena svaviShayesprAmANyaM syAditi bhAvaH | tarhi vaiShNaveShu rAmakR^iShNAdiviShNukartR^ikashivastutyAdi kathamuchyata ityata Aha - 'tachcha' iti | chastavarthaH | vachanAdityanuvtate | tadityasyAvR^ittiH | tathA cha - cho yato vaiShNaveShu yachChivastutyAdyuchyate tattu 'eSha moham' iti vachanAjj~nAtena tena mohArthatvena 'uktaM' pratyuktaM samAhitaM 
ityuktamityarthaH | asya 'ato na tadvirodhaH' ityadhyAhR^itenAnvayaH |
|| iti jij~nAsAdhikaraNam ||
|| 2. janmAdhikaraNam ||
(1) etadadhikaraNapratipAdyaM darshayati - 'brahmaNaH' iti | nirbAdharUDhibalAt jIva evedaM brahma, tasya chAsandhigdhatvAnna jij~nAsyatvamiti prAptetannirAkartuM brahmashabdena jIvagrahaNe bAdhakarUpaM shrutyuktaM jij~nAsyabrahmaNo lakShaNamAha sUtrakAra ityarthaH | "shrutyuktaM lakShaNamAha" iti TIkayA "sA viShNorbrahmatvavidhAtrI taittirIyashrutiryAni tasya lakShaNAnyAha tAnyanena sUtreNa bhagavAnAha" iti tattvapradIpokteH tachChabdAdhyAhAreNa bhAShyArtha uktaH | ata eva lakShaNamiti samudAyaikavachanamiti j~nAtavyam| anena pUrvatra vivakShitabrahmajij~nAsAkShepeNeha pUrvapakShotthAnAt pUrvAdhikaraNenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | brahmaviShayatvAchChAstrasaN^gatiH siddhaiva | yadyapi 'brahmashabdashcha viShNAveva' ityanena brahmashabdo viShNAveva mukhya ityuktam | tathApi bhAShyakArairuktatvespi sUtrakR^itAnuktatvAt brahma kiM jIva uta viShNuriti bhavatyeva sandehaH | sUtraM paThati - 'janma' iti | yata ityuktestadbrahmeti prakR^itaM bhavatIti sheShaH| yadvA - "janmAdyasya yata iti sUtre shrutamiti vAkyasheShaH" | iti sudhokteH shrutamiti vAkyasheShaH | janma Adiryasya sR^iShTyAdisamudAyasya tajjanmAdIti tadguNasaMvij~nAnabahuvrIhiH, tasya samAsArthaikadeshasya janmano guNatvena visheShaNatvena saMvij~nAnAt | tathA cha - 'asya' pramitasya jagato 'janmAdi yato' bhavati shrutamiti vA tadbrahmeti sUtrArtha ityabhipretya asya jagato janma Adipadokte sthitisaMhR^itI yatastadbrahmetyAdyanyathApratItivAraNAya sUtraM yathAvadvyAchaShTe - 'sR^iShTi' iti | atra prayojakavyApAravAchisR^iShTisaMhAraniyamanashabdairlakShaNayA prapaJNchaniShThajanmanAsha- niyamyatvarUpaprayojyavyApArAH pratipAdyante | lakShaNAprayojanaM brahmaNa upAdAnatvAbhAvapradarshanamiti chandrikoktiH | sR^iShTyAdInAmaShTAnAM cha pratyekaM lakShaNatvaM, na tu samuditaveSheNa, ativyAptyAdyabhAvAt | etachcha lakShaNamananta- guNapUrNatvasyApyupalakShakam | ekenopalakShaNasambhavespi mumukShuj~neyatvAtsArthakamaShTAnAM vachanam | yathoktaM shrImanmahA- bhAratatAtparyanirNaye -
sR^iShTirakShAhR^itij~nAnaniyatyaj~nAnabandhanAn |
mokShaM cha viShNutashchaiva j~nAtvA muktirna chAnyathA ||
iti | yata ityanantaraM 'shrutAH' 'bhavanti' iti vA sheShaH | asya tadbrahmetyupaskR^itenAnvayaH ||
(2) nanu jagajjanmAdikartR^itvaM yadi viShNvekaniShThaM bhavettadA brahmashabdena jIvagrahaNe bAdhakarUpaM syAt; 
tasya viShNvekaniShThatvameva kuto j~nAyata ityata Aha - 'utpatti' iti | asya jagato 'yasmAt' puruShAt 'utpattisthitisaMhArAH' bhavanti 'niyatiH' niyamanam 'AvR^itiH j~nAnaM' cha yasmAdbhavati 'bandhamokShau cha' yasmAdbhavataH 'saH ekarAT' svatantro 'hariH' eva ityarthaH | viriJNchAdiShu ativyAptiparihArArtham 'ekarAT' iti| 'iti skAnde' ityanantaraM 'vachanAt sR^iShTyAdikartA harireva' iti vAkyasheShaH |
(3) jij~nAsyaM brahma viShNureva bhavet janmAdikartR^itvAt ityanumAne hetvasiddhiM jij~nAsyabrahmalakShaNasya tatrAnupalambhakR^itAsambhavaM vA nirAkartuM jagatkAraNatvalakShaNaM jij~nAsye brahmaNi "tadvijij~nAsasva" ityataH pUrvavAkye kathitamityAha - 'yataH' iti | vaishabdaH prasiddhau | bhUtashabdaH "astitvAdbhUtanAmabhyaH sarvajIvebhya eva yat" iti gItAtAtparyanirNayavachanAjjIvavAchI tadupalakShitasarvajagatparaH | tathA cha -  'imAni bhUtAni yato jAyante yena jAtAni' utpannAni 'jIvanti' prANaM dadhati 'yat' cha pralaye 'prayanti' pravishanti yachcha 'abhi' svechChayA samyak 'vishanti' muktau 'tat' tadeva 'brahma' nAnyat | mukhyataH tajj~nAnAya vedArthabhUtaM 'tadvijij~nAsasva' tadviShayakavichAraM kurvityarthaH | itishabdaH shrutistha eva | tasya 'iti varuNo bhR^igumuvAcha' iti kriyApadenAnvayaH |
(4) lakShaNasyAtivyAptishaN^kAM uktAnumAnasya vyabhichArashaN^kAM vA parihartuM spaShTArthatvAtprathamaM smR^itimupanyasya idAnIM sR^iShTyAdikartR^itvaM pratyekamapi viShNvekaniShThaM kimu sarvamiti bhAvena sthitikartR^itvasya viShNvekaniShThatve shrutimAha - 'yaH' iti | ushabda evArthaH, tridhAtvityekaM padaM, utashabdassamuchchaye | tathA cha - 'yo' viShNuH 'ekaH' eva 'tridhAtu' prakR^itipuruShakAladhArakaH 'pR^ithivIM' bhUmiM 'dyAM' shriyaM cha 'vishvA' vishvAni sarvANi cha 'bhuvanAni' 'dAdhAra' dadhAretyarthaH | niyamanasyApi viShNvekakartR^itve shrutimAha - 'chaturbhiH' iti | sa iti sheShaH, nashabda ivArthaH, chashabdo mAtrArthaH | tathA cha - sa bR^ihachCharIro mUlarUpI viShNuH 'nAmabhishcha' nAmamAtraiH svarUpabhedashUnyaiH 'chaturbhiH' vAsudevasaN^karShaNapradyumnAniruddhaiH 'sAkaM navatiM' navatisaN^khyAkAn 'vyatIn' - deveShu yaugikosyaM shabdaH - visheSheNA- dhikAn devAn kimutAnyAn 'vR^ittaM chakraM na' vartulaM rathAN^gamiva yugapat 'avIvipat', viparivartana iti dhAtuH, paryavartayadityarthaH | aShTau vasavaH ekAdasha rudrAH viShNuvyatiriktaikAdashAdityAH hiraNyagarbheNa saha dasha prajeshvarAH pradhAnena paJNchAshanmaruta iti navatiH | tattvapradIpe tu - prathamaM TIkoktArthamabhidhAya -
AdityA vasavo rudrA marutashchAshvinAvapi |
bR^ihaspatishach kAmashcha manurdakSho vinAyakaH |
bhR^igushchaivAniruddhashcha dharmo nirR^itireva cha |
kuberasahitA devAH navatissamprakIrtitAH |
ananto garuDo vAyuH chatvAro brahmaNA saha ||
iti pramANAnusAreNa prakArAntareNa chaturuttaranavatiruktA | tatraiva nAmavadbhiH kIrtimadbhiriti cha vyAkhyAtam |
(5) eteShAM lakShaNAnAmativyAptiM viShNvekaniShThatvoktyA smR^ityA chArthAt parihR^itAmapi sAkShAdanyatra lakShaNAbhAvaM pratipAdayantyA shrutyA nirAha - 'paraH' iti | viShNAvityAkR^iShyate | tattvodyotaTIkoktarItyA muktA amuktAshcheti sheShaH | ata eva TIkAyAM ka ityuktam | tathA cha - 'tanvA' svamUrtyaiva na tu kIrtimAtreNa 'vR^idhAna' aparichChinna he viShNo tvaM yato 'mAtrayA' miteH 'paraH' vilakShaNossi aparimitossIti yAvat | ata evaMbhUtasya 'te mahitvaM' jagatsR^iShTyAdirUpaM mahimAnam 'anu' api kespi muktA amuktAshcha 'nAshnuvanti' na prApnuvantItyarthaH | yadvA - 'nAshnuvanti' nAnubhavantItyarthaH | nAshnuvantIti vartamAnaniShedhAt syAduttaratretyata Aha - 'na' iti | prApnotIti sheShaH | tathA cha - he 'viShNo' 'devamahimnaH' ramAdimahimnaH 'param antaM' sImAnaM mahimatAratamyaparAvadhibhUtaM 'te mahitvaM' mahimAnaM 'jAyamAno' na prApnoti, jAto 'nApa' ityarthaH | upalakShaNaM chaitat janiShyamANo na prApsyatItyapi draShTavyam | ata eva tattvapradIpe - "paro mAtrayA tanvA vR^idhAna | na te mahitvamanvashnuvanti | ubhe te vidma rajasI pR^ithivyA viShNo devatvaM paramasya vitse | na te viShNo jAyamAno na jAto devamahimnaH paramantamApa | udastabhnA nAkamR^iShvaM bR^ihantaM dAdhartha prAchIM kakubhaM pR^ithivyAH" iti R^igdvayamevameva vyAkhyAtam | tathA hi - mAtrAyAH paraH parimANAtItaH tanvA vR^idhAnaH tanvA vardhamAnaH dehena pUrNaH - itthaM bhAve tR^itIyA - deharUpeNa pUrNa ityarthaH | yatashchidAnandAdyAtmako viShNorabhinnashcha dehaH | te mahitvaM mahimAnaM nAnubhavanti na prApnuvanti cha | te tvadIyAyAH pR^ithivyAH prakR^iteH rajasI rajoguNakArye ubhe puNyapApe vayaM vidmaH | prakR^iteH rajasA hi puNyapApe sR^ijyate | paramasya te mahimAnaM tvameva vitse | tvameva mahimnaH mahimasamudAyasyAntaM brahmaNaH shriyo vA mahimAnamatishayito hi viShNu- mahimA anyamahimnAM param antaM te mahimAnaM na kaJNchidApa | yatrAkaM nAsti tannAkam | R^iShvaM prakAsharUpam | bR^ihantaM pUrNaM lokam udastabhnAH udastabhnaH uchchairastambhayaH | pR^ithivyAH prathivyAtmakasya brahmANDasya prAchIM kakubhaM dishaM indrasthApanena dAdhartha dhR^itavAnasi | sarvadhAraNopalakShaNametaditi |
(6) jagatkAraNatvaM cha brahmaNo na vikAritvena, kintu pitR^ivannimittattvenaiveti shrutyA darshayati, - 
'yaH' iti | 'yaH' eka eva 'naH' asmadAdisarveShAM 'janitA' janayitaiva 'pitA' na dattaputrapitR^ivat pAlakapitR^imAtram | yadvA - "sa eva pitR^isaMsthastupAtR^itvAtpitR^inAmakaH" ityaitareyabhAShyadishA "pitA pAtA" iti tattvapradIpokteH 'janitA' janakaH 'pitA' pAtA chetyarthaH | 'yo vidhAtA' visheSheNa dhArakaH poShakaH, "muktAnAM poShaNaM cha j~nAnamokShadAnena" iti tattvapradIpokteH | "vidhAtA kartA" iti prameyadIpoktiH | tasyA dhAraNapoShaNayoriti bhAvaH | yo 'vishvA' vishvAni sarvANi bhuvanAni tadgata 'dhAmAni' gR^ihANi jIvAdisvarUpANi cha 'veda' jAnAtItyarthaH | 'ityAdi' iti vAkyam 'uktArthe pramANam' iti sheShaH | Adishabdena etajjAtIyakashrutyantaraM "dyAvAbhUmI janayan" iti cha gR^ihyate || 2 ||
|| iti janmAdhikaraNam ||
|| 3. shAstrayonitvAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe pUrvoktajagajjanmAdikAraNatvarUpabrahmalakShaNasya rudrAdiShvativyAptiparihArAya jagatkAraNe pramANamuchyate | siddhAntapratij~nAmupaskR^itya darshayati - 'anumAnataH' iti | kAraNatveneti sheShaH| tathA cha - shivo jagajjanmAdikartA sarvaj~natvAt vyatirekeNa yaj~nadattavat ityAdyanumAnAt viShNoH 'anye' rudrAdayospi jagatkAraNatvena 'na kalpanIyAH' na shaN^kyA ityarthaH| kuta ityatastatra hetvA- kAN^kShAyAM sUtramupanyasyati - 'shAstrayonitvAt' iti| jagatkAraNasyeti sheShaH | "tannirdhAritayuktirvA" ityanuvyAkhyApade "tannirdhAritetyataH paraM vyAptishabdosdhyAhAryaH" iti sudhokteryathA tatra madhyesdhyAhAraH, yathA vA "sarvendriyavivarjitatvAdyartha uktaH" iti gItAbhAShyaprameyadIpe AdItyataH paraM shabdashabdosdhyAhArya ityuktestatra yathA madhyesdhyAhAraH, yathA vA "puruShAdvadhavikArasamUhatenakR^iteShu" iti mahAbhAShyavAkye samAsamadhye teneti padAdhyAhAraH, tathAstrApi shAstrashabdAtparamekashabdosdhyAhAryaH yoni- shabdAtprAk j~naptishabdashcha | tathA cha R^igAdirUpaM shAstraM cha tadekamasahAyaM cha j~naptiyonirj~naptikAraNaM yasya vastunaH tattathoktaM tasya bhAvastattvaM tasmAditisUtrArthaH | anena na jagatkAraNamAnumAnikaM tasya shAstraikasamadhigamyatvAt dharmAdivat ityanumAnamuktaM bhavati | na cha dR^iShTAnte sAdhyavaikalyam | na hi dharmAdinishchayosnumAnena bhavati | tathA cha - anumAnAdanyeShAM jagatkAraNatAsAdhanamayuktamiti na teShu lakShaNasyAtivyAptiriti bhAvaH |
(2) kAraNasya shAstraikavedyatvaM kuta ityata Aha - 'na' iti | taittirIyavAkyamidam | atra hrasvokArapAThaH| 'aupaniShadaH' iti shrutyantaram | atrAN^aH prashleShaH kAryaH | Adishabdena "sarve vedA 
yatpadaM" (kaTha. u. 2-15) "vedAhyevainaM" (bhAllaveyaM) "taM tvaupaniShadaM puruShaM pR^ichChAmi" (bR^i. u. 5-9-26) iti vAkyaM cha gR^ihyate | 'taM' pUrvaprakR^itaM 'bR^ihantaM' pUrNaM 'sarvAnubhuM' sarvamanubhavatIti sarvAnubhUH taM sarvaj~nam | yadvA - sarvamanubhAvayatIti sarvAnubhustaM AtmAnaM sarvajagatkartAraM sarvasvAminaM vA | 'sAmparAye' samyakparasyAsyaH prAptiH samparAyaH sa eva sAmparAyaH, tAdarthye saptamI, tathA cha mokShAya 'avedavit' - viShNu- tattvanirNayaTIkoktarItyA atra vedashabdena sadAgamA gR^ihyante | tathA cha sadAgamatadarthAj~nAnI vedaviruddhaj~nAnI vA 'na manute' na jAnAti, vedAdanyat jagatkartAraM na pramApayatIti yAvat | kintu vedavideva jAnAti veda eva pramApayatIti prathamashrutyarthaH | puruSho jagatkartA A aupaniShadaH upaniShadekasamadhigamya ityanyashrutyarthaH | gamyatvaM grAhyatvaM taddhitArthaH | AdishabdopAttashrutyapekShayA 'shrutibhyashcha' iti bahuvachanam| chashabdosdhyAhR^itasAdhyasamuchchaye, svoktisamuchchaye vA | asya shAstrayonitvAdityanenAnvayaH | kAraNasyeti sheShaH | tathA chaivamAdishrutibhyaH kAraNasya shAstraikayonitvAvagamAt nAsiddhiriti bhAvaH | naJN.hdvayAN^ghaTitashrutyudAharaNena sUtra ekashabdosdhyAhArya iti sUchitam |
(3) aupaniShadasyApi kAraNasyAnumAnena siddhiH kiM na syAdityata Aha - 'na cha' iti | chosvadhAraNe | tathA cha - 'anumAnasya' anumAnamAtrasya 'prAmANyam' atIndriyArthapramApakatvaM netyarthaH | tathA cha - na tenAnyasya jagatkartR^itAsAdhanaM yuktamiti bhAvaH | nanu kathametat 'sarvadharmopapatteshcha' (sU. 2-1-38) ityadhikaraNe svAtantryAdihetunA viShNoH pUrNatvAdisiddhyaN^gIkArAdityata uktam - 'niyata' iti | idaM cha svAtantryArthakaM pramANa- rUpaprakR^ityarthavisheShaNam | anumAnasyeti hetugarbham | tathA cha - anumAnatvAdeva na tasya svAtantryeNAdR^iShTArtha- nishchAyakatvaM, pratipakShAdisambhavAt, kintvasvAtantryeNa | svAtantryaM cha sahAyarAhityam | tachcha na svAtantryAdihetAvasti shrutisAhAyyarahitatvena svatantratvAnna pramANatvamiti bhAvaH | kuto nAnumAnasya niyataprAmANyamityata Aha - 'shruti' iti | smR^iterapyupalakShakametat | atra sahAyashabdo mUlavAchI | tasmAtsvArthe ShyaJN | shrutishcha tatsAhAyyaM cheti karmadhArayaH, tatastena rahitamiti tatpuruShaH | shrutyanugrAhyatvarahitamiti yAvat | chaH samuchchaye | evashabdo bhinnakramaH | tathA cha - 'kutrachit' asmAdAdyadR^iShTe shrautesrthe 'shrutisAhAyyarahitamanumAnam' Ishvaro na svatantraH chetanatvAdityAdi liN^gam, tathA yaj~nahiMsAsdharmatvAnumAnaM cha tathA 'pramANAntaram' anumAnAdanyat rAmakR^iShmAdidoShagrAhi mAnuShatvagrAhi cha pratyakShaM 'nishchayAt' sphuTamatIndriyArthaM 'na sAdhayet' iti yojanA | yadvA - arthaM nishchayAnna sAdhayenna sAdhayedevetyarthaH | uktaM hi gItAbhAShye - "sa nishchayena yoktavyaH yoktavya eva bubhUShuNetyarthaH" iti uktaM hi prameyadIpikAyAm "ayogavyavachChede nishchayashabdaH" iti |
(4) tarhi kIdR^ishasya pratyakShAderadR^iShTArthanishchAyakatvamityata Aha 'shruti' iti | bahuvrIhirayam | tathA 
cha - shrutismR^itirUpasahakAriyuktaM 'yatpramANAntaraM' yashodAdipratyakShaM tat 'uttamam' | ataH tat 'pramANapadavIm' anupramANasya pramAkaraNatvarUpAM paddhatiM 'gachChet' prApnuyAdityanvayaH | taditi pAThespyevameva yojanA | evaM shrutismR^itisahAyo yastarkaH viShNuH svatantraH pUrNatvAditi samavyAptikAnumAnaM sospi pramANapadavIM gachChedityanvayaH | 'atra' asmin viShaye 'vichAraNA' saMshayo 'na' kArya ityarthaH nAtretyanena svoktArthesprAmANyashaN^kA nirAkR^itA |
(5) tarkapadasya vyApyAropeNetyAdyanyathApratItinirAsAya tarkasvarUpamAha - 'pUrva' iti | 'atra' vipratipanne vAkye 'kosrthosbhimataH' tAtparyaviShayo 'bhavedityAdyam' evaMbhUtavimarshapUrvakaM 'pUrvottarAvirodhena' upakramopasaMhArAvirodhena tadaikarUpyeNa-liN^gAntarasyApyupalakShaNametat - tathA cha - upakramAditAtparya- liN^gaiH atra tAtparyaviShayArthosyameva bhavedityAdyaM yat 'UhanaM' yatpramAj~nAnaM tatsAdhanaM liN^gaM sa eva 'tarkaH' atrAbhimataH | 'shuShkatarkaM' shrutismR^itisahAyarahitaM tannirapekShaM chetanatvAdi tarkaM tu varjayet, tenAtIndriyArthanishchayo na kArya ityarthaH | kechittu ka - ityasyobhayArthatvamAshrisya "kashChandasAm" (R^i. 10-115-9) iti vAkyam 'atra' ityanena parAmR^ishyate | ata eva 'ityAdyam' ityapi yuktamityAhuH | 'kaurme' ityanantaraM purANe yata uktamiti sheShaH | asya 'na cha' ityanenAnvayaH |
(6) na kevalaM shrutyAdisAhityahInAnumAnasya prAmANyAbhAve sAdhaka sadbhAvaH, api tu tatprAmANyAbhyupagame bAdhakaM chAstItyAha - 'shakyatvAt' iti | prayoktumiti sheShaH | 'anumAnAm' iti karmaNi ShaShThI | chashabdo na kevalamityuktasamuchchayArthaH | tathA cha - shrutyAdisAhityahInAnAm 'anumAnAM' chetanatvavastutvAdirUpakevalahetUnAM 'sarvatra' rudrAderjagatkAraNatvAbhAvAdau shashAdeH shrR^iN^gitvAdau sAdhyospi prayoktuM 'shakyatvAt' nAnumAnasya niyataprAmANyamiti yojanA |
(7) atraiva pramANamAha - sarvatreti | 'hi' yasmAt 'AgamaM vinA' taddhInA 'anumA' 'sarvatra' IshvarakAraNatvAbhAvAdau 'kartuM' prayoktuM 'shakyate' 'tasmAt' anumA 'AgamaM vinA udIkShitum' udIkShayituM j~nApayitum arthamiti sheShaH 'shaktimatI' sAmarthyayutA netyarthaH | 'vArAhe' ityasyApi 'kaurme' itivadanvayaH | tasmAtkevalAnumAnasyAnirNAyakatvAchChAstreNaiva kartR^itvanishchaya iti sthitam |
(8) nanvatIndriyArthAbhAvena pratyakShetarasyAprAmANyAtkathaM shAstrAdIshvarasiddhiriti nAstikyavAdaM mokShadharmavachanena nirAchaShTe - reta iti | reta ityAdiprathamaikavachanAntAnAM padAnAM pratyekaM pramANamiti padenAnvayaH | 'atrArthe' iti sheShaH | tathA cha - retodhAtvAdi 'atrArthe' atIndriyArthasattve anumAnAdi- prAmANye cha pramANaM pramApakaM bhavatItyarthaH| bhAShyakArIyadvitIyetishabdasya evaM mokShadharmavachanAtpratItairhetubhirnAstikyavAdo na yujyata iti yojanA | nAstikA eva nAstikyaM, 
nAstikasamudAyo vA nAstikyam | tathA cha - nAsti paralokaH, dharmo nAsti, adharmo nAstIti dhiyA vAda ityarthaH | yadvA - nyAyadIpikoktarItyA - AstikyaM dharmAdAvastyanena prayojanamiti bhAvo buddhiH, tatpUrvako vAdaH, tadanyo nAstikyavAda ityarthaH | retodhAtvAdInAmanumApakatvaprakArastvittham - retashshabditacharamadhAtusharIrayoH kAryakAraNabhAvo na pratyakShaH, kintvanvayavyatirekAkhyAnumAnagamya iti tatprAmANyasiddhiH | mR^itasharIre siktasya retasaH sharIrAkAraNatvena yadadhiShThite sharIre siktaM retaH sharIrAtmanA pariNamati tajjIvasiddhiH| vandhyAdisarvasharIre siktasya retasaH kAryAkaratvena yatpreritaM retaH kAryakaraM tadIshvarAdR^iShTasiddhiH | tata eva tatpratipAdakAgama- prAmANyasiddhiH | evaM vAtapittAdidhAturapathyAdinA jIvachCharIre kvachideva vikriyate, na mR^itasharIre, nApi jIvatsarva- sharIreShu | tato jIveshvaratadbodhakAgamaprAmANyAdisiddhiH | vaTakaNikApadoktavaTabIjAdvaTa utpadyata iti suprasiddham, na cha bharjitAyAstasyAH, nApyabharjitAbhyassarvAbhya iti tatprerakeshvAdR^iShTasiddhiH | ghR^itena jIvachCharIra eva pInatA jAyate, na mR^itasharIre kShiptena nApi jAvatsarvasharIreShu | 'dhUmAdhivAsanaM' nAma puShpAdisampattyarthaH dhUmena vR^ikShasya saMskAraH | tenAshuShkavR^ikSheShveva puShpAdisampattiH, na shuShke, nApyashuShkeShu sarveShu | etAbhyAmapi liN^gAbhyAM jIveshvarAdR^iShTAdisiddhiH | keShAJNchitsAdhanavisheShAt 'jAtismR^itiH' pUrvajanmasmR^itirbhavati anenaiva puNyena evaM svargosnubhUtaH, anena pApenetthaM narakamanubhUtamiti | sA cha kasyachideva, na sarvasya, na chetanAdyabhAve sA yuktetyatospi chetanAdR^iShTAdisiddhiH | ayaskAntAkhyashilAvisheSheNAyo bhramati, na chAchetane cheShTakatvaM dR^iShTaM, nApi sarvachetanAnAmityetasmAdapi tatprerakeshvarAdR^iShTAdisiddhiH | sUryakAntAkhyashilAvisheSheNAgnirjAyate, na chAsau shaktirachetane yuktA | atospi prerakeshvarAdR^iShTAdisiddhiH | ambubhakShaNena jIvachCharIra eva tR^iShNA nivartate, na cha tanmR^itasharIre pAtrAntare vA nihitaM pachyate | nApi jIvatsarvasharIreShu | tasmAdapi jIveshvarAdisiddhiH | pretyetyanantaraM sthitasyeti sheShaH | 'pretya' jIvaM vihAya sthitasya dehasya 'bhUtApyayo' bhUteShu laya ityarthaH | tathA cha - maraNena dehasya pR^ithivyAdipaJNchabhUteShu layo bhavati, na jIvato, na chechChayetyatospi tanniyAmakeshvarAdisiddhiH | evaM devatAsbhyupayAchanena keShAJNchideva sampadAdikaM bhavati, evaM mR^ite dehe cheShTAnivR^ittirbhavati, na purA na svechChayA | atospi jIveshvarAdR^iShTAdisiddhiriti |
(9) yuktyantareNApi nAstikyavAdaM dUShayati - darshanAchcheti | cho yuktisamuchchaye | Adishabdena pApaM gR^ihyate| tathA cha svAdhyAyabrahmacharyAdirUpAtyutkaTatapaAdiphalasya tejassvitvAdeH pratyakShata eva darshanAchcha na nAstikyavAdo yujyata ityarthaH | puNyapApAkhyAtIndriyavastunastatsAdhakAnumAnAgamaprAmANyasya chAN^gIkAryatvAditi bhAvaH |
(10) nanu yadyanumAnasyAnishchAyakatvena shAstrAdeva kAraNatvasiddhiH, tarhi pAshupatAdishAstreNa 
rudrAderjaga- tkAraNatvasiddhiH syAdityata Aha - R^igiti | akArAntosyamatharvashabdaH | R^ikcha yajushcha sAma chAtharvashcheti tathoktAH | evashabdasya R^igAdikameveti sambandhaH | 'mUlarAmAyaNamevetyavAntararAmAyaNavyudAsaH' iti sudhoktiH | chashabdau samuchchaye |
(11) tarhi mAnavAdyashAstraM syAdityata Aha - yachcheti | chosvadhAraNe, dvitIyospyarthe | tathA cha 'etasya' R^igAdeH 'yat' yadeva 'anukUlam' aviruddhArthapratipAdakaM mAnavAdi purANAdikaM vA 'tat' sarvamapi 'shAstraMprakIrtitaM' prAmANikaiH 'ataH' etasmAt vedAt tadanukUlAchcha 'anyaH' viruddhaH udAsInashcha yo 'granthavistAraH' pAshupatAdi- rUpagranthavistaraH 'tannaiva shAstram', kintu 'kuvartma' kutsitamArgaH, mArga iva mArgaH, kutsitaj~nAnopAyosmAnamityarthaH| R^igAdikamevetyevakArastu viruddhAdiviShaya iti bhAvaH | skAnde purANe ityuktamityanvayaH | pAshupatAdeH kuvartmatva- mitishabdArthaH |
(12) itospi pAshupatAdikaM kuvartmetyAha - sAN^khyamiti | atraivaM yojanA - na kevalaM skAnde, kintu mokShadharmeShvapi | 'sAN^khyaM yogaH pAshupataM vedAraNyakameva cha' 'ityArabhya' upakramyAdhItena 
paJNcharAtras kR^itsnasya vaktA nArAyaNassvayam |
j~nAneShveteShu rAjendra sarveShvetaddhishiShyate ||
ityuttaravAkyena sAN^khyAdiShu prakR^iteShvapi tatparityAgena paJNcharAtrasyaiva prAmANyarUpamAdhikyamuktaM yatostaH pAshupatAdikaM kuvartma amAnameveti | nanvanena paJNcharAtraprAmANyameva bhavennAnyAprAmANyamityata Aha - itareShAmiti | vedapaJNcharAtrayoranyeShAM sAN^khyAdInAmityarthaH| 'bhinnamatattvaM' viruddhadarshanatvaM 'pradarshya' j~nApayitvA pratipAdyeti yAvat|
sAN^khyaM yogaH pAshupataM vedAraNyakameva cha |
j~nAnAnyetAni bhinnAni nAtra kAryA vichAraNA ||
iti vAkyasheSheNeti sheShaH | pradarshyetyasya paJNcharAtrasyaiva prAmANyamuktamityanenAnvayaH | parasparaviruddhAnAmeka- prAmANyoktAvanyAprAmANyalAbhAditi bhAvaH | tarhi vedAraNyakasyApyaprAmANyaM syAdityata Aha - vedeti | 'aikyAbhiprAyeNa' iti | ekArthatvarUpamUlamUlibhAvAbhiprAyeNetyarthaH | tathA cha paJNcharAtrasya vedasamAnArthatvena tatprAmANyoktau vedaprAmANyamevoktaM bhavatIti na tasyAprAmANyamiti bhAvaH | na chaikyAbhiprAyaH kutaH kalpyata iti vAchyam, yatosdR^iShTaviShayasya pauruSheyasya paJNcharAtrasya nirmUlatvesprAmANyAdAdhikyakathanamasaN^gataM syAt | 'sAN^khyam' IshvarAvatArAnyakapiloktaM shAstram |
kapilo vAsudevAkhyaH tantraM sAN^khyaM jagAda ha |
sarvAgamaviruddhaM cha kapilosnyo jagAda ha ||
ityuktatvAt | 'yogo' hi hiraNyagarbhoktaM pAtaJNjalam | 'pAshupataM' pashupatinA proktam | araNye nirjane deshe adhyetavyatvAdAraNyakamityupaniShaduchyate | vedAshchAraNyakAni cha, teShAM samAhAraH vedAraNyakaM, dvandvaikavadbhAvo vA | varNAshramarAjadAnadharmAdipratipAdyadharmabahutvAt mokShadharmANAM bhedAdvA mokShadharmeShviti bahuvachanam | ata eva tattvapradIpe - mokShadharmeShviti bahuvachanaM dharmabhedAdityuktam | mokShadharme hi -
sAN^khyaM yogaH pAshupataM vedAraNyakameva cha |
j~nAnAnyetAni bhinnAni utAho neti chochyatAm |
iti vaishampAyanoktaM prativachanaM chAsti | ime yudhiShThirabhIShmakartR^ike cha | bhagavataH j~nAnAni j~nAnasAdhanAni bhinnAni bhinnamatAni | viruddhanAmapi matAnAM na sarveShAM prAmANyaM sambhavati vastuno bahurUpatvAbhAvAt, kintvekasyAtra prAmANyamitareShAmaprAmANyaM vAchyam | tatra kasya prAmANyaM kasya vAsprAmANyamiti punaryudhiShThirajanamejaya- hArdaprashnottaramAha bhIShmo vaishampAyanashcha | "sAN^khyasya vaktA kapilaH" ityArabhya "paJNcharAtrasya kR^itsnasya" ityanena j~nAneShu j~nAnasAdhaneShu etatpaJNcharAtram | abhiprAyastu paramAptatamena nArAyaNena sarvasya paJNcharAtrasya kR^itatvA- tprAmANyaM tAvatsiddham, viruddhAnAM chaikaprAmANye anyAprAmANyaM cha| etachchAdyavAkyasthavedAraNyakapadena vedamUlakapaJNcha- rAtrasyottaravAkyasthapaJNcharAtrapadena cha mUlabhUtavedAraNyakasyopalakShaNAmaN^gIkR^ityobhayorekavAkyatAyAmeva sambhavati | anyathA paJNcharAtrasya pUrvamaprakR^itatvena pUrvottaravAkyayorasaN^gatatvApAtaH | upalakShaNAmaN^gIkR^ityaikavAkyatAyAM cha svIkR^itAyAM vedapaJNcharAtrayoreva prAmANayaM siddhyati | na tadviruddhapAshupatAdInAmiti teShAmaprAmANyameveti |
(13) evaM sUtraM vyAkhyAya yatpareNoktaM shAstrasya yoniriti tadayuktamiti bhAvena svAbhimatArthaM darshayati - shAstramiti | kAraNArthakena yonishabdena yogyatayA j~naptessambandhe pramANamiti paryavasya- tItyabhiprAyeNa 'yoniH pramANam' iti vyAkhyAtam | 'asya' jagatkAraNasya 'iti shAstrayoni' ityanantaraM tushabdosdhyAhAryaH | ata eva gItAbhAShye "iti tu shAstrayonitvam" ityuktam | turevArthaH | tathA cha - shAstraM yoniH pramANaM yasya tachChAstra- yonItyeva shAstrayonipadArtho brahma, na tu shAstrasya yonItyarthaH| paravyAkhyAnaM tUktAnupayuktamayuktaM cheti TIkAyAmeva dUShitam || 3 ||
|| iti shAstrayonitvAdhikaraNam ||
|| 4. samanvayAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe jagatkAraNasya shAstrayonitvAnna lakShaNAtivyAptiriti pUrvAdhikaraNaphalAkShepa- parihAramukhena tasya lakShaNatvasiddhaye viShNoreva jagatkAraNatvena shAstragamyatvaM netareShAmapIti samarthyate | pUrvapakShasUchanapUrvakaM siddhAntamAha - aj~nAnAmiti || kartari ShaShThIyam | itareShAM iti sambandhe | samuchchayArthasyAperubhayatrAnvayaH | pratItyA AgamopalakShaNA vA | tathA cha - na kevalaM pAshupatAdyuktam, kintu 'aj~nAnAM' shrutitAtparyArthAj~nAnibhi- rApAtataH j~nAyamAnamapi na kevalaM viShNoH kintu 'itareShAM' rudrAdInAmapi shAstrayonitvaM, jagatkAraNatvena shAstragamyatvaM netyarthaH | nanu pratItyAderaj~nAnamUlatvAdikaM parikalpyAnyeShAM kAraNatayA shAstrayonitvAgrahaNe ko heturiti pR^ichChati - kuta iti | pratIyamAnamapItyanenAsyAnvayaH | tatra hetukathanAya sUtramupanyasyati - tattviti | yata ityAdau grAhyam |
(2) sUtrAkSharANi vyAchaShTe - anvaya iti | anvIyate svArthena sambadhyate tatparatayA j~nAyate shAstraM shabdo vAsnenetyanvayaH upapattyAditAtparyaliN^gamityarthaH | sUtrAnusArAdekavachanaM samudAyAbhiprAyam | tena chopakramAdInAM kvachidavirodhaM sUchayati | AdipadaM shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAnasamAkhyAnAmapi grAhakam | atra shrutyAdiShaTkaM cha grAhyamiti TIkokteH | atra vAkye shrutyAdiShaTkamapyAdipadena grAhyamiti hi tasyArthaH |  parantu shrutyAdInAmupakramA- divattAtparyagrAhakatvAbhAvAdAgamArthamAtranirNAyakatvAt nAtra tannidarshakapramANoktiH |  ata evottaratra -
shrutirliN^gaM samAkhyA cha vAkyaM prakaraNaM tathA |
pUrvaM pUrvaM balIyaH syAdevamAgamanirNaye ||
iti tatrApi pramANaM vakShyati | uktaM hi pramANalakShaNaTIkAyAm "upakramAdInAM tAtparyaliN^gatvameteShAM punarartha eveti visheShaj~nApanArtho yogavibhAgaH" iti | na chaivam "atra shrutyAdiShaTkaM cha grAhyam" iti TIkAyAM tAtparyagrAhake- ShvantarbhAvoktirayukteti vAchyam, yatostretyasya samanvayashabdArtha ityevArtho na tAtparyagrahakeShviti, 'AkAsha- stalliN^gAt' 'shabdAdeva pramitaH' (bra.sU. 1-1-22, 7-24) ityAdau shrutiliN^gAdibhirAgamArthaniraNayadarshanena teShAmapi anvIyate shaktirUpasambandhavattayA j~nAyate padajAtamebhiritivyutpattyA anvayashabdArthatvauchityAt | na chopakramopasaMhArAbhyAsApUrvatAphalArthavAdopapattayaH shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAnasamAkhyAshcha tAtparyaliN^gAnIti j~nAna- pAdIyasudhAvirodha iti vAchyam, atra shakterapi saMyojanAt | ata eva chandrikAyAmupakramAdipramANakaH shaktitAtparya- lakShaNassambandhaH samanvaya ityuktam | atradipadaM shrutyAdInAmapi grAhakam | vyutkrameNAnvayaH | anenAtra bR^ihatsaMhitA- vachanodAharaNaM vakShyamANasya 
shrutirliN^gamiti vachanasyopalakShakamiti sUchitam |
(3) kAni tAnyupapattyAdIni kutra cha liN^gAnItyata Aha - uktaM cheti | upapattyAdItyanuShajyate| na kevalamupapattyAdyuktaM nirdiShTaM, kintu tajj~nApyaM choktamiti chArthaH | asmaduktamupapattyAdi liN^gaM bR^ihatsaMhitAyAmapyukta- miti vA | kimuktamityatastatpaThati - upakrameti | prakaraNAdirupakramaH tadanta upasaMhAraH | upakramopasaMhArashcha tau tathoktau | atropakramopasaMhAratadaikarUpyAbhyAsApUrvatAphalArthavAdAshcheti pramANalakShaNokteH pratyekavivakShayA vishakali- tAvupakramopasaMhArau dvau samudAyavivakShayA ubhayAvirodhalakShaNaM ekArthatvalakShaNaM vA tadaikarUpyamapi pR^ithaktAtparyagrAhaka- manusandheyam | ata eva dvivachanaprayogaH | ekaprakArAsakR^iduktirabhyAsaH | prAchuryeNa pramANAntarAsiddhArthabodhakatA apUrvatA | phalavadarthapratipAdakaM phalam | stutiH, nindA, ekakartR^ikopAkhyAnarUpA parakR^itiH, anekakartR^ikopAkhyAna- rUpaH purAkalpashcha, arthavAdaH | upapattiH yuktiH | 'tAtparyanirNaye' vAkyatAtparyanishchaye 'liN^gaM' sAdhanamitiyarthaH| yadvA - nirNetavye tAtparye sAdhye 'liN^gaM' heturityarthaH| liN^gamityasya upakramAdipadaiH yathAyogyaM pratyekaM sambandhaH | smR^iterupakramAditvespi virodhe uttarottaraprAbalyasUchanAya bhAShye upapattyAdIti vyatyasyoktiH | sAmAnyavisheShabhAvena upapatterupakramAdibhyaH pR^ithaguktiH | yadvA - etachchopakramAdi svArthe shabdAtmakamapi idametatparam abAdhe satyetadupa- kramatvAt ityAdirUpeNa vAkyatAtparye liN^gaM cha bhavati | upapattistu yathAsgnyAdirUpasvarthe tathA tAtparyespi ayametattAtparyaviShayaH upapannatvAt iti prakAreNa liN^garUpeti pR^ithaguktiH |
(4) sUtraM yojayati - upakramAdIti | 'shAstre' iti sheShaH | samityasyArthaH samyagiti | sarvasminnityapi draShTavyam | 'nirUpyamANe' ityanena saMshabdArthasya adhyAhR^itakriyayAsnvayo  darshitaH | tushabdasyArtha eveti | 'shAstrayoni' ityanuShaktapadasyArthaH shAstrAgamyamiti | tathA cha yatostrAnvayapadoktaiH shrutiliN^gavAkyaprakaraNasthAna- samAkhyopakramAdibhiH shaktitAtparyaliN^gaiH 'saM samyak' balAbalavimarshapUrvakaM 'sarvasmin' shAstre R^igAdirUpe 'nirUpyamANe' vichAryamANe ekArthe shaktitAtparyarUpavyApakadharmavattayA avagamyamAne 'tadeva' viShNvAkhyaM brahmaiva 'shAstragamyaM' tatpramANakaM pratIyate, na rudrAdi, atosj~nAnAM pratIyamAnamapi netareShAM shAstrayonitvamiti yojanA | liN^gairiti tR^itIyayA nirUpyamANe iti saptamIprayoge cha upakramAdikaM tAtparyahetuH | tAtparyaM cha shAstrapramANakatve heturiti sUchitaM bhavati | na kevalamupapattyAdikaM samanvayashabdArthaH, kintu taddhetukaH shAstrajanyapramAgocharatvarUpaH shAstrayonitve hetubhUtaH | "tatparatvasambandhospi" iti sudhokteH | anena 'samanvayAt' sAvakAshatvaniravakAsha- tvAdinA balAbalanishchayapurassaraM anyatarabAdhayA vAkyArthavimarsharUpasamyagvichAritatvalakShaNasamyakttvayuktAdupakramA- 
dishaktitAtprayaliN^gasamudAyAtmasamanvayAt sarvashAstrasya bhagavatyeva samyagvachanavR^ittyA shaktitAtparyAkhya- sambandhAvagamAt tadviShNvAkhyaM brahmaiva jagatkAraNatayA shAstrayoni na rudrAdIti 'samanvayAt' ityasyAvR^ittyA sUtrayojanA darshitA bhavati |
(5) nanu karmavidhAnAdirUpashAstrasya kathaM brahmaparatetyAshaN^kAM bhagavadvAkyena pratiShedhati - mAmiti| yadyapi bhAgavate "ityasyA hR^idayaM loke" iti pAThaH, tathA pUrvottarArdhayorvyutkrameNa pAThashcha dR^ishyate| tathAspyAchAryokte- ranyakalpIyosyamityadoShaH | ekAdashaskandhe uddhavaM prati kR^iShNavachanametat | atrAsmachChabdena kR^iShNa uchyate | tathA cha "vasante vasante" ityAdi karmavidhAtrI shrutiH 'mAm' uddishyaiva matpUjAtvena karmavidhatte | indrAdyabhidhAtrI 'mAmabhidhatte' madguNAnaishvaryAdInabhidhatte | 'ahaM vikalpyaH' kalpanaM vidhAnaM tathA cha -
chatvAri vAkparimitA padAni tAni vidurbrAhmaNA ye manIShiNaH |
guhA trINi nihitA neN^gayanti turIyaM vAcho manuShyA vadanti || (R^i. 1-164-45.)
iti shrutyA yA vAgvaktR^ittvAnnimittAdvAkbdito hariH tasyA yAni sthAnApekShayA 'parimitAni' parichChinnAni 'chatvAri padAni' vAsudevAdirUpANi tAni ye manIShiNaH brAhmaNAH ta eva viduH | tatra vAcho hR^idayaguhAyAM nihitAni vAsudevAditrINi rUpANi 'manuShyAH' sAdhAraNAH 'neN^gayanti' na jAnanti | 'turIyam' aniruddhAkhyaM tu 'vadanti' jAnanatItyevaMrUpeNa ahameva chatuShTvasaN^khyAvishiShTavAsudevAdivividharUpatayA bahutvena vidheya ityarthaH | 'ahama- pohyaH' 'na surAM pibet' (manu. 11-94.) ityAdivAkyenApriyAditi sheShaH| tathA cha "niShedhabuddhiviShayamapriyaM hi hareH smR^itam" iti bhAgavatatAtparyokteH surApAnAdikaM madaprItisAdhanatvAt niShidhyate ityapriyadvArA 'na surAM pibet' ityAdinA ahameva niShedhya ityarthaH | athavA - ahamapriyAdapohyaH mamAprItikarAtsurApAnashabditAt "surA harerguNA me syuH" iti chintanAttapadapekShya apohyo niShedhya ityarthaH | taduktaM bhAgavatatAtparye - vidhirUpatvena kalpanaM vikalpaH chatvAri vAgityAdi | tatra vAgityanuvAdaH |
vidhibhAge hareH pUjaivAbhidhAne cha tadguNAH |
vikalpe tadbahutvaM chApyapohe tu tadapriyam |
uchyate sarvavedeShu tachcha veda sa eva hi || iti | tathA -
surA harerguNAH proktAste me syuriti chintanam |
surApAnamiti proktaM tanna kuryAtkathaJNchana || iti |
tattvapradIpe tu - 'dve vA va brahmaNo rUpe' iti vikalpya vividhaM kalpayitvA 'tatra yassa AtmA' (talavakArabrAhmaNam) iti sadoShAdapohyo nirdoShatvena vidheyospyahamevetyarthaH uktaH | atra tattvapradIpapakShe vikalpyeti lyap | TIkAkR^itpakShe tu vikalpyashabdassamAsAntargato vyasto veti visheShaH | iyaM cha bhagavati 
vAkyasamanvayarItiH - Adyasya itishabdasya prakArArthasya hR^idayamityanenAnvayaH | dvitIyasya evaMbhUtAyA ityarthaH | tathA cha hyevaMbhUtAyA vidhiniShedhAdirUpAyA anyaparatvena pratItAyAshchAsyAshshruteriti 'mAM vidhatte' ityAdyuktaprakAreNa 'hR^idayaM' tAtparyam 'ahameva veda' jAnAmi 'madanyaH kashchana' kospi visheShataH prAyaH na veda na jAnAtItyarthaH | bhAgavata ityanantaraM tadeva shAstragamya- mityuktatvAt na kathamitishaN^kAvakAsha iti vAkyasheShaH || 4 ||
|| iti samanvayAdhikaraNam ||
|| 5. IkShatyadhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe saMshabdoktaM vAchyatvaM kArtsnyaM chAkShipya samAdhIyate | pUrvapakShayati - nanviti | 'ityAdibhishshrutibhiH' iti tR^itIyApaà¤¼JNchamyarthe | netyAdyAvartate | tathA cha 'tat' pUrvasUtre tachChabdoktaM brahmashabdagocharaM shAstroktaM kAraNaM na, kutaH? yato na shabdagocharaM shAstramukhyArthaH na, tadapi kutaH? yato na shabdagocharaM shabdAvAchyaM, nachekShaNIyatvavirodhaH tadasiddheH | kutaH? yato na tadgocharaM j~nAnaviShayaH na, aj~neyamiti yAvat | na chAvAchyatvAj~neyatvayorasiddhiH | "yato vAcho nivartante" ityAdi shruteriti yojanA| 'yato vAchaH' iti vAkye avAchyatvasya 'aprApya manasA saha' ityaj~neyatvasya cha uktatvAditi bhAvaH | "trayI na shrutigocharA" ityatra gocharashabdasya visheShyaliN^gatayA prayogAt 'na tachChabdagocharam' iti sAdhu | sudhAyAM tu shabdAnAM gavAM j~nAnAnAM charashcharaNaM vR^ittiryasmin tachChabdagocharamiti vyadhikaraNabahuvrIhiM charashcharaNamasyAstIti matvarthIyAchpratyayAntatvaM chAshritya shabdagocharamityasya sAdhutvamuktam | 'yataH' iti taittirIyavAkyam | yato 'vAcho' vedA vAgindriyANi cha 'manasA' manorUpendriyeNa saha 'tamaprApya' tadviShayakavR^ittij~nAnamajAnantya eva nivartante | taM brahmaNa AnandaM vidvAnna bibheti ityarthaH | guNaguNinorabhedAshrayeNaitadudAhR^itam |
(2) 'ashabdam' iti kAThakavAkyam | atra sarvatra yachChabdo yojyaH | na vidyate shabdo guNaH pramANaM vA yasmiMstattathoktam | prAkR^itashabdaguNashUnyaM shabdapramANAviShayaH shabdabhinnaM chetyarthaH | 'asparshaM' sparshaguNashUnyaM tata eva sparshaliN^gAviShayaH tadbhinnaM cha, 'arUpaM' rUparahitam ata eva chakShuShapratyakShAviShayastadbhinnaM cha | 'arasaM' rasaguNashUnyaM rasabhinnaM cha | agandhamityasyApyupalakShakametat | 
anena paà¤¼JNchamAtrAvilakShaNatvamapyuktam | 'avyayaM nityam' ityAbhAyAM svarUpato dehatashcha nAshashUnyatva- muchyate | agandhavadityanena gandhavatpR^ithivIlakShaNatvamuktam | anenopalakShaNayA paJNchamahAbhUtavilakShaNatva- mapyuktaM bhavati | asya 'nichAyya taM mR^ityumukhAtpramuchyate' ityanenAnvayaH| 
(3) 'avachanena' ityanyachChrutivAkyam | 'avachanena' vachanavR^ittiM vinaiva lakShaNayA 'provAcha brahma guruH' shiShyAyopadidesheti pararItyAsrthaH |
(4) 'yadvAchA' ityanyattalavakAravAkyam | 'vAchA' taduchchAryeNa shabdena yat 'anabhyuditam' anuktam | yena vAk 'abhyudyate' uchyate | shrotrendriyeNa na shrR^iNoti puruShaH | yenedaM shrotraM shrutaM tadeva brahma tvaM viddhItyarthaH | atra pUrvapakSharItyA vachanavR^ittiniShedhaH | AdipadenaivaMjAtIyakA shrutirgR^ihyate |
(5) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArayati - neti || itishabda Avartate | tathA cha atra sUtrakAraH iti pUrvapakShyuktaM shrutitAtparyAparij~nAnaprAptaM brahmaNosvAchyatvaM neti niShedhatItyarthaH | sUtraM paThati - IkShateriti | atra tadityanuvartate | tachcha AsdhyAyaparisamApteH vidheyasamarpakamapIhoddeshyasamarpakam | na vidyate shabdo vAchako yasya tadashabdam | tathA cha 'tat' brahma 'ashabdaM' shabdAvAchyaM na, kintu vAchyameva | kutaH? IkShateH | dhAtunirdeshosyaM, tathaiva sudhokteH | tathAspi shabdamAtrasyAsAdhakatayA tena tadartho lakShyate | tena prakR^itAnukUlatayekShaNIyatvaM vivakShyate | tathA cha 'IkShateH' IkShaNIyatvAt j~nAnaviShayatvAdityarthaH ityAshayena sUtraM vyAchaShTe - sa iti | idaM cha ShaTprashnavAkyam | atra "yaH punaretaM trimAtreNaumityanenaivAkShareNa paraM puruShamabhidhyAyIta sa tejasi sUrye sampanno yathA pAdodarastavachA vinirmuchyate evaM ha vai sa pApmanA vinirmuktaH sa sAmabhirunnIyate brahmalokam" iti pUrvavAkye prakR^ito yaH akArokAramakArAkhyAMshatrayayuktapraNavoktaprakAreNa paramAtmAnamabhidhyAya tamaparokShIkR^itya cha tejorUpe sUrye sampannatvagvinirmuktasarpavadvidhUtapApassAmAbhimAnidevaiH satyAkhyaM brahmalokaM prAptaH praNavopAsako jIvaH saH 'jIvaghanAt' jIvasArAttachChreShThAt 'etasmAt' chaturmukhAttadupadeshena 'parAtparam' uttamAduttamaM 'purishayaM' sakaladehAntargataM 'puruShaM' pUrNaM vAsudevaM paramAtmAnaM 'IkShate' jAnAtItyarthaH | yadyapi ShaTprashnaTIkAyAM "jIvaghanAdviriJNchAttadupAsanayeti yAvat, IkShate punarabhivR^iddhaj~nAno bhavati | IkShitvAcha taM prApnoti" ityukterIkShatera- parokShaj~nAnArthatvaM pratIyate | tathApi mUle j~nAnasAmAnyaviShayatvarUpekShaNIyatvahetorasiddhiparihArAya asyAH shruterupanyastatvAt "hiraNyagarbhopadeshena" iti TIkokteshcheha prakR^itAnuguNyAdIkShatiH parokShaj~nAnArtho vyAkhyeyaH| 'Atmani' ityaparaM kANvavAkyaM jij~nAsAnaye vyAkR^itam | 'vij~nAya' ityanyadvAjasaneyavAkyam| 'brAhmaNo' brahmaniShTho dhIraH 'taM' paramAtmAnamevaM shAstreNAchAryAdvA 'vij~nAya' parokShato j~nAtvA 'praj~nAM' prakR^iShTamapokShaj~nAnaM 'kurvIta' 
sampAdayedityarthaH | ityAdIti | evamAdivAkyairityarthaH | Adishabdena "AtmA vA are draShTavyaH" (bR^i.u. 4-4-5.) "ajaAtmA mahAn dhruvaH" (bR^i.u. 6-4-20.) "tameva dhIro vij~nAya" (bR^i.u. 6-4-21.) ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | IkShaNIyatvAt | avagamopalakShakametat | anyathAsnanvayAt | anenAsiddhiH parihR^itA | tadanyathAs- nupapatteriti sheShaH | vAchyameveti sautranaJNdvayalabdhArthoktiH | na tvavAchyaM nApi lakShyamiti evashabdArthaH | tadityanenAsyAnvayaH | aniyamasUchanAya sUtrabhAShyayoH pratij~nAhetvorvyutkrameNoktiH |
(6) nanvastvIkShaNIyatvaM brahmaNaH, tathAspi na tadanyathAnupapattyA tasya vAchyatvaM vAchyaM pratyakShAdinAspIkShaNIyatvopapatterityata Aha - aupaniShadatvAditi | tadityetadvipariNamyAnuvartate | tathA cha 'tasya' brahmaNaH 'aupaniShadatvAt' upaniShadekasamadhigamyatvAt 'avachanena' vachanetarapramANena 'IkShaNaM' j~nAnaM netyarthaH | tathA cha shrutismR^itisAhAyyarahitapratyakShAdyavedyatvavishiShTekShaNIyatvAnyathAsnupapattyA brahmaNo vAchyatvaM siddhyatyeveti bhAvaH | parisheShapramANaparatayA vA idamAvR^ittya vyAkhyeyam | yojanA tu brahmaNashrutiShUktaM IkShaNaM pramANenaiva hi bhavet | prasaktapramANeShu cha 'nAvachanena' vachanetarapramANenekShaNaM sambhavati aupaniShadatvAt vachanenaiva bhavadIkShaNaM nAvachanena vachanavR^ittyanyalakShaNAdinA sambhavati | kutaH? 'avachanena' bhAvapradhAno bahuvrIhiH | avachanatvenAvAchyatvena nimittena ataH parisheShAdIkShaNaM vAchyatvameva sAdhayatIti |
(7) nanu shrutisiddhamavAchyatvaM kathamIkShaNIyatvayuktimAtreNa dUShyate? 'prAbalyamAgamasyaiva' iti yuktitaH shruteH  prAbalyokterityataH sautro heturAgamopalakShaka iti bhAvena vAchyatve shrutismR^itI chAha - sarva iti || kaThAnAmiyaM shrutiH| sarve vedA 'yatpadaM' yasya brahmaNaH svarUpam 'Amananti' mukhyavR^ittyA satAtparyaM pratipAdayanti | sarve vedAH sarvANi tapAMsi prasiddhAni 'yat' brahma prati 'vadanti' yaduddeshena kartavyAnIti bodhayantItyarthaH | tattvapradIparItyA 'tapAMsi' AlochanarUpA yuktaya iti vA | sarvairvedairahameva 'vedyo' mukhyataH pratipAdyaH | ahaM 'vedAntakR^it' brahmasUtrakR^it 'vedavit' vedArthaj~nAnI cheti gItAsmR^ityarthaH | AdipadAt 'atha kasmAduchyate' 'nAmAni sarvANi' 'vachasAM vAchyamuttamam' ityAdessaN^grahaH | tathA cha shrutau 'Amananti' iti sAkShAdvAchyatvokteH, smR^itau cha 'ahameva' ityavadhAraNopapattaye mukhyatayA vedyatvasya vivakShaNIyatvAt tasya cha vAchyatvaM vinAsyogAtsarvashabdalakShaNAyAshchA- sambhavAdvAchyatvamevAbhyAM siddhyatIti bhAvaH | smR^itibhyashchetyasya vAchyamevetyanenAnvayaH | AdishabdopAttashrutismR^itya- pekShayA bahuvachanam | na kevalamIkShaNIyatvahetoriti chArthaH |
(8) nanvevaM vAchyatvasya yuktyAdisiddhatve avAchyatvAj~neyatvAbhidhAyakodAhR^itashruteH 'yato vAchaH' ityAdirUpAyAH kA gatirityata Aha - avAchyatvAdikamiti | aj~neyatvamatarkyatvaM cha AdishabdArthaH | tushabdaH shaN^kAvyAvartakaH bhinnakrameNAvadhAraNe vA | tathA cha 'aprasiddhatvAt' sAkalyena agocharatvA- nnimittAdeva brahmaNi 'avAchyatvAdikam' avAchyatvAdivyapadesho yujyata iti na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH | anena siddhAnte 'ashabdam' ityAderaprasiddhatvAtsAkalyena vAchakashabdashUnyamityAdirthaH | 'avachanena' ityasya tu sAkalyena vachanamantareNetyartha ityuktaM bhavati |
(9) nanvaprasiddhinimittakosvAchyatvAdivyapadeshaH kva dR^iShTa ityata Aha - na taditi | yasmAt 'vipashchito' j~nAnino mero rUpaM pashyantospi 'IdR^igiti' sAkalyena 'na pashyanti' na jAnanti | anenAprasiddhatvahetuH sUchitaH | tasmAnmero rUpaM na j~neyaM pratyakSheNa | na vAchyaM shabdena | 'na tarkyate' nAnumIyate cha liN^genetyuchyata ityarthaH | itivaditi | iti vAkya ivetyarthaH | asyAvAchyatvAdikamiti pUrveNAnvayaH |  tathA cha yathA merurUpe aprasiddhi- nimittakAvAchyatvAdivyapadeshastathA brahmaNyapIti bhAvaH |
(10) na kevalaM 'pashyantaH' ityuktyanyathAsnupapattimAtreNaiva aprasiddheraj~neyatvAtarkyatvAvAchyatvavyapadesha iti vyavasthA siddhA, api tu smR^itisiddhA cheti bhAvenAha - aprasiddheriti | tadbrahma yataH 'paraM' pUrNam atassAkalyenAprasiddhatvAdavAchyamuchyate | sarvasadAgamoktatvAttatprasiddhatvAdvAchyaM cha bhavatItyarthaH | evamaprasiddhi- prasiddhibhyAM tat atarkyam anumeyaM cha aj~neyaM j~neyaM j~nAnipratyakShagamyaM cha 'smR^itaM' smR^itikArairuktamityarthaH | gAruDe ityanantaraM uktamiti sheShaH | asyApyavAchyatvAdikamityanenAnvayaH |
(11) evaM 'yato vAchaH' ityAdishrutInAM yuktyAdibalAdarthAntaropapatterna tadbalAchChabdAvAchyaM brahmeti sUtraM vyAkhyAyApavyAkhyAM pratyAkhyAti - na cheti | chashabdaH svasiddhamapi netisamuchchaye | tathA cha jagatkAraNaM 'ashabdaM' pradhAnaM na, kutaH? ashabdaM hi tat | 'ashabdaM' pradhAnaM kAraNaM neti vA, kutaH? 'IkShateH' 'tadaikShata' iti jagatkAra- NasyekShaNakartR^itvashravaNAtpradhAnasya chAchetanatvena tadasambhavAditi sAN^khya- matanirAkaraNaparatayA vyAkhyAne prathama- pratij~nAyAM hetUkR^itam 'ashabdatvam' ashrautatvam 
'itarasiddhaM' svetarasAN^khyasiddhaM na, na kevalametAvat, kintu svasiddhamapi na, sAN^khyena vaidikatvAbhyupagateH | sUtrakAreNa 'ajAmekAm' (tai. A. 10-10-1.) ityAdi shrutyuktatvAN^gIkArAt |
yadvA - tattvapradIparItyA mAyinA sAN^khyaM prati hetutvenopanyastamashabdatvaM mAyItarasya sAN^khyasya na siddhaM nApi sAN^khyetaramAyisiddhamuktahetubhyAmeva | tathA chAsiddhiriti na tadvyAkhyAnaM yuktamitibhAvaH | evamashabdatvaM shrautatvaM brahmaNassAN^khyetaramAyisiddhaM na, tanmate avAchyatvAt | chakArAdIkShitR^itvamapi siddhaM na, tasyekShati- svarUpatvAdityapi vyAkhyeyam | tathA cha hetudvayamapi svapakShapratikUlamiti na paravyAkhyA yukteti bhAvaH tattvapradIpe tu 'nacha' ityAdibhAShyaM 'itarasiddhaM' mAyisiddhamashabdatvaM na shrutyarthaH uktanyAyena brahmaNo vAchyatvAt | evam 'ashabdatvam' avAchyatvaM brahmaNa itarasya mAyinospi na siddham | brahmaNi vyavahArAbhAvaprasaN^gAt iti dvedhA vyAkhyAyaparakR^itavyAkhyApratyAkhyAnAya paroktahetoShTIkArItyAssiddhyuktiparatayAspi vyAkhyAtam || 5 ||
(12) IkShaNIyatvasya hetorvyadhikaraNAsiddhimAkShipya samAdhAtuM sUtram - 'oM gauNashchennAtmashabdAt' iti | asyArthaH - 'yataH AtmanyevAtmAnaM pashyet' ityAdishrutyukta AtmA 'gauNaH' sattvAdiguNabaddho jIva evAtasta- danyathAsnupapattyA vAchyospi sa eva syAnna nirguNaH paramAtmeti chet - na, kutaH? 'AtmAnaM pashyet' itIkShaNIye tasminnAtmashabdashravaNAditi | 'AtmapatasAmAnAdhikaraNyAya pulliN^ganirdeshaH' ||
(13) sUtraM vyAchaShTe - na cheti | atra yato 'dR^ishyaH' IkShatishrutau dR^ishyatayoktaH 'AtmA' jIvAkhyo gauNa eva atastadanyathAnupapattyA vAchyospi sa eva syAt 'na nirguNaH' guNAtIto viShNuH 'dR^ishyaH' IkShatishruttyuktaH | gauNa- grahaNe bAdhakasyetaraj~nApakasya chAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | ato na sa vAchyaH iti chodyaM na yuktam | kutaH? 'Atma- shabdAt' 'Atmanyeva' iti vAkye IkShaNIye tasmin AtmashabdashravaNAddR^ishyo nirguNa eva, ata evekShatyA liN^gena vAchyospi sa eva bhavediti yojanA | yadyapi sudhAyAM gauNapadaM mAyAshabalitaishvaryAdidharmayuktasaguNabrahmaparatayA vyAkhyAtaM tathApi pUrvapakShiNo mAyAshabalitaM vA guNabaddhA jIvA vA dR^ishyA vAchyAshcha, na sarvathA nirguNaM brahmetyAshayAnna virodhaH |
(14) nanvAtmashabdasadbhAve kutosyaM nirguNo na gauNa ityata Aha - ya iti | yaH 'sarvataH' prakAreNa 'guNaiH' sattvAdibhiH shUnyaH yashcha dukhakhAdidoSharahitaH yashcha heyopAdeyarahitaH | bhAvapradhAnosyam | heyatvasahitopAde- yatvarahita iti | upAdeya evetyarthaH | tattvapradIparItyA svAbhAvikadoSharahito guNapUrNatvenAptakAmatvAdupAdeyarahita iti vA | tattvodyotaTIkArItyA doShAbhAvAddhAturabhAvAdvA heyatvarahitaH, laukikaguNAbhAvAdupAdAturanyasya svatantra- syAbhAvAdvA upAdeyatvarahitaH aniShTAbhAvAddheyaM nAsti, apUrtyabhAvAdupAdeyamasya nAstIti vA tathoktaH | ya evaM bhUtassa AtmetyabhidhIyate | ya etadviruddhasvabhAvavAn sosnAtmeti satAM mataM sammatamitythaH | kvachit 'hR^idi hyeSha AtmA' 
ityAdAvetadanyasvabhAvespyAtmapadaprayogAt kathaM sosnAtmetyata Aha - anAtmanIti | 'anAtmani' Atma- shabdamukhyArthabhinne jIve 'AtmashabdaH' 'sopachAraH' upachAraH paramamukhyavR^ittyanyamukhyavR^ittiH tatsahitastadvR^ittika ityarthaH| tushabdo visheShArthaH | 'vAmane' ityanantaraM 'nirguNaikaniShThatvenoktAt' iti sheShaH | asya nAyaM dR^ishyo vAchyashcha gauNaH, kintu nirguNa evetyanenAnvayaH |
(15) atraiva pramANAntaramAha - dve vAveti | 'brahmaNaH' parabrahmaNaH rUpaM cha rUpaM cha rUpe | tatrAdyo rUpashabdaH svarUpaparaH dvitIyo rUpyate j~nAyate brahmAkhyamiti vyutpattyA pratimAparaH | vAveti nipAtasamudAyaH prasiddhidyotakaH | te rUpe darshayati - Atmeti | AtmashabdamukhyavAchyastadavAchyashchetyarthaH | 'tatra' AtmanAtnormadhye 'sa yaH' ityanvayaH | anyathA paunaruktyAt | tathA cha 'saH' prasiddho 'yaH' AtmA AtmashabdamukhyArtho viShNuH 'saH nityaH' dehahAnyAdirahitaH 'shuddhaH' karmalepavidhuraH 'kevalaH' jaDAmishraH 'nirguNaH' sattvAdiguNAbaddha ityarthaH | cho visheShaNasamuchchaye | evaM prathamoddiShTAtmashabdArthaM lakShaNamukhena pradarshya athAnAtmAnamuktalakShaNavyatirekamukhena darshayati - atheti | yasmAdAtmA evaM bhUtaH 'atha' tasmAt 'yosnIdR^ishaH' nityatvAdirahitaH ha prasiddhaH | 'sosnAtmeti' satAM sammatamityarthaH | 'brAhmaNam' ityanantaraM yato nirguNasya viShNorevAtmatvaM vaktIti sheShaH | asyApi 'vAmane' itivadanvayaH |
(16) nanUpachAreNApyAtmashabdasya gauNe prayogasadbhAvAtsa eva shrutyukto dR^ishya AtmA kiM na syAdityata Aha - na cheti | 'mukhye' AtmapadamukhyArthe nirguNe dR^ishyatayekShatishrutipratipAdye sambhavati sati amukhyArthagauNagrahaNaM na yujyata ityarthaH | atra satItyanena mukhyasambhavAkhyo heturuktaH | amukhyaM na yujyata ityanena sAdhyam | ubhaya- samuchchaye shaN^kAparihArasamuchchaye vA chashabdaH || 6 ||
(17) nanu Atmashabdo mukhyata eva gauNAtmaparaH kiM na syAt | na choktashrutismR^itivirodhaH, tatrAtmashabdo nirguNe viShNau mukhyo jIveShvamukhya ityanukteH AtmanAtmashabdayoshchetanAchetanaviShayatvasambha- vAt | kaà¥¢JNcha - AtmAnAtmashabdayoH prasiddhachetanAchetanaparatveshruterArjavaM, prasiddhArthAparityAgAt, rUpashabdasyAnekArthAkalpanAchcha | na cha jIve nirdoShatvAdyayogaH, duHkhAdidoShasyaupAdhikatvena jIvasyApi svabhAvato nirdoShatayA shruteH svabhAvaviShayatvopapatterityAshaN^kAM parihartuM sUtraM paThati - oM tanniShThasya iti|| neti vartate | tathA cha - 'tanniShThasya' asya Atmaj~nAninaH 'mokShopadeshAt' nAtmashabdamukhyavAchyo gauNa iti sUtrArthaH |
(18) tanniShThasya mokShopadeshespi kutosyamAtmA na gauNa ityaprayojakatvamAshaN^khyAha - na hIti | 
gauNamokShapadasamabhivyAhR^ito hishabdo virodhAkhyahetusUchakaH | tathA cha - 'hi' yasmAt 'gauNAtmaniShThasya' guNabaddhajIvaj~nAninaH tajj~nAnAdguNabandhanivR^ittirUpo 'mokSho' na sambhavati, virodhAt tasmAt 'na hi' nAprayojakatA shaN^kyetyarthaH |
(19) asiddhishaN^kAM parihartuM kossAvAtmaniShThasya mokShopadesha ityatastaM darshayati - yasyeti | atra shrutiH svaprayuktamushabdam eveti vyAchaShTe | 'u' ekaH pradhAna iti vA | tachChabdo viShNutajj~nAniparaH | tathA cha - 'hi' yasmAt 'saH' viShNuH 'sarvasya kartA' tasmAdeva 'vishvakR^it' vAyukartA 'pratibuddhaH' svatassarvaj~naH 'asmin sandohe' sanduhyate puruShArtho aneneti vA kAryakAraNasaN^khAtarUpatvAdvA bhUtasamudAyarUpatvAdvA sandohanAmake madhyadehe sthite 'gahane' gambhIre hR^idayaguhAsthAne 'praviShTaH' saH 'AtmA'  viShNuH 'yasya' yenopAsakena 'anuvittaH' samayagj~nAtaH 'tasya' adhikAriNaH 'u' pradhAnaH tasya viShNoryo 'lokaH' sa eva lokaH sthAnaM bhavatItyarthaH | 'sandoghe' iti pAThespyayayamevArthaH 'sandehe' iti pAThe anekArthasaN^kaTa ityarthaH | tattvapradIpe tu - sa vishvakR^it kR^itakR^ityaH | kutaH? yataH sa hi paramAtmA prasannaH sarvashaktiH sarvamasya j~nAninaH kAryaM karotItyuktam | asmin pakShe prathamaH prathamAntatachChabdo viShNuj~nAniparaH, vishvashabdaH kR^ityaparaH, sarvashabdo j~nAnikAryaparaH | TIkAkR^itpakShe tu - prathamaH prakR^itaviShNuparaH, vishvashabdo vAyuparaH, sarvashabdo jagatpara iti bhedaH | pakShadvayespi dvitIyatR^itIyau viShNutallokapara| 'iti' ityevaMrUpe bR^ihadAraNyake 'AtmaniShThasya' tajj~nAnino 'mokSha upadishyate' | asya yata ityupadishyate ato 'na gauNa AtmA' iti vakShyamANapratij~nayAsnvayaH | sUtrasya tu na gauNa Atmashabda iti pUrveNAnvayaH | Atmetyanena sautratachChabdo nAtmashabdaparaH, kintvarthataH pradhAnAtmapara ityuktaM bhavati |
(20) Atmashabdo viShNAveva mukhyaH na jIveShvityatra na kevalaM tanniShThasyetyAdinoktamanumAnaM mAnam, kintu sUtrakR^idabhipretAH spaShTashrutismR^itayashcheti bhAvena tAM tAshchAha - ayamiti | brahmetyantasya upadishyata iti pUrve- NAnvayaH | 'ayamAtmA' ramAbrahmAdiShu AdAnAdikartR^itvena sthitaH AtmA 'brahma' viShNureveti mANDUkashrutyarthaH "sosyaM viShNU ramAbrahmarudrAnantAdigaH sadA | AdAnAdanakartR^itvAdAtmA" iti mANDUkabhAShyoktaH |
(21) "vadanti tattattvavidastattvaM yajj~nAnamadvayam | brahma" ityaparaM bhAgavatavAkyam | advayaM samAdhikashUnyaM j~nAnasvarUpaM yattattvaM vadanti j~nAninaH tat deshakAlAdiShu bR^iMhitatvAt sarvAntaryAmitvAdyaishvaryAdiguNavAttvAchcha nimittAt 'brahmeti paramAtmeti bhagavAniti shabdyate' abhidhIyata ityarthaH | asyApi pUrveNa sambandhaH | tatraiva chaturthaskandhe "dattam" ityanyadvAkyam | etachcha 'anasUyA 
tathaivAtrerjaj~ne putrAnakalmaShAn' iti pUrvArdhenaivAnvetavyam |
patnI marIchessukalA suShuve kardamAtmajA |
kAshyapaM pUrNimAnaM cha yayorApUritaM jagat ||
iti prakR^itena samuchchayArthastathAshabdaH | tathA cha - anasUyAkhyA atribhAryA atreH sakAshAt 'AtmeshabrahmasambhavAn' AtmA viShNurIshorudraH brahmA chaturmukhaH AtmA cheshashcha brahmA cha te tathoktAH taissaha bhavantItyAtmeshabrahmasambhavAH tAn 'akalmaShAn' apApAn yo dattaH durvAsAH somashchaitAn putrAn 'jaj~ne' janayAmAsetyarthaH | yadvA - anasUyA atrerdattAdIn janayAmAsa, te cha AtmeshabrahmasambhavA iti vipariNAmena vyAkhyeyam | atra brahmAveshena sahotpanne chandre niruktasambhavashabdo mukhyaH | sAkShAdviShNurudrAMshatvena tatsambhUtayordattadurvAsasostu ChatrinyAyenAmukhya iti draShTavyam | yadyapi "atreH patnyanasUyA trIn jaj~nestiyashasaH sutAn | dattam" iti bhAgavatapAThaH, tathAspyanuvyAkhyAne evaM paThitatvAttathaiva sudhAyAM vyAkhyAtatvAttadanyakalpIyaM pAThAntaraM bhaviShyatItyadoShaH | asyApItyupadishyata ityane- nAnvayaH | chetanastviti pAdmavAkyam | 'prabho' iti kasyachitsambodhanam | tatreti sheShaH | Adyastushabdo visheShArthaH | dvitIyosvadhAraNe | tathA cha - 'jIvAH brahmAdayaH proktAH AtmA tu' tachChabdamukhyavAchyastu 'janArdano' viShNuH 'ekaH' eva proktaH pramANeShu | 'itareShu' brahmAdiShu 'AtmashabdaH sopAchAraH' paramamukhyavR^ittyapekShayA hInavR^itti- yukta iti j~nAnibhirabhidhIyata ityartaH | kutastasyaivAtmatvaM nAnyeShAmityata Aha - tasyeti | yataH 'tasya' nirguNasya Atmano 'j~nAnAnmokSho' bhavatIti "yasyAnuvittaH" (bR^i.u. 6-4-31.) ityAdau 'udAhR^itaH' uktaH atosyamAtmA nirguNo viShNureva nAnyaH | kutaH? tasyaiva viShNornirguNasya mokShadAtR^itvasambhavAt, anyeShAM tadasambhavAdityarthaH | Atmaj~nAnAnmokShopadeshespi kuto netareShAmAtmatvaM teShAmapi mokShadAtR^itvasambhavAdityata Aha - saguNA iti | turavadhAraNe | tathAcha - 'apare' viShNoranye brahmAdayo yataH 'saguNAH' sattvAdiguNabaddhA eva na svatastadvidhurAH ataH 'tajj~nAnAnnaiva' sarvathA 'muchyate' adhikArItyarthaH, guNabaddhAtmavij~nAnAt guNabandhanivR^ittirUpamokShAyAgAditi bhAvaH | nanu viShNAvapi nirguNatvenAstu mokShadAtR^itvasambhAvanA, tannishchayastu kuta ityata Aha - paro hIti | 'hi' yasmAt 'viShNuparaH' svatantraH | tattvapradIparItyA sarvottama iti vA, 'puruShaH' pUrNaH 'tasmAnmokShastato' viShNo- rbhavedeveti smR^itaH smR^ityukta ityarthaH| 'iti pAdme' ityasyApi ityupadishyata iti pUrveNAnvayaH|| 7||
(22) yuktyantareNAtmashabdAdito na gauNa ityAha sUtrakR^it - heyatveti | atra heyatvaM nAma mokShArthaM prAdhAnyena j~neyatvenAvihitatvam | tathA cha - na kevalaM tanniShThasya mokShopadeshAt, kintu "tamevaikam" iti shrutau Atmano heyatvAvachanAt, pratyuta 'jAnatha' ityaheyatvavachanAt, jIvasya cha "anyA vAcho vimuJNchatha" iti mumukShubhirheyatvavachanAchcheti sUtravR^ittimabhipretya sUtraM vyAchaShTe - tamiti | he R^iShayaH 'tam' AtmAnaM 
viShNum 'eva ekaM' pradhAnaM 'jAnatha' jAnIdhvam | 'anyAH' jIvAdiviShayiNIH 'vAchaH vimuJNchatha' tyajata, prAdhAnyena viShNvitarAn na jAnIdhvamityarthaH | 'jAnatha AtmAnam' iti vishleSho viShNoH sarvato vilakShaNatvapradarshanArthaH | vikaraNa- vyatyayastu ChAndasaH | amR^itasyetyekavachanaM samudAyavivakShayA | tathA cha - 'amR^itasya' muktavargasya 'eShaH' viShNuH setuH' mukhyAshraya ityarthaH | 'iti' ityevaMrUpAyAM muNDakashrutau 'anyeShAM' jIvAnAM 'heyatvavachanAt' ityanena chashabdasamuchcheyaM darshitam | sautranaJNo vyatyAsena anvayamabhipretya samuchcheyAntaramAha - asya viShNoraheyatveti | chashabdaH samuchchaye | sUtre gauNasUtrAdanuvR^ittasya "na gauNa AtmashabdaH" ityasyArthamAha - neti | gauNa Atma- shabdamukhyavAchyo na, kintu nirguNo viShNurevetyarthaH| tathA cha - AtmashabdAdIkShatishrutyuktospi nirguNa eveti siddham| tasyekShatyanyathAsnupapattyA vAchyatvamiti bhAvaH || 8 ||
(23) yuktyantareNApi nirguNasya viShNorvAchyatvamupapAdayatsUtramupanyasyati - svApyayAditi | sUtraM vyAchaShTe pUrNamiti | 'ado' mUlarUpaM 'pUrNam' 'idam' avatArarUpaM cha 'pUrNam' | 'pUrNam' avatArarUpaM sR^iShTikAle 'pUrNAt' mUlarUpAt 'udachyate' udgachChati | tattvapradIparItyA amuShmAdidaM saN^khyAmAtreNodachyate ekameva bahusaN^khyaM bhavati visheShAdeveti vA | pralaye mUlarUpaM 'pUrNasya' svasya 'pUrNam' avatArarUpam 'AdAya' svIkR^ityaikIbhUya 'pUrNameva' anyatrAlInaM sadeva svayam 'avashiShyate' iti bR^ihadAraNyakashrutyarthaH | 'sa' ityanyAshrutiH | tadarthastu - 'sa' viShNuH 'AtmanaH' svasmAt mUlarUpAt 'AtmAnam' avatAragataM svasvarUpaM 'uddhR^itya' sR^iShTikAle pR^ithagvyaktIkR^itya pralaye 'Atmani' svasvinneva 'vilApayati' ekIbhAvayati | 'atha' anantaraM sa viShNuH 'Atmaiva' mUlarUpyeva 'bhavati' avashiShyata iti | 'sa devaH' iti skAndasmR^itiH shrautatachChabdArthavivaraNarUpA | 'devo' dyotanAdeH 'nirguNaH' sattvAdiguNebhyo niShkrAntaH tata eva guNakAryadoShahInaH 'puruShottamaH' kSharAkSharachetanottamaH 'AdikR^it' vishvasyo- tpattikartA prathamakartA vA 'saH' shvetadvIpago 'hariH' AdisR^iShTau 'bahudhAbhUtvA' varAhAdibahurUpANi sR^iShTvA 'punaH' atha pralaye 'ekIbhUya' mUlarUpeNa tAnyekatAM prApayitvA ahipatau 'shete' yoganidrAM karotItyarthaH | itItyasya iti shrutyuktatvAchchetyadhyAhAreNa 'vAchyameva tat' iti paramasAdhyenAnvayaH |
(24) etachChrutyuktospi nirguNaH kutaH? gauNa eva kiM na syAdityastatra sautraM hetuM sAvadhAraNasvashabdAvR^ittyA yojayati - svasyaiveti || evakAro bhinnakramaH | itishabda AvR^ittostrApi yojyaH| vachanAdityAvartate | na gauNa ityanuvartate | ayamiti sheShaH | svApyayapadaM pUrNatvasyApyupalakShakam | tathA cha pUrNamiti shrutau svApyaya- padopalakShitapUrNatvasya vachanAt svasya svasminnevApyayavachanAchcha, sa iti spaShTashrutAvapi Atmanyeva vilApayIti svasya svasminnevApyayavachanAt, tasya cha nirguNahariniShThatAyAH smR^itau vachanAchcha ayaM nirguNa eva na gauNa iti yojanA | vAchyatve svApyayasya sAkShAddhetutvAbhAvAt sUtre bhAShye cha chashabdAbhAvaH | yadyapyatropalakShaNA- bhiprAyakaTIkArItyA pUrNatvahetusamuchchAyakashchashabdosnuvartanIyaH | tathAspyasya vAchyatve sAkShadahetutvAttatra hetvantarasya j~nApakachashabdo nAnuvartanIyaH | na cha
