shrutyuktatvAchchetyadhyAhR^itahetau chashabdAvashyaMbhAvAt kathaM tadabhAva iti  vAchyam, sUtrashrutahetau chashabdAbhAva ityabhiprAyAt | ata eva TIkAyAM tatretyuktam | tathA chAyaM sUtrArthaH - na kevalaM nirguNaviShNvAkhyaM brahma IkShaNIyatvAdvAchyam, kintvetachChrutyuktatvAchcha | shrutyuktaM nirguNameva na gauNamiti kutaH? purNatvAtsvasya svasminnapyayAchcha, gauNasyApUrNatvAt anyasmin layena svApyayashUnyatvAchcheti | shrutyuktasvApyaya- pUrNatvayorasiddhiparihArAya hetau sAdhyasAmAnAdhikaraNyopapAdanAya cha shrutismR^ityorvachanAdityuktaM bhAShye | nanvayaM svApyayavAn anyatrAlInashcha gauNassyAt, nirguNosnyosstIti chet - na, yadyayaM svApyayavAn gauNaH tarhyayaM nirguNashchobhau pralayesnyatra layahInau tiShThataH? uta ekasminnanyasya layo bhavati? nAdyaH "idaM vA agne naiva kiJNcha nAsIt" (tai.brA. 2-2-9-1.) ityAdishrutivirodhAt, atra pralaye dvitIyamAtraniShedhAt | dvitIye na tAvadgauNasya nirguNe layaH, tasya svApyayavattayA avasthAnAbhyupagamAt | tathA cha nirguNasya saguNe layo vAchyaH | sa cha na sambhavatItyAha - na hIti | 'gauNAtmani' jIve 'nirdoShasya' sattvAdiguNabandharUpadoShahInasya nirguNasya  viShNorlayo nopapadyata ityarthaH | hishabdena "yatprayanti" (tai.u.3-1.) ityAdishrutivirodhAditi hetuH sUchitaH | tasmAnnirguNasya svasminneva layo vAchya ityatosyamananyalIno nirguNa eveti tasyaiva shrutyuktatvAdvAchyatvaM siddhamiti bhAvaH | atra naye gauNAdivyapadeshaH sattvAdiguNayuktatvatadabhAvarUpadharmAshrayajIvaparamAtmaviShayaka eva, na tu mukhyAsambhave gauNAshrayaNA- dityatreva nirguNosyamityatreva vA mukhyArthaguNahInaviShaya iti sUchanAya nirguNasyeti vaktavyatvespi nirdoShasyetyuktam |
(25) nanvastu nirguNasya viShNorvAchyatvopapattau satyAM kAraNatvena shAstragamyatvam | tachchopakramAdibalAt prasiddhashAkhAsveva kAraNatvena pratipAdyatvaparyavasitam | aprasiddhashAkhAsu punaranyospi kAraNatvena uchyatAm | na cha tA na santi, tAsAmAnantyeneyattAsnishchayAdityata Aha - na cheti || chospyarthaH | tathA cha - 'kAsuchit' aprasiddhashAkhAsu 'anyathA' anyo nirguNAt saguNospi 'anyathA' akAraNatvAdeH kAraNatvena Atmashabda- mukhyavAchyatvena mokShajanakaj~nAnaviShayatvena cha, nirguNo vA 'anyathA' akAraNatvAdinA 'uchyate' uchyatAmiti 'na' iti yojanA | 'nAnyathA' ityanena sUtre gauNasUtrAnnetyasyAnuvR^ittiH anyathetyadhyAhArashcha sUchitaH | 'tattu sam' ityuktAdanyathA netyarthaH | kuto netyatastatra hetutvena sUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - gatIti | uttarasUtrapadAkarShaNena sarvAdhikArisAdhAraNaM gatisAmAnyasya shrutatvAditi yojanAmabhipretya asiddhiparihArAya tatsUtrasUchitAM shrutimAha - sarva iti | vedA ityasya vivaraNaM 'sarve' iti | tathA cha - 'sarve vedAH' tathA 'supramANAH' suShThu pramANaM pramANAnantaraM mUlabhUtaM yAsAM tAH 'yuktayaH' | 'tathetihAse' iti vakShyamANAnurodhAdatretihAsA apyupalakShyAH | tathA chetihAsAshcha | 'brAhmaM' brahmaikaviShayam 'ekam' ekavidhameva ramArthaviShayakatvAt 'paramam' uttamaM 'j~nAnaM' 'prakAshyante' utpAdayanti, na punaranekam | ataH 'sarveShu vedeShu' tathA yuktiShu 'tathetihAse' itihAseShu 'kutashchit' kashchidapi viShayakR^ito vA prakArakR^ito vA 'virodho na' ityarthaH j~nAnarUpamekameva brahmasvarUpaM 
j~nApayantIti vA | shruteriti paJNchamI tR^itIyArthe | gaterityasya vyAkhyA j~nAnasyeti | sAmAnyAditi sautrapade prAtipadikArthamAha - sAmyamiti | viShayaguNAnAmananyathoktyA sAmyamityarthaH | "na hyekatra j~nAnAnandAdikamuktvAsnyatrAj~nAnAdirUpatvaM brahmaNa uchyate" iti tattvapradIpokteH kathyata iti sheShaH | na tu viShamatvamiti vA svayameva sAkShAnna tvanyamukheneti vA evashabdArthaH | tathA cha - 'sarve vedA' iti shrutyA svayameva sAkShAdgateH sarvashAkhotpAdyaj~nAnasya sAmAnyAt ekavidhatvokteH na kAsuchichChAkhAsu anyathochyata iti sUtrArthaH | atra bhinnaviShayaprakArakeShvapi j~nAneShu j~nAnatvena sAmyasattvAtsAmyAdityuktau viShayaprakAraikyaM na siddhyatIti sAmAnyAt samAnatvAt ekavidhatvAt ityuktaM sUtre | bhAShyapadasyApyayamevArtha eti dhyeyam || 10 ||
(26) itashcha nirguNaM brahma vAchyamityAha sUtrakR^it - shrutatvAchcheti| cho hetusamuchchaye | tadashabdaM neti vartate| tathA cha tadviShNvAkhyaM nirguNaM na kevalamIkShatyAdibhiH nAshabdaM shabdavAchyam | kintu "ekaH" iti shvetAshvatarashrutau 'shrutatvAchcha' svavAchakanAmnA sAkShAduktatvAchchetyartha ityAshayena sUtropAttashrutiM paThati - eka iti | 'ekaH' pradhAnaH svasmin bhedashUnya iti vA 'devo' dyotanAdeH 'sarvabhUteShu gUDhaH' sarvaprANiShu guptatayAsvasthitaH | na kevalaM bhUteShu sthitaH kintu 'sarvavyApI' cha deshataH kAlato guNatashcha sarvaM vyApnotItyarthaH | na kevalaM sarvabhUteShu sthitimAtraM, kintu 'sarvabhUtAntarAtmA' sarvaprANinAM antaHsthitvA A samyak tanniyantA cha mAtA cheti vA | AdAnAdikartR^itvAdvA tathoktaH | 'karmAdhyakShaH' karmAdhipatiH, "karmopari asyAkShANIndriyANi vartanta ityadhyakShaH" iti tattvapradIpokteH | 'sarvabhUtAdhivAsaH' sarvaprANi- nAmAshrayaH | sarvaM sAkShAdIkShate pashyatIti 'sAkShI' | IkShaNaM cha na prAkR^itaM kintu chaitanyasvarUpamityAha - 'chetA' j~nAnarUpa iti | 'kevalo' jaDAmishraH samAbhyadhikashUnya iti vA "kevalaM tAdR^ishAbhAvAt" iti dvitIyatAtparyokteH | kevalaM chaitanyenekShaNamasaMpraj~nAtasamAdhisthasya yoginospi bhavatIti tadvyA- vartanAyAha 'nirguNa' iti sattvAdiguNabandhahIna ityarthaH, prAkR^itaguNahIna iti vA | itishabdasya 'shrutau nirguNasya' iti padadvayAdhyAhAreNa shrutatvAditi sUtreNAnvayaH | "atra vAchyatvaM pratipAdayatsUtraM tadupAttashrutyudAharaNapUrvakaM paThati - eka iti" iti kvachitkaTIkApAThAnusAreNa bhAShye kvachit shrutipAThAnantaraM sUtrapATho dR^ishyate | tatpakShe tvanvayassulabha eveti dhyeyam | shrutatvespyashabdaH kiM na syAdityaprayojakatvashaN^kAyAmAha - na hIti | 'hi' yataH 'ashabdaH' avAchyaH padArtho 'na shrUyate' na shrutipadenochyata ityarthaH | ato nAprayojakatvaM hetoriti vAkyasheShaH | virodhAdityapi hishabdArthaH | nanu ashabdasyApi brahmaNo lakShaNayA shrutatvaM kiM na syAdityata Aha - na cheti | 'aprasiddham' avAchyasya brahmaNo lakShyatvaM na kalpyamityarthaH | kutaH? yatosvAchyasya vastuno lakShyatvamaprasiddham ata iti vyAptiparatvenApIdaM yojanIyam | nanu 
kathametat? gaN^gApadAvAchyasyApi tIrasya tatpadalakShyatva- prasiddherityata uktaM - sarveti | 'sarvashabdAvAchyasya' brahmaNo lakShaNAyAH vedapadalakShyatvasyAyukteH vipratipannaM na lakShyaM, kenApi padenAvAchyatvAt vyatirekeNa tIravaditi yuktiviruddhatvAdityarthaH | tathA cha - nAsmAbhiH kevalAvAchyatvena lakShyatvAbhAvaH sAdhyate yena tIrAdau vyabhichAraH shaN^kayeta, kintu sarvashabdAvAchyatvena | tachcha na tIrAdigataM, tasya tIrAdipadavAchyatvAt | brahma tu na tathA, tasya sarvashabdAvAchyatayaiva pareNAN^gIkR^itatvAt | ato na vyabhichAra iti yuktivirodho duShparihara iti bhAvaH | nanu lakShyatvAbhAvavati pravAhAdau hetvabhAvAdasAdhAraNamiti chet - na, lakShaNAyogyasyaiva lakShyapadArthatve sarvapadArthAnAmapi kiJNchitpadalakShaNAyogyatvena tadabhAvarUpasAdhyasya kutrApyabhAvena sapakShasyaivAbhAvAt || 11 ||
|| iti IkShatyadhikaraNam ||
|| 6. AnandamayAdhikaraNam ||
(1) athAdhyAyapAdayorupodghAtatvena pITharUpAyAmasyAM paJNchAdhikaraNyaM brahmasvarUpanarUpaNe anavasheShAtkimadhyAyAtmakasheShagranthenetyata Aha - tameveti || tathAspItyAdau yojyam | samanvayashabdashcha vipariNAmenAvartanIyaH | tathA cha - tathAspi prakaTanaM vinAsdhyAyAkhyasheShagranthasya kR^ityAntarAbhAvespi 'tameva' "tattu samanvayAt" ityanena hetutayA sAmAnyataH siddhavadupanyastameva samanvayAt 'samanvayam' upakramAdiliN^gaj~nApyaM samyagvachanavR^ittyA sarvashAstrIyavachanAnAM harau nirUpaNaM tatparatvaM 'prakaTayati' prativAkyagrahaNena taddhetUpanyAsAdinA prapaJNchayati "AnandamayosbhyAsAt" ityAdinA anena prathamenA- dhyAyena sUtrakAra ityarthaH | anyathA pratij~nAmAtrasya "tadeva shAstrayoni, samanvayAt" iti siddhavadupanyAsamAtrasya sAdhakatve "viShNoranyadeva shAstrayoni, kutaH? samanvayAt samyaktAtparyaviShayatvAt, tathA anyadeva tAtparyaviShayaH, kutaH? upakramAdiliN^gAt" ityapi prativAdI brUyAditi bhAvaH | yathopakramAdikaM tajj~nApyaM tAtparyaM cha samanvayashabdArthaH tathA bhAShyaM yojitam adhastAt | yadyapyatra sUtrasya pratIkatvena uttaratra udAhariShyamANatvAnnAtrApyudAhartavyatA | tathAspi sUtrAnudAharaNe AnandamayAkhya- viShayAparij~nAnAttasya viShNutvasamarthane kA pUrvasaN^gatirityevaM shaN^kAsnudayAt  tanmUlaprashnAnudayAt AnandamayA- parij~nAne brahmaNastadavayavatvapratItimukhenAkSheparUpashaN^kAnudayAchcha etadAkSheparUpasaN^gatipradarshanAya 
cha adhikaraNa- saN^gativiShayakashaN^kotthApanAya atrApi sUtrodAharaNaM, uttaratra tu pratIkatveneti draShTavyam | adhyAyAntaravyAvR^ittyartha- mAnandamayetyAdi | prathamenetyanukttvA evaMvachanena etadadhikaraNamArabhyAdhyAyArambhaH, paJNchAdhikaraNyAstu nAdhyAyAntarbhAva ityapi sUchitam | samanvayAdhikaraNamArabhyaivAdhyAyArambhaH tasyaitatprapaJNchatvAditi pakShe adhyAyena adhyAyasheSheNetyartha ityavirodhaH | chaturthapAde na samanvayaH kriyata iti paramatanirAsAya 'samastena' samagreNetyuktam | devatApashUdrAdhikaraNayoH samanvayAkaraNAt samastenetyanupapannamityAshaN^kAnirAkaraNAya 'prAyeNa' prAchuryeNeti | prAya iti sakArAntAvyayaparyAyosyamakArAntaH prAyashabdaH | tasmAtprakR^ityAditvAttR^itIyAyAM prAyeNeti bhavati | ata eva viShNutattvanirNayaTIkAyAM bhUmArthe 'prAyaH' ityavyayamapyasti ityapishabdaH prAyoji | prameyadIpespi sAntasyai- vAvyayatvamuktam |
(2) tarhi adhyAyasyaikArthatvAt pAdabhedaH kiM nibandhana ityataH samanvetavyabhedAt samanvayespyavAntarabheda iti bhAvena prathamAdhyAprathamapAdapratipAdyaM darshayati - prAyeNeti || 'asmin' prathame pAde 'prAyeNa' bAhulyena 'anyatra' viShNoranyatra 'prasiddhAnAM' shrutyAdito lokato vAsspAtato rUDhatvena pratIyamAnAnAM nAmAtmakAnAM 'shabdAnAM' 'paramAtmani' viShNau niruktaH 'samanvayaH' 'pradarshyate' prapaJNchyata ityarthaH | atrApi antaradhikaraNe antaHsthatva- liN^gasamanvayapratipAdanAt avyAptinirAsAya - prAyeNeti | tattvapradIpe tu eka eva bhAShye prAyeNeti shabdaH | tasyaivottaratrApi sambandha ityAshayena "prAyeNAnyatra prasiddhAnAM shabdAnAmiti cha sambandhaH" ityuktam | tathA - AnandamayAdhikaraNe liN^gavichArattadapi prAyeNeti vyAvartyamiti choktam | yadvA - TIkAyAmapyAvR^ittyabhiprAyeNaikasyaiva punaruttaratrApi anvayapradarshanAya pratIkagrahaNaM kR^itamiti na granthavairUpyaM kalpyam | ata eva tattvapradIpAnusAreNa "AnandamayanAmnaH iti TIkAyAmAnandamayanAmashbadaH AnandAdinAmaparo vA yojyaH" ityuktaM chandrikAyAm | atha paroktaM pAdArthaM dUShayati - neti | 'anyathA' prathame spaShTabrahmaliN^gAnAM shabdAnAM dvitIyatR^itIyayoraspaShTabrahmaliN^gAnAM samanvayaH pratipAdyate | tayostu savisheShanirvisheShaviShayatayA bhedaH | chaturthapAde tu pradhAnasyAshAbdatvoktirityevaM rUpossmaduktAdanyaprakAreNa pAdArtho na vAchyaH ityarthaH | kuto netyata Aha - taditi | 'tasya' paroktapAdArtha- niyamasya 'adR^iShTeH' etadadhyAyagatapAdeShvadarshanAdityarthaH | sarvasAN^karyAditi bhAvaH | tachcha TIkAdAvuktam |
(3) nanvAnandamayAdhikaraNamArabhya sarveShAmadhikaraNAnAmavashyavaktavye saN^gatipaJNchake asminnadhikaraNe loka- tosnyatraprasiddhAnandamayashabdopalakShitaguNivAchishabdAnAmAnandAdiguNavAchishabdAnAM cha brahmaNi samanvayakaraNAt asyAstu shAstresdhyAye pAde chAntarbhAvarUpA saN^gatiH | tathAspi Anandamayasya viShNutvasamarthane kA pUrvasaN^gatirityatosvyavahitapUrvAdhikaraNenaiva saN^gatirvaktavyeti niyamAbhAvAt 
vyavahitapUrveNa jij~nAsAdhikaraNena tadviShayeNa cha asyAnantaryalakShaNalakShitAmAkShepikIM saN^gatiM tAvaddarshayati - brahmeti || uktaM jij~nAsAdhikaraNe iti sheShaH | 'tachcheti' | yajjij~nAsyatayA pratij~nAtaM brahma tadevetyarthaH | yadvA - prakR^itAnusandhAnArthashchashabdaH | itItya- nantaraM 'shrutau' iti sheShaH | 'AnandamayAvayavarUpamiti' AnandamayAkhyasya kasyachitpuchChAkhyAvayavabhUtaM pratIyata ityarthaH| nanu brahmaNosvayavatvoktAvapi kimarthamAnandamayasya viShNutvasamarthanamityata Aha - na hIti| hishabdo hetau| 'ata' ityAvartate | 'tachcha' ityAdi 'ityata Aha' ityantaM saN^gatiprayojanobhayaparatayA vyAkhyeyam | na hItyeta- ttadupapAdakam | yojanA tu - yato 'brahma puchChaM pratiShThA' iti shrutau jij~nAsyatayoktaM brahma AnandamayAkhyasya kasyachidavayavarUpaM 'pratIyate' uchyate yatashcha anyAN^gatayA jij~nAsyatvespi 'avayavinam' AnandamayaM vinA 'avayavamAtrasya' avayavasyaiva kevalasya brahmaNo na pR^ithak 'j~neyatA' jij~nAsyatA sambhavati | amukhyatvAt | nApi jij~nAsAyA eva tyAgo yujyate | "tadvijij~nAsasva" (tai. u. 3-1.) iti shrutivihitatvAdityevaM shaN^kA prAptA | ataH shaN^kArUpasaN^gatisadbhAvAt atrAnandamayasya viShNvanyatvapakShe brahmajij~nAsAkShepAt viShNutvapakShe cha tatsamAdhA- nAt evaM cha pUrvapakShasiddhAntayoH phalasadbhAvAchcha 'ato' brahmajij~nAsAsiddhyartham 'AnandamayosbhyAsAt' ityAnanda- mayasya viShNutvam 'Aha' samarthayati sUtrakAra iti |
"tasmAdvA etasmAdvij~nAnamayAt | anyosntara AtmAnandamayaH | tenaiSha pUrNaH | sa vA eSha puruShavidha eva | tasya puruShavidhatAm | anvayaM puruShavidhaH | tasya priyameva shiraH | modo dakShiNaH pakShaH | pramoda uttaraH pakShaH | Ananda AtmA | brahma puchChaM pratiShThA" (tai.u. 2-5-2.) iti taittirIyavAkyasyAyamarthaH | 'tasmAt' Atmapado- ditAt 'etasmAt' jIvasharIragatAt vij~nAnapUrNatvAt vij~nAnamayashabdavAchyAt viShNoH ananyospyanyashabdoktaH 'AnandamayaH' AnandapUrNatvAdAnandamayashabdavAchyaH 'AtmA' nArAyaNaH 'antaro' vij~nAnamayasyAntaHsthitaH 'tena' Anandamayena 'eShaH' vij~nAnamayashabdavAchyo vAsudevaH 'pUrNaH' nishChidratvena pUritaH | vaishabdaH prasiddhau | 'sa eSha' AnandamayaH 'puruShavidha eva' puruShAkAra eva | 'tasya' Anandamayasya sharIrasthAnIyasya puruShAkAratAm 'anu' anusR^itya 'ayaM' vij~nAnamayaH sharIrasthAnIyaH 'puruShavidhaH' tasmAtprAdurbhUtaH,
uttaraiH pUritAH pUrve nishChidratvena sarvashaH |
sarvespi puruShAkArA uttarAtpUrvasambhavaH ||
iti taittirIyabhAShyokteH | 'tasya' Anandamayasya viShNoH avayavabhUtaM 'pareyaM priyanAmakam' iti bhAShyokteH | parairuttamaiH devaiH prApyatvAtpriyashabdavAchyaM yatsukhaM tattasya 'shiraH' tadevAnandamayAkhyasya jIvasharIrasya parairanyairupa- kartR^ibhiH prApyatvAt priyanAmakamupakArajanyavaiShayikasukhAkhyaM yachChiraH tatsthaM cha | evamAnandamayAkhyasya viShNoH ye dakShiNottarabAhumadhyadehAH modapramodakAritvAnandatvanimittairmoda- 
pramodAnandanAmAnaH te AnandamayAkhyajIvasharIrasya dakShiNottarapakShAtmanAmAno dakShiNasavyabAhumadhyadehAH| 'modo' bhoganimittakaH 'pramodaH' "tadvisheShotthaH" ityaitareya- bhAShyokteH | 
munnAma viShayotthaM yatprakR^iShTaviShayAtpramut |
sukhaM svarUpabhUtaM yadAnanda iti kathyate ||
iti bR^ihadbhAShyokteshcha | apakR^iShTaviShayodbhUtatvaprakR^iShTaviShayotthatvajIvasvarUpAnandatvanimittairmodapramodAnandanAmAna- steShu sthitAshcha | evamAnandamayAkhyasya viShNoH 'puchChaM' pratiShThati gachChati loka AbhyAmiti vyutpattyA pratiShThApadokto yaH pAdAkhyosvayavaH tadbrahma 'brahmasR^iShTyA tu bR^iMhayet' iti taittirIyabhAShyoktarItyA sR^iShTyAdikriyayA vishvaguNavR^iddhikaratvAdbrahmashabdavAchyaH sa evAnandamayAkhyajIvasharIrasya yat puchChaM yaH pAdAkhyosvayavaH tatsthite brahmAkhye pradhAnavAyau sthitaH | anena koshAvayavasya brahmashabdavAchyatvaM brahmashabdavAchyapradhAnavAyvadhiShThAnatvanimittaM, pradhAnavAyorbrahmashabdavAchyatvaM tu parabrahmAdhiShThAnatvAdityuktaM bhavati | anenAnandamayAdishabdavAchyasya viShNoravayava- bhUtAH ye priyAdayaH te viShNvabhinnAH ye chAnandamayAdijIvakoshAvayavAH priyAdayaste pratisharIraM bhinnA iti dvividhAH priyAdaya ityuktaM bhavati | yathoktaM chandrikAyAm - ye jIvAbhimanyamAnAnandamayAdikoshAvayavAH priyAdayaste pratisharIraM bhinnAH, na te AnandamayAdyAkhyasya viShNoravayavAH | ye cha bhagavatosvayavAH priyAdayo na te pratisharIraM bhinnA kintvabhinnA iti jIvasvarUpasyAnandasya hR^idayAkhyamadhyagatatvAtkoshamadhyadehatvaM svarUpadehasya jaDAvayavatvaM chAmukhyaM yujyate | yadyapi bhAShye 'shiro nArAyaNaH' ityudAhariShyamANavachanaparyAlochanayAssnandamayAkhyo nArAyaNaH punarnArAyaNAdirUpeNa paJNchadhA bhinnaH shiraHprabhR^ityavayavAtmanA tiShThatIti pratIyate | taittirIyabhAShye tu - priyAdInAmanandamayAvayavatvam | tathApi priyAdisukhavisheShadehasthitabrahmAkhyapradhAnavAyugatAnAM nArAyaNAdirUpANAmeva AnandamayAkhyaviShNvavayavatvasambhavAtteShAmeva |
pareyaM priyanAmakam |
modapramodanAmAnau modanAchcha pramodanAt |
dehasthavAyusaMsthaM cha brahma sR^iShTyA tu bR^iMhayet || iti |
taittirIyabhAShyoktarItyA priyAdishabdavAchyatvasyApi sambhavAnna virodhaH | tattvapradIpe tu - priyashirastvAdinaye "shravaNotthaM priyaM, darshanottho modaH, bhogotthaH pramodaH" iti padatrayasyArthAntaramuktam | tathA tatraiva "'abhAvaM bAdariH' iti sUtreNa 'priyApriye' (ChAM. 8-12-1.) iti shrutisthapriyashabdena 'pareyaM priyanAmakam'  iti taittirIyaChAndogyabhAShyayoruktatvAtparaprApyasukhasAmAnyavAchakena prAkR^itaM sukhaM grAhyamiti sUchitam" iti choktam | idaM tvavadhayam - paridR^ishyamAnamannamayaM sharIram | tadantaH prANamayo 
dehaH tadantarmanomayo dehaH | tadantarvij~nAnamayo dehaH | tadantarAnandamoyassti | eteShu paJNchasu dehAkhyakosheShu tattachChabdavAchyAni puruShAkArANi aniruddhapradyumnasaN^karShaNa- vAsudevanArAyaNarUpANi dehadehibhAvena vartanta iti |
(4) evaM saN^gatiM phalaM choktvA viShayasaMshayau darshayati - Anandamaya iti || Anandamaya ityupalakShakapadena viShayo darshitaH | brahmAdirityatra brahmA Adiryasya jIvasaN^ghasyeti vigrahaH | brahmA chaturmukhaH, Adishabdena rudrendra- bR^ihaspatimukhA devAstattaddehAgatajIvAshcha gR^ihyante | prakR^itishabdena chitprakR^itiH | 'iti saMshaya' iti sheShaH |
(5) atra sayuktikaM pUrvapakShAnAha - brahmashabdAditi || AnandamayamadhikR^ityadAhR^ite 'asti brahmeti chedveda' (tai.u. 2-6-1.) ityAdau shrutAdbrahmashabdAdityarthaH | brahmashabdasya anyatrApi vR^itteH kathaM tena chaturmukhasyAnanda- mayatvanishcha ityato yuktyantaramAha - shateti | chospyarthe samuchchaye | "te ye shataM prajApaterAnandAH, sa eko brahmaNa AnandaH" (tai.u. 2-8-4.) iti vAkyAdarthAtsUchitena shatAnandanAmnetyarthaH | yadvA - AnandamayashabdasamAnArthakena hiraNyagarbhe vidyamAnena shatAnandanAmnetyarthaH|  'prAptiH' Anandamayatvasyeti sheShaH | tathA cha - hiraNyagarbhasya Anandamayatvasya prAptirityanvayaH |
(6) evamekaM pUrvapakShamabhidhAya anyamAha - aShTamUrtitvAditi || chashabdo rudrasya cheti sambadhyate | prAptirityasyAnukarShaNArtho vA tathA cha - rudrasya chAnandamayatvaprAptiH kutaH? sUrye proktatvAt | 'yashchAsAvAditye' (tai.u. 2-8-5.) ityAnandamayasya sUrye sthiteH uktatvAdrudrasya cha sUryAdyaShTasharIratvA- dityarthaH | tathA cha - rUdra- liN^gasya Anandamaye shrutatvAt Anandamayo rudra evepi bhAvaH | rudrasya sUryAdyaShTapratimatvaM cha -
sUryo jalaM mahI vahnirvAyurAkAsha eva cha |
dIkShito brAhmaNassoma ityetAstanavaH kramAt ||
iti viShNupurANavAkyAtsiddham |
(7) pUrvapakShAntaraM darshayati - evamiti || uktAbhyAm 'anyeShAm' indrabR^ihaspatyAdInAmapi 'evam' uktaprakAreNa svAvarasUryAdyadhiShThAtR^itvAdinA AnandamayatvaprAptirityarthaH |
(8) sayuktikaM pUrvapakShAntaramAha - mameti | yojanA tu chitprakR^itervAsnandamayatvaprAptiH | kutaH? brahmashabdAt| Anandamaye shrutasya brahmashabdasya 'mama yonirmahadbrahma tasmin garbhaM dadhAmyaham' iti gItAyAM chitprakR^itau prayogAditi| smR^itau - mahat brahmeti bhinne pade | tathA cha mahat brahmashabdavAchyA lakShmIH mama yoniH garbhAdhAnArthaM bhAryA | tasmin brahmaNi prakR^itau ahaM garbhaM dadhAmi dadha ityarthaH | arjunaM prati 
kR^iShNavAkyametat | kathaM sAvakAshena brahmashabdena prakR^iterAnandamayatvanishchaya ityato hetvantaramAha - 'bahubhAvAt' bahurUpatvAchcheti | cho hetusamuchchaye | tathA cha 'soskAmayata | bahu syAm' (tai.u. 2-6-2.) ityAnandamayasya 'bahubhAvAt' bahubhAvashravaNAt tadabhimAnitvAchchi- tprakR^iteH svAbhimanyamAnavikArijaDadvArA bahubhAvasambhavAdityarthaH | evaM prakR^iterityasya jaDaprakR^iterityarthAshrayeNa pUrvapakShAntaramapi draShTavyam | yojanA tu jaDaprakR^itervAssnandamayatvaprAptiH | kutaH? abhimAnitvena vinA sAkShAdbahu- bhAvAdeveti |
(9) sayuktikaM pUrvapakShAntaramAha - bR^iha jAtIti | tattaddehagatasarvajIvAnAM vA AnandamayatvaprAptiH | kutaH? jIvAnAM brahmashabdAt | jIvavAchibrahmashabdAdityarthaH | na tatra pR^ithaghgheturgaveShaNIya ityevashabdArthaH | kuto brahmashabdasya jIvavAchitvamityata uktam - bR^iha jAtIti | bR^ihadhAtuH jAtyAdiShu vartata ityarthaH | itItyanantaraM dhAtuvyAkhyAnAditi sheShaH | brahmashabdasya sAdhAraNatvAdanishchAyakatvamityata Aha - annamayatvAdeshcheti | idaM chAvartate, tatra dvitIyo vipariNamyate | Adishabdo bhinnakramaH | tena prANAdikaM gR^ihyate | yathAkramashcha chashabda uktAnuktahetusamuchchaye | tathA cha - na kevalaM brahmashabdAt, kintu, yato jIvAnAm 'annarasamayaH' 'prANamayaH' ityuktAnnAdimayatvAt annAdivikAra- dehAdyabhimAnitvAdannamayatvAdi prAptam atastatprAyapaThitatvAchchAnandamayatvaprAptiriti yojanA | atra hiraNyagarbhAdInAM jIvatvespi devatvavivakShayA pR^ithaguktiH | ata eva tattvapradIpe - "brahmAdiryasya devatAsaN^ghasya" ityapi brahmAdirityasya vigraho darshitaH | tatrApi hiraNyagarbharudrayoratiprasiddhatvAdvakShyamANakrameNa pR^ithaguktiH | atha indrAdInAM "brahmA shivaH sureshAdyAH" iti vachanoktakrameNa kSharadevoktyanantaramakSharAyAH prakR^iteruktiH | atha atyalpapratibhA- natvAt dR^ishyamAnadehAbhimAnijIvAnAmiti dhyeyam |
(10) siddhAntayati - tathApIti || yadyapyevamanyeShAM prAptiH, tathApi atra ye Anandamayashabdenochyante na te hiraNyagarbhAdaya ityarthaH | kastarhItyAshaN^kate - kintviti | uttaramAha - viShNureveti | ya uchyate sa viShNurevetyanvayaH | anenodAhR^itAnandamaya iti sUtrapratij~nAbhAgasya saN^gatyarthamanvayArthaM samanvayasUtrodAhR^ito vidheyasamarpakaH 'tattu' iti pratij~nAbhAgo vyAkhyAto bhavati | kuta Anandamayo viShNurevetyataH pravR^ittaM sautraM hetuM vyAchaShTe - tadeveti | ityAdiShu vAkyeShu tasminviShNAveva prasiddhasya mukhyArthatvenoktasya brahmashabdasya tasminnAnandamaye AnandamayaM pratyudAhR^ite 'asanneva' iti shloke 'abhyAsAt' asakR^ichChravaNAdityarthaH | abhyAsAdityanantaraM 'viShNau tAtparyAvagamAt' iti sheShaH | aprayojakatvashaN^kAvAraNAya brahmashabdasyAnyatra niravakAshatvaj~nApanAya tasmin prasiddheti eveti choktam| Adishabdena 'paramaM yo mahadbrahma' 'vAsudevAtparaH 
ko nu brahmashabdodito bhavet' iti vAkyaM gR^ihyate | tadeveti shrutyarthastu jij~nAsAnayesbhihitaH | 'etameva' iti shrutyarthaH sarvatrAdhikaraNe vakShyate |
(11) 'brahmashabdaH' iti smR^itau 'pare' pUrNe iti hetugarbhavisheShaNam | vAshabdosvadhAraNe | tathA cha yato viShNuH paraH, ataH 'pare' viShNAveva brahmashabdo mukhyatayA 'iShyate' aN^gIkriyate prAmANikaiH | na tu viShNoH 'anyatra' hiraNyagarbhAdiShvapItyarthaH | kuta ityatasteShAM brahmashabdamukhyArthatvAbhAve hetumAha - 'pare' anye yasmAda- sampUrNA iti | tarhi 'tasmAdetadbrahma nAma rUpamannaM cha jAyate' (mu. 1-1-9.) 'dve brahmaNI veditavye' (maitri.u. 6-22.) 'brahmANi jIvAH sarvespi' ityAdau brahmashabdasteShu kathamiShyata ityata Aha - kvachidanyatreShTospi brahmashabdaH 'upachAreNa' paramamukhyavR^ittyanyamukhyavR^ittyaiva bhavediti | 'brahma' iti bhAgavata- smR^ityarthaH | prAgevoktaH | madhye AtmapadopetasAdhAraNasmR^ityupAdAnanimittaM tu abhyAsAdityasya 'anyontara AtmA' (tai. u. 2-2-1.) ityAdau brahma- vAchakAtmashabdAbhyAsAdityapyartho varNanIya iti j~nApanamityuktaM chandrikAyAm | 'vAsudevAtmakam' iti vyAsasmR^itivAkyaM tu 'buddhyAsvihiMsan puShpairvA praNavena samarchayet' iti pUrvavAkyena saha yojanIyam | atra hi vAsudevAtmakaM brahmetyAderbhagavAn brahmeti pratIyate iti nyAyadIpokteH | 'yatiH' 'vAsudevAtmakaM' kR^iShNAkhyaM brahma 'buddhyA' manasA samarchayedityanena yatInAM mAnasapUjochyate puShpAdyairvA samarchayet ityanena kAyikapUjA | 'avihiMsan' kasyAspi hiMsAM hAnimakurvanniti teShAM sAmAnyadharmoktiH | anena yatInAM vaiShNavatvaprayuktAt tulasIpuShpAdyAharaNarUpAdvaisheShikAddharmAdahiMsAlakShaNaH sAmAnyadharma eva balavAnityuktaM bhavati | yathoktaM bR^ihadbhAShye - 'sAmAnyadharmo balavAn dharmAdvaisheShikAdyataH' iti | 'praNavena' oN^kAreNa 'mUlamantreNa' aShTAkShareNa vA samarchayedityanena vAchikapUjochyate iti j~nAtavyam |
(12) uktamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtraM paThitvAsskShepAMshaM vyAchaShTe - vikAreti || atra cho hetusamuchchaye | prakR^itishabdena chidachitprakR^itI gR^ihyete | Adishabdena jIvA gR^ihyante | prakR^ityAdaya iti cha vipariNamyate | naJN Avartate | Anandamaya ityasti, kiM tu viShNuriti cha | tushabdo visheShArthosvadhAraNArthe cha | tathA cha - Anandamayo na viShNuH, kintu, prakR^ityAdaya eva | kutaH? yatostra 'vikArashabdo' vikArArthakamayaTChabdo 'yujyate' prayujyate | sa cha yato vikAratadabhimAnitvAbhyAmeva 'yujyate' pravartate | ataH prakR^ityAdInAmeva yujyate | kutaH? jaDaprakR^itervikArAtmakatvAchchetanaprakR^ityAdInAM cha vikArAbhimAnitvAt | na tu paramAtmanaH, tasyAvikAritvA- danabhimAnitvAchcheti yojanA | 'iti chenna' ityaMshaM vyAchaShTe - iti mAbhUditi | shaN^keti sheShaH | kuta ityataH pravR^ittaM sautraM hetuM vyAchaShTe - prachureti | AnandamayaH kathyata iti sheShaH | hishabdo hetau 
| tushabdosvadhAraNArthaH | tathA cha 'hi' yataH 'AnandamayaH' padArthaH 'prachurAnandatvAt' pUrNAnandatvAchcha nimittAdevAnandamayapadena kathyate 'na tadvikAratvAt' AnandavikAratvAdata iti shaN^kA mAbhUditi yojanA | mayaTChabdasya prAchuryarUpArthAntaramapekShya pravR^ittatvena tadvirodhAbhAvAditi bhAvaH mayaDityAkhyapratyayasya prAchuryArthatvaM cha 'tAdAtmyArthe vikArArthe prAchuryArthe mayaT tridhA' iti vachanAtsiddhamityapi herarthaH | yadyapi shrutisUtragatAnandamaya iti vyAkhyeyapadasya taddhitAntasyArthakathanAya tadanukUlatayA AnandaH prachuro yasmin sa AnandaprachuraH iti samAsaH kAryo na tadviparItaH prachura Anandossmin sa prachurAnanda iti | tathAspyAndamaya iti taddhitavR^ittyananuguNAnandaprachuraiti samAsavAkyAbhidhAne brAhmaNaprachuro grAma itivat AnAnandasyApi prAptestadvAraNAya prachurAnanda iti viparItasamAsaH kR^itaH | kechittu - sUtre prAchuryAdityukta- tvAdAnandasyetyarthalabdhaM, tathA chaitadvAkyAnusAreNAnandaprachuratvAditi samAsavAkyaprayogaH kAryo yadyapi, tathAspi uktaprayojanAbhiprAyeNa prachurAnandatvAditi sautravyAsavAkyaviparItasamAsaH kR^ita ityAhuH | tanna, "Anandaprachura iti yathAsthitAbhidhAne" ityAdiTIkAvirodhAt | yadyapyAnandamaya iti shrutisUtrAnusAreNa prAchuryasya visheShyatvenoktAvapi nAnAnandaprAptiHSha prAkAshaprachuro ravirityuktespi savitaryandhakAraleshApratIteH | tathA chAnandaprachuratvAdityeva vyAkhyAtumuchitam | prAchuryasya vyadhikaraNasajAtIyajaivAnandAlpatvenApi nirUpayituM shakyatvAt | tathApi prAchuryasya visheShaNatAyA- manAnandAprApteH parairapi svIkR^itatvAt visheShyatAyAM tu tasya samAnAdhikaraNavijAtIyAlpatva- nirUpyatvAt brAhmaNaprachuro grAma ityAdAviva tatprAptirevetyaN^gIkR^itatvAdubhayavAdisiddhyanusAreNaiva vyAkhyAtavyatvAt tadabhiprAyeNa prachurAnandatvAditi vyAkhyAtaM bhAShye ityuktaM chandrikAyAm |
(13) nanu nAyamAnandamayashabdaH prachurAnandatAmabhidhatte | kintu vikArArthatvameva | annAdivikArArthAnna- mayAdishabdaissaha paThitatvAdityata Aha - annAdInAM cheti ||  idaM chAvartate | mayaTChabda iti chAnuvartate | tena samuchchayArtha chashabdasyAnvayaH | vAchyavAchakayorabhedavyapadeshaH | tathA cha na kevalamAnandasya mayaTChabdaH, kintvannA- dInAM sambandhimayaTChabdospi annAdInAM prAchuryameva vaktItyarthaH | evashabdo vikArArthatAvyAvR^ittyarthaH | Adishabdena prANAdayo gR^ihyante | pUrvam 'annamayatvAdeshcha' iti, atra cha 'annAdInAm' iti bahUnAM grahaNAt, sautrAnandamaya- shabdosjahatsvArthalakShaNayA samAnanyAyashabdAntaropalakShaka iti sUchitam | nanu kathamatrAnnamayashabdosnnaprAchuryArthaH | auShadhijanitAnnaprAchuryasya annopajIviShu pArthivasharIreShu sambhavespi aprAkR^itavigrahe harau asambhavAt | annaprAchuryakathanasyAtyalpatvApAdakatvAchchetyata Aha - adyata iti | 'vAkyena annashabdasya' iti sheShaH | 'yujyate' ityanantaram 'annamayashabdArthaH' ityadhyAhAraH | 'paramAtmanaH' ityasti | na kevalaM sahapAThavirodhAbhAva iti chArthaH| tathA chetthaM yojanA - 'tatprAchuryam' annaprAchuryamannamayashabdArtho yujyate | kathaM?  yatastatparamAtmano yajyate | na chAlpArthatvena mAhAtmyarUpatvAbhAvAtsa kathaM harau yujyata iti 
vAchyam | yatostrAnnashabdena sudhoktarItyA bhAvapradhAnena tattadbhUtAdyatvabhUtAttR^itvarUpArthadvayameva yujyate, uchyate na prasiddhAnnam | ku etajj~nAyate | "adyatestti cha bhUtAni | tasmAdannaM taduchyata iti" vAkyenAnnashabdasya vyAkhyAnAt | prasiddhAnnasya bhUtAttR^itvAyogena tadgrahaNAsambhavAditi | shrutyarthastu - yato bhUtaiH prANibhiH 'adyate' upajIvyate 'bhUtAnyatti' saMharati cha | tasmAttadviShNvAkhyaM brahmAnnamuchyate vedeShviti | evaM prANamanashshabdayoH prakR^iShTacheShTakatvapUrNAvabodhArthatvena shvAsavAyvantaHkaraNabuddhiprAchuryArthatAyAmalpA- rthatA pariharaNIyA ||
(14) nanu tathApi prachurabhUtAdyatvaM kathamabhisaMhitaM brahmaNaH, bhakShyatvarUpAdyatvasya tatrAyogAdityatos- dyatvashabdArtamAha - upajIvyatvamiti || atra 'atosdyate' ityanuvyAkhyAnAnusAreNAdyatvamiti ChedaH | tathA cha sudho- ktarItyA gauNyA vR^ittyA upajIvyatvamevAdyatvaM vivakShitaM, na tu charvyatvam | tachcha brahmaNyaviruddhamiti bhAvaH | tattvapradIpe tu - "na chAnyAnnaM sarvabhUtAdyaM, na cha tatkasyApi mukhyAdyam | kintu tadgato viShNurevAdanaphalabhUta- tR^iptituShTidAtR^itvAnmukhyAdyaH, tasmAdupajIvyatvamevAdyatvam,
atttR^itvAtsarvalokAnAmannamityuchyate hariH |
upajIvyashcha bhUtAnAmiti chAnnaM janArdanaH ||
iti ukteH" iti upajIvyatvasya mukhyArthataivoktA | na cha virodhaH, kampanAdhikaraNoktarItyA samanvayatAtparyeNa tattvapradIpapravR^itteH | 'vajravat' ityAdAviva yathA kathaJNchidbrahmaparatvAbhiprAyeNa sudhApravR^itteH | nanu kathamannamayashabdaH tatprAchuryArtho yujyate | "oShadhIbhyosnnam | annAtpuruShaH" (tai.u. 2-1-2.) iti prasiddhAnnavikAradehamuktvA "sa vA eSha puruShosnnarasamayaH" (tai.u. 2-1-3.) iti ya eva puruShaH sosnnarasamaya iti annavikAra- puruShaparAmarshAdanuvAdAt | anyathA tadvirodhaH syAdityata Aha - sa iti | 'avirodhaH' ityAkR^iShyate | tathAcheti vAkyena yasmAdAtmanaH AkAshAdikamutpannaM sa eSha puruSha iti 'anyasya' dehAdanyasyAtmanaH 'prArambhAt' parAmarshAt 'avirodho' na parAmarshavirodhaH | kimarthamasau parAmR^ishyate ityAshaN^kApanodanAya parAmarshAditi vaktavye prArambhAdi- tyAha | pUrvamAtmanaH AkAshAdikAraNatvamuktvA tasyaiva 'anyArtham' anyakAryAya annamayAdipaJNcharUpatvapradarshanAya punaH 'prArambhAt' prakrAntatvAdityarthaH | 'sa vA' iti shrutau vaishabdosvadhAraNe prasiddhau vA | annashabdo bhAvapradhAnaH| rasatvamuttamatvaM, tachchAnnatvavisheShaNam | tathA cha yasmAtsatyatvAdilakShaNopetAdAtmana AkAshAdikamutpannaM 'saH' Atmapadodito bhUtAdisraShTA 'eShaH' jIvasharIragaH 'puruShaH' pUrNaShaDguNaH dehAkhyapurishayaH bhagavAn 'annarasamayaH' uttamAnnatvapUrNa ityarthaH | taittirIyabhAShye tu - "annasyAtttR^itvAdi- 
rUpasyAnnamayasharIrasya yataH sArabhUto viShNuH atosnnarasamayaH" iti annashabdasyAvR^ittyA rasashabdasya kramavyatyAsena cha vyAkhyAtam |
(15) nanvevaM mayaTChabdasyobhayArthe prayogAdatrApyubhayapakShe doShadarshanAtpaJNchAnAM mayaTAM prAchuryamevArtho na vikAritvamityatra kiM niyAmakam?  kiJNchAnnamayAdInAM paJNchAnAM brahmatAsbhyupagatau 'ekameva' (ChA.u. 6-2-1.) ityAdishrutivirodhaH syAt ityata Aha - yesnnaM brahmeti || atrAdishabdena 'ye prANaM brahmopAsate' (tai.u. 2-3-1.)| 'AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn' (tai.u. 2-4-1.) 'vij~nAnaM brahma chedveda' (tai.u. 2-5-1.) 'asti brahmeti chedveda' (tai.u. 2-6-1.) iti vAkyajAtaM gR^ihyate | asti AnandarUpaM tadvachcha | 'ityAdi' iti luptasaptamIvibhaktikam | 'shlokeShu' iti sheShaH | brahmashabdapadaM tachChravaNopalakShakam | evaM pradarshite hetudvayesdhyAhR^itahetudvArAnvayayogye krameNa sAdhye Aha - na vikAritvamiti | 'mayaTAmartha iti nishchIyate' iti sheShaH | 'avirodho' virodhAbhAvaH | chashabdospyarthaH | tathA chetthaM yojanA - 'yesnnaM brahma' ityAdiShu annamayAdInpratyudAhR^itashlokeShu annamayAdiviShayatvena 'brahmashabdAt' brahmashabdashravaNAdanyathAsiddhatatsamabhi- vyAhArAt ubhayathAspi sambhavatAM mayaTAM prAchuryamevArthaH na vikAritvamiti nishchIyate | ato na niyAmakAkShepo yuktaH | evamekasyaiva brahmaNo 'bahurUpatvAchcha' shabdAdekasyaiva bahurUpatvavachanopapatteH 'ekameva' iti shrutivirodhospi neti | pUrvaM 'tasminneva prasiddhabrahmashabdAbhyAsAt' ityuktvA atra brahmashabdAdityetAvanmAtrokteH prayojanaM tu "brahmashabdasyAnandavij~nAnamayayorivAnyeShvabhyAsAbhAvAtteShvasiddhi- parihAreNa brahmashabdashravaNarUpasarvasAdhAraNahetvarthakathanameva" ityuktaM chandrikAyAm |
(16) atrAnyaiH Anandamaya eva brahma | tadgatamayaTa eva prAchuryArthatA | annamayAdayastu koshAH | tadgatAnAM mayaTAM cha vikArArthatvamityuktam | tadayuktamityAha - na cheti || prAyapaTitamayaTAM 'pR^ithakkalpanA' arthadvaividhyakalpanA na yuktA | tatashchAnnamayAdInAM madhye ekasyaiva brahmatvakalpanA cha na yuktaiva, prAyapAThavirodhena kliShTatvAdityarthaH | yastu vAdI annamayAdInAM paJNchAnAmapyabrahmatAM brUte, sa tu sUtrakAreNaiva pUrvapakShIkR^ita iti na tatpakShaM pratyAkShipadbhAShyakAraH | tattvapradIpe tu - na cheti vAkyaM na cha mAyinA pR^ithakkalpanA 'satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma' (tai.u. 2-1-1.) 'tasmAdvA etasmAdAtmanaH' (tai.u. 2-1-2.) ityatra brahmochyate | annamayAdayaH paJNchakoshA mitho bhinnAH teShAM brahmashabdoktatvespi abrahmatvam| antyapuchChasyaiva brahmatvam | annamayAdyatikramo mokShaH | vakShyamANAnAM chakShushshrotramanovAchAM nAnnamayAdiShvanuvR^ittiH | 'annaM brahmeti vyajAnAt' (tai.u. 3-2.) ityAdau paà¤¼JNchamasyAnandasya brahmatvam | 'etamAnandamayamAtmAnamupasaN^kramya'

(17) AnandamayamAtrasya viShNutve, hetvantararUpaM prAchuryameva mayaDartha ityatra cha hetuM pratipAdayatsUtramupanyasyati - taddhetviti || Anandamaya iti tattviti chAnuvartate | tadityasyAvR^ittiH | sa chAsau hetushchetyapi vigrahaH | tathA cha na kevalaM brahmashabdAbhyAsAt | kintu 'taddhetuvyapadeshAt' tasminnAnandamayaprakaraNe tasya viShNoH tasmin anandapUrNatvenAnandamayatve prAchuryasyaiva mayaDarthatve cha taddhetuvyapadeshAt lokacheShTakatvAkhyahetUkteshchAnandapUrNatvenaivA- nandamayashabdavAchyo viShNureveti sUtravR^itti- mabhipretya tameva hetuvyapadeshaM darshayati - kohIti | 'yat' yadA yadi 'eShaH AkAshaH' AsamantAtprakAshamAno viShNurAnandaH pUrNAnando na syAt tadAssau lokaM na pravartayediti sheShaH | AnandodrekamantareNa pravR^itto kAraNAntarAbhAvAditi bhAvaH | yadyasau na lokaM pravartayet | tadA 'ko hyevAnyAt' ko vA janaH lokaM cheShTayet | 'kashcha prANyAt' dharmAdau cha kaH pravartayet | na kospi | anyasyAsvAtantryAditi taittirIyabhAShyaTIkArItyA shrutyarthaH | sudhAyAM tu NyarthAnandarbhAvena na kospi lokikIM vaidikIM pravR^ittiM kuryAditi vyAkhyAtam | itItyasya iti taddhetuvyapadeshAdityanvayaH ||
(18) yaduktaM brahmashabdAdAnandamayAdInAM viShNutvamiti na tadyuktam | brahmashabdasya aparabrahmaNi jIvespyupa- patteH| tasya parabrahmaNi mukhyatvespi viShNoH AnandamayAvayavatvoktyAdinA bAdhakenAmukhyArthasyaiva grahaNopapatterityA- shaN^kAM pariharat AnandamayAdishabdavAchyasya viShNutve yuktyantaraM vadan sUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - mAntravarNikamiti | yata ityAdau yojyaM, 'na te' iti pratij~nAsnuvartate | tathA cha yataH 'satyaM j~nAnamanantaM brahma' (tai.u. 2-1-1.) iti 'mantravarNe' mantrAkShare tadAtmakavAkyavisheShe 'lakShitaM' lakShaNavattayA proktameva parameva brahma nAlakShitaM, nAparamityevArthaH| annamayAdishabdaiH 'gIyate' pratipAdyate atospyAnandamayAdayo nApare | kintu parameva brahmeti yojanA | kutosnnamayA- dishabdairmantravarNalakShitasyaiva pratipAdanaM j~nAyata ityata uktam - shabdAnusandhAnAditi | 'shabdAnAM' satyaM j~nAnamanantam ityevaMrUpANAm annamayAdishabdAnAM cha arthAnusandhAnAt jAtAt 'anusandhAnAt' 
ekArthatvaj~nAnAdityarthaH | mantravarNespi brahmetyevoktatvAtkathaM tadarthAnAmapyannamayAdishabdAnAM parabrahmArthatAj~naptirityata Aha - brahmaviditi | pravR^itta iti sheShaH | asya buddhyA viviktena mantravarNapadenAnvayaH | tathA cha yato 'brahmavidApnoti param' (tai.u. 2-1-1.) iti | parabrahmatajj~nAnatatprAptIH sUchayitvA saN^kShepeNaktvA tatra prAptashaN^kApanodAya pravR^itto mantravarNaH | tatostra lakShitaM paraM brahmaiveti j~nAyata ityarthaH | sUtre AnandamayAdistattviti chAnuvartate | chashabdo yatha ityarthe yuktisayuchchaye cha | tathA cha na kevalaM brahmashabdAdevAnandamayAdiviShNvAkhyaM parabrahmaiva nAparabrahmetyavasIyate | kintu yato mAntravarNikaM 'satyaM j~nAnam' iti vedavAkyena lakShaNavattayA proktaM paraM brahamaivAnnamayAdishabdaiH 'gIyate' pratipAdyate cha | atastatsamAkhyAnAdArthikAdapIti sUtrArthaH | 'brahmavit' parabrahmaj~nAnI 'paraM' paramaM brahmApnoti | parabrahma- prAptikAmaH parabrahma jAnIyAt iti shruteH phalitosrthaH | kiM tadbrahmeti shaN^kAyAM satyamityAdi pravR^ittam | tatra satyashabdenoktaM yat gatijIvananAshaprApakatvaM tadevAnnamayaprANamayashabdAbhyAmuchyate | anantashabdenoktaM deshataH kAlato vastutashcha aparichChinnatvam | paramAtmAsnantaH pUrNAnandatvAdityAnandamayashabdenopapAdyata iti satyAdishabdAnAM annamayAdishabdAnAM chakArthatvam anusandheyam | atra deshAnantyaM nAma anavadhikaparimANatvam | kAlAnantyaM nAma anavachChinnasattAkatvam | vastvAnantyaM nAma aparichChinnasaN^khyAguNakarmavigrahavattvam ||
(19) nanu viShNorAnandamayatvaM na yuktaM, tasya tadavayavatvAt | na chAsiddhiH, brahmapuchChamityukteH | avayavinashchAvayavatvavirodhAdityata Aha - na cheti | tasyetyAtkR^iShyate | 'tasya' viShNorAnandamayatve tadavayavatvoktivirodho netyarthaH | avayavatve cha avayavitvasya virodhospi neti chashabdArthaH | kuta ityatosvayavina evAvayavatvasyAvayavitvasya cha shrutyuktatvenAvayavyAderavayavAdyabhedAdityAshayena tAM shrutimudAharati - sa iti | 'saH' nArAyaNaH 'shiraH' shIrShaM, shiraH sa iti vA | evam uttaratrApi vyAkhyeyam | dvitIyAditachChabdAH smR^ityanusArAtpradyumnAdiparAH | 'pakSho' bAhuH 'uttaraH' savyaH 'AtmA' madhyadehaH 'puchChaM' pAdau itItyasyaivaMrUpAyAM chaturvedashikhAyAM tasyaivAvayavibhUtasyaiva viShNoravayavatvo- kterityanvayaH | evashabdenAvayavAvayavibhedo nivAritaH | evaM avayavasyAvayavitve na kevalamiyaM shrutiH, kintu - bhAShye upalakShaNayA gR^ihItA 'padaM puchChaM pratiShThA vai puruShaH' iti tattvapradIpodAhR^itashrutirapi pramANatayA grAhyA | asmin pakShe bhAShyagatAvayavashabdaH arshaAdyajantosvayaviparaH ||
(20) avayavina avayavatvaM viruddhamityAshaN^kAM shrutyA parihR^ityAtra smR^itiM chAha - shira iti | atra chitrAdau likhyamAnanavanArIrUpe avayavibhUtAnAmanekastrINAmekadehAvayavatvaM tathA nArAyaNAdipaJNcharUpANAM ekAvayavatvamuchyate| AdyashchaH pakShasamuchchaye | rUpayoH parasparasamuchchaye dvau | avayavibhUta eva nArAyaNaH shira ityevashabdAnvayaH | evamavayavibhUtaH pradyumno dakShiNaH pakSho bAhuH | aniruddhaH savyaH | vAsudevaH 'sandoho' madhyadeha ityanvayaH | apiveti nipAtasamudAyaH pakShAntare | pUrvasmin pakShe nArAyaNasya

'aishvaryAt' IshvarasAmarthyAt tayorekatrAvasthAnarUpAvirodhopapatteH IshvarashaktishchAghaTitaghaTiketi bhAvaH | evaM 'tasmin' avayave 'tasmin' avayavitve na virodhaH | kutaH? ekaikasyAvayavasya sarveshvaratvAdityapi vyAkhyeyam | evaM na virodha ityetat avayavAvayavinorabhedesyamavayavI ayam avayava iti bhedavyavahAravirodhospi netyapi vyAkhyeyam | tatra hetustu visheShabalAchChaktivyaktibhAvAditi chashabdena sUchitaH | ata eva chashabdosnuktasamuchchayArthaH aishvaryAchchetyanveti | kiJNcha - kiM tarkAnyapramANenAvayavinosvayavatvamavayavasyAvayavitvaM cha viruddham?  uta avayavI nAvayavaH avayavitvAt | avayavo vA nAvayavI avayavatvAllokavaditi tarkapadoktAnumAnena?  nAdyossiddhatvAt | na dvitIya ityAha - atarkya iti | 'hi' yasmAdatarkyaH tasmAt 'atarkye' tarkAgochare bhagavati tadviShaye 'tarkaH' avayavI nAvayavaH avayavitvAt ityAdirUpo hetuH 'kutaH' sAdhako bAdhako vA netyarthaH | kiJNcha - loke parimitashaktitva eva virodhadarshanAt viShNorvirodhopayogiparimitashaktishUnyatvAt tarkyatvAN^gIkArespi na virodha ityAha - aprameya iti | 'aprameye' deshakAlaguNairaparichChinne bhagavati 'pramA' etAvadeva sAmarthyaM nAtosdhikamiti shaktiparichChedaH 'kutaH' netyarthaH | tathA cha paroktatarkasya sopAdhikatvenApramANatvAnna virodhitvamiti bhAvaH | anena 'atarkya' ityasyAsattarkAgochara ityartha ityuktaM bhavati | iti bR^ihatsaMhitAyAmityasya 'tasyaivAvayavatvokteH' ityanuShaktenAnvayaH ||
(21) nanu yaduktaM sa vA iti vAkyessya paramAtmana eva parAmarshaH na annAtpuruShaH ityuktadehasyeti tadayuktam; Atmano dUrasthatvAddehasya sa samApasthatvAtsamIpoktaparityAgena dUrasthaparAmarshAN^gIkAre kAraNAbhAvAt | kiJNcha - puruShapadena prakR^itasyaiva puruShapadenoktatvAt Atmanashcha tena aprakR^itatvAtpuruShapadena parAmarshAyogaH | na cha -
prakR^itiM puruShaM chaivaM viddhyanAdI ubhAvapi |
puruShaH prakR^itistho hi bhuN^kte prakR^itijAn guNAn ||

tadityAvartate | evamuchyata iti cha | anyadvihAyeti sheShaH | tathA cha sa vA iti vAkyena chideva chinmAtraM brahmachaitanyameva uchyate parAmR^ishyate na dehaH | na cha tasya dUroktivirodhaH, puruShapadenA- prakR^itatvavirodhashcheti vAchyam | yatastat Atmana AkAshassambhUtaH (tai.u. 2-1-2.) ityAkAshAdipuruShAntashabdairuktaM tattatsArabhUtam AkAshAdipadArthashreShThabhUtaM chinmAtraM brahmaiva sa vA iti parAmarshavAkyenochyate | evaM tarhi puruShapadena dvayorapi prakR^itatvAdubhayaparAmarshosyamastviti na cha vAchyam | yataH tatsArabhUtaM puruShasArabhUtaM chinmAtraM brahmaivAnyadehAdikaM vihAya saH iti parAmarshavAkyenochyate | kuta ityata Aha - raseti | rasashabdaghaTitAnna- rasamayashabdena visheShaNAt sArAnnamayatvarUpapuruShavisheShaNAbhidhAnAdityarthaH | jaDAmishrajIvavilakShaNabrahmabodhArthaM mAtra- padam | rasashabdena rasashabdArthena mukhyatvena visheShaNAt visheShitatvAt annatvarUpavisheShaNasyeti vA | tatashchAtra annarasosnnasArosnnashabdArtheShu mukhyAttR^itvAdilakShaNastatprachuraH iti sudhokteH | TIkAyAM chaitanyamAtraM brahmaivetyanvayaH | nanvanuvAkAntare annamayaprANamayamanomayavij~nAnamayAnandamayA me shuddhyantAm (yAj~nikI. 66.) iti prArthitashuddhInA- mannamayAdikoshAnAmabhidhAnam| kintu, tattatsArabhUtaM tattatkoshaniyAmakaM tadgataM brahmachaitanyameva uchyate | kutaH? (22) nanvannamayAdInAM paJNchAnAM brahmatAsnupapannA 'tasmAdvA etasmAdannarasamayAt | anyosntara AtmA prANamayaH' (tai.u. 2-2-2.) iti parasparaM bhinnatvenoktatvAt | evamekasyaiva brahmaNo bahurUpatvAt na 'ekameva' iti shrutivirodhaH ityapyayuktamapramitatvAdityata Aha - ananya iti || apiryadyapItyadyarthe | tathAshabdaH samuchchaye | tathA cha 'puruShottamo bhagavAnviShNuH' 'ananyospi' abhinnospi anyo bhinna iti shabdena prochyata | tathA yadyapyeka- stathAspi bahurUpavAn bhavatItyarthaH | kathamityata ubhayaghaTakamAha -

(23) nanu brahmashabdasya sAdhAraNatvAt taddhetuvyapadeshasya viShNuniShThatayA spaShTapratibhAnAt mantravarNasamAkhyAyAshcha anyaliN^gAdibhyo durbalatvena sAvakAshatvAt ananyathAsiddhahetvantarasya chAbhAvAdAnandamayAdayo viriJNchAdaya eva santviti shaN^kAM pariharatsUtramavatArayati - na cheti || chosvadhAraNe | viriJNchAdaya ityanenAnveti | tathA cha 'uktaprAptyA' brahmashabdashatAnandatvAShTamUrtitva- bahubhAvAdirUpoktaprApakenAnna- mayAdishabdairviriJNchAdirevochyate | na viShNuriti na, kintu, viShNureva tairuchyate | na viriJNchAdirityarthaH | kuto neti hetvAkAN^kShAyAM sUtramupanyasya pratij~nAMshasya na chetyAdibhAShyeNaiva vyAkhyAtatvAtsautramananyathAsiddhahetumeva vyAchaShTe - netara iti | hishabdo hetau | 'anyaj~nAnAt' viShNvanyaviriJNchAdij~nAnAt | yadyapyayaM netara ityuktasAdhye na hetuH| tathAspi tasyAnanyathAsiddhatvopapAdakatvAddhetutvoktiH | asya hetuvAkyasya adhyAhR^itahetuvAkyadvArA na cheti pratij~na- yAsnvayaH | anenAnandamayAdiH viShNoritaro viriJNchAdirna, kutaH?  'brahmavidApnoti param (tai.u. 2-1-1.) ... sarvaM vai tesnnamApnuvanti (tai.u. 2-2-1.).... sarvameva ta Ayuryanti' (tai.u. 2-3-1.) ityAdinA AnandamayA- dermuktihetuj~nAnaviShayatvokteH, tasya chetaratra 'anupapatteH' ayogAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | viShNuj~nAnAdeva mokSho netaraj~nAnAdityetatkuta ityata Aha - tamiti | 'hi' yasmAt 'tamevam' iti shrutyA mokShasya viShNuj~nAnAdanya upAyo nAstItyuktam | tasmAdviShNoranyaj~nAnAnmokSho nopapadyata ityarthaH | shrutyarthastu prAgevoktaH ||
(24) hetvantareNa brahmAdInAmAnandamayatvaM parAkurvatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - bhedeti | atra pUrvahetu- samuchchAyakena chashabdenAnandamayAdirnetara iti pratij~nAvAkyAnuvR^itterapi sUchanAt | tadvihAya sUtroktaM bhedavyapadeshaM darshayati - te ye shatamiti || AdishabdaH  'AnandAH' ityataH parospi yojyaH | tatrAdyena 'te ye shatam' ityasya pUrvottarataittirIyavAkyAni gR^ihyante | dvitIyena 'yato vAcho nivartante | aprApya manasA saha | AnandaM brahmaNo vidvAn', (tai.u. 2-4-1.) ityAdi | yadvA sakR^ichChruta eva sarvasaN^grAhakaH| anena nAnandamaya itaro viriJNchaH, kutaH?  bhedavyapadeshAt | viriJNchasya 'te ye shatam' (tai.u. 2-8-4.) ityAdinA rudrAchChataguNAnandatvokteH, Ananda- mayasya cha 'yato vAchaH' ityAdinAsparimitAnandatvokteH | evaM na rudraH, tasya hiraNyagarbhAchChatAMshonAnandatvokteH | nApi prakR^ityAdayaH, 'adR^ishyenAtmye' ityAdau 
prakR^ityAdyayogyasvAtantryAdirUpabhedakadharmashravaNAt | nApyAnandamayo brahmAdijIvasamudAyaH, tasya 'sa yashchAyam' iti apakR^iShTotkR^iShTasarvajIsthitirUpabhedakadharmokteH jIvasamudAyasya chAnevaMvidhatvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | ete cha sarve vyapadeshAH taittirIyashrutigatAH | tatra 'prajApatiH shivaH shepho liN^gamityabhidhIyate' iti shaivapurANavachanAt 'prajApateH' rudrasya 'ye shataM' shataguNitA AnandAH te 'brahmaNaH' chaturmukhasya eka Ananda iti prathamavAkyasyArthaH | 'adR^ishye' sAkalyenAj~neye 'anAtmye' AtmanaH ime AtmyAH jIvagINAH na vidyante AtmyAH yasmin sosnAtmyaH tasmin jIvaguNavidhure | athavA - AtmanaH svAminos- yamAtmyaH svAmisambandhI sa netyanAtmyaH tasmin, svAmirahita iti yAvat | 'anirukte' sAkalyena nirvachanAgochare | 'anilayane' ananyAshraye AnandamayashabdavAchye viShNau tadviShaye yosdhikArI 'abhayaM' yathA bhavati tathA dhyAnarUpAM 'pratiShThAM' sthitiM 'vindate' prApnoti, karotIti yAvat | 'atha' anantaraM 'saH' upAsakaH 'abhayaM' bhayarahitaM bhagavantaM 'gataH' prApto bhavatIti dvitIyabhedavyapadeshasyArthaH | 'puruShe' puruShapadopalakShitApakR^iShTajIveShu 'yaH' ayamAnandamayo viShNurasti | 'yashchAditye' AdityapadopalakShitotkR^iShTajIveShvasti 'saH' ubhayatra sthito viShNuH 'ekaH' abhinna iti tR^itIyabhedavyapadeshasyArthaH | 'yato vAchaH' ityAdistu prAgeva vyAkhyAtaH ||
(25) nanvastvAnandamayaH paraM brahma | tathAspi tena kathaM brahmAdInAM bhedaH sambhavati | tadbhedasya 'tattvamasi' ityAdi shrutiviruddhatvAdityata Aha - na cheti || bhedavyapadeshasyeti sheShaH | chaH samuchchaye | etadvirodhashaN^kA- parihArasamuchchitasyaiva bhedavyapadeshasya vivakShitArthasAdhakatvAt | evamanyatrApi | tvaM tadbrahmAsItyadvaitarItyAssdya- shrutyarthaH | dvatIyasyAstu ahaM brahmAbhinnossmIti | Adyam uddAlakena shvetaketuM pratyupadiShTaM ChandogavAkyam | dvitIyaM bR^ihadAraNyake vAmadevoktam | atrobhayatrApi vishiShTayoraikyAsambhavAt tattvamahaMbrahmapadairlakShitachaitanyayoraikyamuchyate | Adishabdena 'tadyoshaM sossau yossau soshaM' (ai.A. 2-2-4.) 'yossAvasau puruShaH soshamasmi' (I. 26.) ityAdishrutirgR^ihyate | kuto netyatastatraitachChrutInAM parabrahmArthakatvena advaitArthatvAbhAvAditi hetUpaskAramabhipretya teShAM parabrahmArthatve pramANamAha - nAmAnIti | 'nAmAni' iti shrutyA tasya brahmaNaH 'tattachChabdaiH' tattvamAdipadairvAchyatvokte- rityarthaH | tathA cha padasamanvayenaiteShAM brahmaparatvAnnaitadvirodha iti bhAvaH | tatprakArastu - tatatvAttat | tvampadabodhyajIvAntaryAmitvAdabhimukhatvAdvA tvam | asanAt jagatsaMharaNAdasiH | aheyatvAt haMnAmakajIvabhinna- tvAdvA aham | pUrNatvAdbrahma | asanAnminuterasmi | yadvA - sumitatvAt smItyukto jIvaH, tadbhinnaM pUrNaM brahma asmItyuchyata iti | j~nAnarUpatvAt nitarAM yantR^itvAchcha yaH | saraNAtsAra- tvAchcha saH | amuShmin amuShmin sthitatvAtparokShatvAchcha asAvasaushabdavAchyaH ityaitareyashrutyarthaH | 'asau' prANe sthitaH 'puruShaH' pUrNaShaDguNaH iti IshAvAsyashrutyarthaH |
(26) astu vA etachChrutInAM aikyaparatvaM vAkyAnvayarItyA | tathAspi naikyashrutivirodho bhedashruteH shaN^kanIyaH, bhagavataH sarvaikyashruteH sarvasvAmitvanimittaikyaparatvAdityAshayena tatra pramANatvena bhAgavatasmR^itiM paThati - idaM hIti || 'bhagavAn' svayam 'itarospi' jagato bhinnospi san 'idaM' pramitaM vishvamivochyate 'tattvamasi' 'ahaM brahmAsmi' ityAdivachaneShu | yathoktaM prathamatAtparye - 'itarospi bhagavAnvishvamiva' iti | kutaH?  'yataH' kAraNAt 'jagatsthAnanirodhasambhavaH' jagataH sthAnaM sthitiH nirodho nAshaH sambhavaH utpattiH te yasmAdbhavanti sa tathoktaH | yadvA - sthApayati nirodhayati sambhAvyatyasmAditi tathoktaH | athavA - tiShThatyasmAt niruddhyate pralIyatessmin sambhAvayatIti sa tathoktaH | tathA cha jagatsR^iShTyAdikartetyarthaH | evambhUtsya jagadbhedaH pramANasiddha iti j~nApanAya hishabdaH | tattvapradIpe tu - bahuvrIhiM vinA idaM vishvaM bhagavAniva; etadadhInatvAt | sa tvitaraH | kaH?  'yato' yasmAt 'jagatsthAnanirodhasambhavo' jagatsR^iShTyAdikamityuktam | atra TIkAyAM cha bhagavAnidaM vishvamivetyanvayaH | svAmitvenaikyavyapadesha ityetadevAha - asarva iti | turashrutiH | bhagavAn sarvabhinnospi sarvasvAmitvAt sarva ityabhedena vedAdiShUchyate ityarthaH | ityapIti shrutisthaH apiH samuchchaye | yata iti sheShaH | asya atospi na virodha ityanvayaH | 
(27) nanu bhedaj~nAnasya mithyAj~nAnatvAtkathaM tadanusAreNaikyashrutayo yojyanta ityAshaN^kAM bhAgavatavAkyena pariharati - vidyeti || idaM cha kA vidyetyuddhavaprashnasyottaratvena kR^iShNenoktaM vachanamekAdashaskandhe | 'Atmani' paramAtmani 'bhidAbodho' jIvAdbhedaj~nAnaM jIve vA yadIshvarAdbhedaj~nAnam | saiva vidyetyarthaH | na cha bhidAyA abodha iti vyAkhyeyam, aj~nAnasya vidyAtvAbhAvAt | nanu bhedaj~nAnasya puruShArthahetutvAt kathaM tasya vidyAtvamityata Aha - bhedeti | idaM cha bhAgavate tR^itIyaskandhagataM vAkyam -
AdyaH sthiracharANAM yo vedagarbhaH saharShibhiH |
yogeshvaraiH kumArAdyaiH siddhairyogapravartakaiH ||
iti pUrvavAkyena 
kartR^itvAtsaguNaM brahma puruShaM puruSharShabham |
sa saN^gatya punaH kAle kAleneshvaramUrtinA ||
jAtesguNavyatikare yathApUrvaM prajApate ||
ityuttaravAkyena cha saha yojanIyam | tatprakArastu - yaH 'sthiracharANAM' sthAvarajaN^gamAnAm 'Adyo' hiraNyagarbhaH saH 'R^iShibhiH' manuShyottamamArabhya garuDasheShAntaiH j~nAnibhiryogasiddhaiH sanatkumArAdyaiH saha 'bhedadR^iShTyA' jIveshvarAdibhedaj~nAnena 'abhimAnena' abhito harermAnena parameshvare bahumAnena AgraheNa cha 'niHsaN^gena karmaNAspi' phalAbhisandhirahitanivR^ittakarmaNA cha muktassan 'kartR^itvAt' jagatkartR^itvAnnimittAt 'saguNaM' sArvaj~nAdiguNasampUrNaM 'puruSharShabhaM' kSharAkSharebhyo varaM 'puruShaM' paramapuruShAkhyaM brahma 'kAle' pralayakAle 'saN^gatya' pravishya punaH 'kAlena' kAlAkhyena 'IshvaramUrtinA' mUrtyA 'kAle' sR^iShTikAle 'jAte' utpanne sati 'aguNavyatikare' sattvAdiguNavikriyAhIne viShNuloke 'yathApUrvaM' pUrvavat prajAyate sarvamuktAdhipatirjAyate iti sudhAyAmuktaH | karmanirNayaTIkAyAM tu - na kevalaM saguNaM, kintu, 'brahma' purNaM 'puruShamiti' bhagavato nAmakIrtanam | puruShatvoktyAssmAdAdisAlakShaNyaM prAptaM, tatparihArAya - puruSharShabhamiti | tadupapAdanAya kartR^itvAtsaguNaM brahmeti visheShArtha uktaH | tattvapradIpe tu - abhimAneneti padaM abhito mAnena visheShaj~nAneneti vyAkhyAya, 'guNavyatikare' iti padaM ChitvA 'sa' brahmAdijIvasaN^ghaH pralaye j~nAnaishvaryA- dyanantaguNaM brahma 'saN^gatya' prApya 'punaH kAle' sR^iShTikAle 'kAlena' j~nAnAtmanA 'IshvaramUrtinA' viShNurUpeNa 'guNavyatikare' guNAnAM sattvAdInAM vyatikare vaiShamye jAte sati yathApUrvaM j~nAnAdiguNatAratamyaM parasparabhedaM cha avihAya tadvishiShTa eva 'prajAyate' prakarSheNa muktAvabhivyajyate | na tu tadabhinno bhavatIti vyAkhyAtam| ayaM padachChedaShTIkAkR^itospi sammataH | tatpakShe 'guNavyatikare kAle' sR^iShTikAle ityarthaH | ubhayatrApi yathApUrvamityasya saMsAra ivetyartha | pUrvakalpe iveti vA |
(28) atraivArthe atharvaNavAkyaM pramANayati - juShTamiti || juShTaM sarvasevyam IshaM svatantram | ata eva anyaM jIvAdbhinnaM viShNum iti tadetatsatyam (mu. 2-1-1-.) ityAdinA prAguktaprakAreNa asya mahimAnaM cha yadA pashyati | pashyo jIvaH tadA vItashoko mukto bhavatItyarthaH | tattvapradIpe tu - juShTaM devaiH asya jIvasya Isham anyaM yadA pashyati mahimAnaM mahimaguNAtmakaM tadA tadaiva vItashoko bhavati na duHkhaleshamapi spR^ishati jIvaH | na tu mahimaguNavihInam anyamanIshamasevitaM pashyan vItashoko bhavatIti vyAkhyAtam | yadyapIyaM shrutiH visheShaNabhedavyapadeshAbhyAm (bra. sU. 1-2-22.) ityatra ayamanyomArga ityukte prasiddhamArgAdanyatvabodhavat anyamIsha- mityukte Ishashabditasya brahmaNaH prasiddheshAdrudrAt anyatvapratIterbrahmaNo rudrAdanyatve pramANatvenoktA |  na tu brahmaNo jIvAdanyatve, nApi Ishatvamanyatve hetUkR^itam | tathApi tat vyAkhyAnAnantaramabhipretyeti na tadvirodhaH | ata eva dyubhvAdinaye bhedavyapadeshAt (bra.sU. 1-3-5.) ityatra jIveshabhedespIyaM pramANatayodAhR^itA |
(29) evaM svAmitvArthatayA parAbhimatAdvaitashrutIrvyAkhyAya vAkyasamanvayAshrayaNena antaryAmitayApi tAH shrutismR^itibhyAM vyAchaShTe - asarva iti | yadyapi asarvaH iti vAkyam Atmashabdasya svAmitvArthatvamupetya svAmitvena nimittenaikyashrutayaH pravR^ittA ityatra pramANatayodAhR^itam | tathAspi svAmitvenevAntaryAmitayAspyaikyashrutayaH pravR^ittA ityubhayatrApyasya pramANatvasambhavAdubhayatrApi pramANatayodAharaNaM yuktam | tattvapradIpakR^itAmapi svAmitvenevAnta- ryAmitayApyaikyashrutayaH pravR^ittA ityubhayatrApi asarvaH iti shrutiH pramANamityabhiprAyaH | na chaivaM tattadantaryAmitvenApi tattachChabdavAchyatvaM viShNorastItyAha - sarvAntaryAmikaH iti tattvapradIpavirodhaH; atra padasamanyavAbhiprAyapratIteriti vAchyam | antaryAmitvenApItyuktyA na kevalaM nAmAni iti shrutibalAttattachChabdapravR^ittinimittatvena tattachChabdavAchyatvaM viShNoH, api tu antaryAmitvenApItyetAvanmAtrapratIteH atra padasamanvaye tAtparyAnavagamAt | mahAvAkyagatasyaitadAdi- shabdasyaikaikasya sarvAntaryAmikaH iti smR^itibalAt antaryAmitvanimittena viShNuvAchitvespi padAntarANAnyaparatvena vAkyasamanvayasyaiva vaktavyatvAt | yadA nAmAni iti shrutibalAt kriyAkArakAdisarvArthavAchisarvapadasya viShNuvAchi- tvAbhyupagamaH tadaiva padasamanvayaH | na tvekaikasya viShNuvAchitva iti na virodhaH tathA chAntaryAmitvanimittena tattvamasyAdivAkyagatatvamahamAdipadAnAM viShNuvAchitve tvaM tvadantaryAmI tat brahma | ahaM madantaryAmI brahmeti vAkyAnvayo draShTavyaH | na chaivami asi asmi iti kriyApadAnvayAyogaH | jIvavishiShTAntaryAmivAchakasya tvamAdishabdasya dagdhR^ishabdasyAyasIvAntaryAmiNi mukhyavR^ittiH | jIvetvamukhyavR^ittirityAshrayaNenAmukhyArthavivakShayA asi asmItyAdipadaprayogopapatteH | yadyapi nimittakathanaprakaraNe vidyAsstmani bhedadR^iShTyA juShTaM yadA iti vAkyatraya- syAnvayAbhAvaH | tathAspi svAmitvanimittenaikyavyapadesha ityatra shrutismR^ityorupanyAne sati tatra prAptashaN^kAparihAra- syAvashyakatvenAvasarasaN^gatyA tadvAkyatrayapravR^itteH | ityAdeH ityasAyatrAkarShaNena na virodhaH ityasyAnukarShaNena chAnvayo draShTavyaH | shrutyarthastu - viShNuH asarvospi sarvanAtmakospi sarva iva sarvAtmaka iva sarvAtmakatvena Iyate | kuta ityatastatrAntaryAmitvaM hetutvenAbhipretya anantaryAmitvapratItyA tasyAsiddhimAshaN^kyAha - Atmaiveti | Atmaiva antaryAmyeva san anAtmeva anantaryAmitvena Iyate j~nAyate rAmakR^iShNAdirUpeShu | tathA cha aj~nAnamUlA anantaryAmitvapratItiriti bhAvaH | nanu viShNorantaryAmitve pratyaktvaM syAt tachchAnupapannaM, parAktvena pratIterityata Aha - pratyaN^iti | bhagavAn pratyaN^ dehAntargatospi parAN^iva bahirmAtravR^ittitveneyate | tathA cha bahirmAtravR^ittitva- pratItirbhrAntiriti bhAvaH| nanu viShNau viruddhAnekadharmAbhyupagame bhedApattyA ekameva iti shrutivirodha ityata Aha - eka iti | eka eva 
bahudhA bahurUpeNeyata ityarthaH | tathA chaikasyaiva rUpabAhulyAt sarvadharmopapattiriti bhAvaH | dvigrahaNAtsarvatra kriyAsambandhaH sUchitaH | tattvapradIpe tu - pratyaN^ parAN^iva abhimukhospyanabhimukha iva eka eva bahudheyate j~nAyate prApyate cha ityuktam | antaryAmitvanimittena sarvAtmakatvena vyapadishyamAnaH kiM sarvaj~naH?  kva cha vyapadishyata?  ityata Aha - sa puruSha iti | anena puruSha evedaM sarvam (tai.A. 3-12.) iti shrutimupAdatte | sampUrNaShaDguNatvAt dehAkhyapure shayanAdvA puruShasaMj~na ityarthaH | sthalAntaramAha - sa iti | anena sarvaM khalvidaM brahma (ChA. 3-14-1.) iti shrutimupAdatte | saH sarvAtmakatvena vyapadishyamAno bhagavAn brahma sarvatra pUrNatvAdbrahmasaMj~na ityarthaH | nanvanyatrAdR^iShTamantargatasya bahirgatatvAdikaM kathaM ghaTata ityata Aha - sa Ishvara iti | saH hariH yataH IshvaraH achintyashaktyupetaH atastasmin anyatrAghaTitamapi sarvaM ghaTata iti ||
(30) smR^itau kapratyayaH sarvadehagatasyApi viShNoraj~nAtatvamAha | yadvA - yAmo niyamanaM tatra bhava ityarthe Thak, yato viShNuH sarvAntaryAmikaH sarvAntarniyAmakaH ata eva eSha Atmeti hovAcha (ChA. 8-3-4.) soshamasmi (I. 16.) tattvamasi (ChA. 6-8-7.) yossAvasau puruShaH (I. 16.) iti vAkyasthena eShoshaMtvamasAviti sarvanAmnA sarvavAchakasarvanAmasaMN^akashabdena sarvamiti nAmnA chAbhidhIyate | na tu sarvasvarUpatvAdityarthaH | shreShThavastvaikyArtha- tayAspi aikyashrutIH smR^ityA vyAkhyAti - naitaditi | mokShadharme hi vaishampAyanaM prati he brahman bhedavAkyAt bahavaH puruShAH pratipattavyAH | aikyavAkyaM tu pradhAnapuruShaparamiti vA?  utAho aikyavAkyAt eka eva puruShaH, dvaitavAkyaM tu vyAvahArikabhedaparamiti? tathA - puruShabAhulyamupetyaikyavAkyasya shreShThaparatvapakShespi Atmasu kiM sarve samAH?  utaikaH shreShThaH?  dvitIye kossAvatra puruSheShu shreShThaH?  sa kathaM hi shreShThaH?  taM tathA cha bhavAn vaktumarhatItyAshayena kR^itasya janamejayaprashnasya vaishampAyanenoktamuttaram -
naitadichChanti puruShamekaM kurukulodvaha |
bahUnAM puruShANAM hi yathaikA yoniruchyate ||
tathA taM puruShaM vishvamAkhyAsyAmi guNAdhikam ||
iti | asyArthaH - etanmataM nechChanti vidvAMsaH | etaditi kimityatastadvivR^iNoti - puruShamekamiti | tathA cha vedAH ekameva puruShaM vadantItyetanmataM j~nAnino nechChantItyarthaH | yadvA - etasmin jagati ekaM puruShaM 
nechChanti, kintu bahavaH puruShAH santIti | tarhyadvaitashrutivirodha iti na vAchyam | yato bahUnAM shreShThaH eka eva, tatparamaikyavAkyam | bahUnAM kaH shreShThaH?  sa kathaM shreShThaH?  ityasyottaramAha - bahUnAmiti | he kurukulodvaha eteShAM bahUnAM puruShANAm AtmAnAM madhye yA yoniH yaH kAraNabhUtaH ekA shreShThaH yathA cha shreShTha uchyate shrutyAdau tathA tena prakAreNa taM vishvaM pUrNaM guNAdhikaM puruSham AkhyAsyAmi vyAkhyAsyAmIti prameyadIpikAvyAsatIrthIyadishA smR^ityarthaH | anena parAbhima- taikyavAkyamuttamavastvaikyaparam | tathA cha sarvotkR^iShTaM yadekaM brahmatattvamasi tasmAdatyavarossi atyavarossmIti shrutyartha ukto bhavati | ityAdeshcha ityasya na cha tattvamasItyAdivirodhaH ityanenAnvayaH |
(31) nanvadvaitashrutyabhAve kathamadvaitaM bhedashrutyAdinA niShidhyate | tasyApratyakShatvena shrutiM vinA prAptyabhAvAt | aprAptasya cha pratiShedhAyogAt ityata Aha - uktA cheti || chaH sAdhyasamuchchaye | cho yato na cha tattvamasi ityAdinA jIveshvaikyasya prAptiH shrutyarthAparij~nAnanimittA prasaktiruktA | ato na tanniShedhAnupapattirityarthaH | nanvetachChrutInAmavirodhakatvespi bhedashruteH brahmaiva san brahmApyeti iti shrutivirodhastu bhaviShyati | atra brahmaiveteya- vakAreNa jIvasyAbrahmatAniShedhena tadadhInatvAdinA nimittena abrahmabhUte brahmatvavyavahAra ityuktagaterasambhavAdityata Aha - brahmaiveti | apiH samuchchaye | na kevalaM tattvamasItyAdikamaviruddham | kintu brahmaiva san iti bR^ihadAraNya- vAkyamapItyarthaH | kuta ityata Aha - jIve eveti | saptamIyaM viShayArthe | tathA cha yato brahmaiva san iti vAkye shrutosyamAdyo brahmashabdaH brahmANi jIvAH sarvespi iti shruterjIva eva, na parabrahmaNi ata ityarthaH | yadvA - jIva iti prathamAntam | tathA cha iti vAkye shrutAdyabrahmashabdokto jIva eva, na parabrahmetyarthaH | tathA cha iti vAkye shrutAdyabrahmashabdokto jIva eva, na parabrahmetyarthaH | tathA cha saH muktajIvo brahmaiva san jIva eva san jIvabhAvamavihAyaiva pralaye parabrahmApnoti | apihitassan pravishatIti shrutyarthopapatteH noktabhedavyapadeshasyaitachChruti- varodha iti bhAvaH | yathoktaM bR^ihadbhAShye -
jIvospi brahmashabdokto jaDAdbahuguNatvataH | iti ||
prApnoti paramaM brahma pralaye pralaye sadA | iti ||
yadyapi muktAvabhede pareNeyaM shrutirAshaN^kitA | tathaiva viShNutattvavinirNayaTIkokteH | tathA cha muktAviti 
vAchyaM, na tu pralaya iti | tathApi sarvajIvasAdhAraNyAya pralaya ityuktiH | nanu brahmashabdasya parabrahmaNyeva mukhyatvAnna jIvessau yujyata ityata Aha - upapadyata iti | chospyarthaH | tathA cha brahmashabdo yadyapi parabrahmaNi mukhyaH, tathApi virodhe svIyapUrvottaravAkyavirodhe prAmANAntaravirodhe vA sati jIvespyupapadyata ityarthaH | prakR^ite cha brahmApyeti ityuttara- bhAvisvavAkyena paramaM sAmyam iti pUrvavAkyena bhedagrAhipratyakShAdinA cha virodhosstIti bhAvaH |
(32) nanu tathApi bhedavyapadeshasya vimuktashcha vimuchyate (kaTha. 2-5-1.) iti kaThashrutivirodhaH | atra saMsArespi jIvasya muktatvoktyA tadanyathAsnupapattyA parabrahmatvAvagamAt ityata Aha - pramAdeti || chashabdospyarthe samuchchaye cha | tathA cha api - jIvasya parabrahmatvAbhAvespi vimuktatvaM vimuktatvavachanaM cha yujyate | na kevalaM brahmashabda upapadyate iti chArthaH | katham?  bandhasya svataHkartR^itvabhoktR^itvAbhimAnarUpasya jIvagatasaMsArasya pramAdAtmakatvAt pramAdapadoktAj~nAnamUlatvena tannimittapratItikatvenAsvAbhAvikatvAt pramAdapadoktAj~nAnamUlatvena tannimittapratItikatvenAsvAbhAvika- tvAt | asvAbhAvike chAvidyamAnapadaprayogadarshanAdityarthaH | ato na tadvirodha iti bhAvaH | bandhasyA- j~nAnamUlatvaM cha -
ubhe satye kShatriyAdya pravR^itte 
moho mR^ityuH saN^gato yaM kavInAm |
pramAdaM vai mR^ityumahaM bravImi 
tathAspramAdAdamR^itatvaM bravImi |
iti tattvapradIpanyAyAmR^itodAhR^itabhAratavachanasiddhaM dhR^itarAShTraM prati sanatsujAtavAkyametat | he kShatriyAdya mR^ityuH saMsAra tadabhAvarUpAmR^itatvaM chetyubhe api satye eva pravR^itte | tayormadhye mR^ityuH mohaH aj~nAnAdhInastanmUlaH | tarhi mithyA syAdityato netyAha - pramAdaM vA iti | ahaM mR^ityuM saMsAraM pramAdaM asvAbhAvikaM bravImi | amR^itatvaM muktatvaM tu apramAdAt pramAdApAyAt bravImItyarthaH |
(33) bandhasyAsvAbhAvikatvaM kutaH siddhamityata Aha - muktiriti || 'anyathArUpam' asvAbhAvikaM rUpaM 'hitvA' tyaktvA 'svarUpeNa' nijarUpeNAvasthitireva muktirityarthaH | bhAgavata ityasya pramAdAtmakatvokte- rityanenAnvayaH |
(34) nanu bhedokteH shrutivirodhAbhAvespi jIvo brahmAbhinnaH chetanatvAt brahmavat | bhedo mithyA bhedatvAt chandrabhedavat | vimatAni sharIrANi madbhogAyatanAni sharItvAt machCharIravat | ityanumAnavirodhastu bhaviShyatItyata Aha - na cheti || chosvirodhasamuchchaye | tathA cha na kevalaM 
shrutivirodhAbhAvaH, kintu tasyAH bhedokteH tenAdvaitaparikalpitAnumAnena virodhospi netyarthaH | anena sautrashchashabdo vyAkhyAtaH |
(35) tatra hetvAkAN^kShAyAM sUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - kAmAditi || 'hi' yatosbhedasAdhanAya paropanyastam 'anumAnam' anumAnatvena parAbhimataM 'pR^ithak' pratyakShAdiviruddhaM shrutisAhAyyarahitaM cha ataH 'tattve' viShaye j~nAnopalakShakametat | tattvaj~nAnArthaM 'nApekShyate' tattvaj~nAnakAraNaM na bhavatItyarthaH | na chAprayojakatA | 'hi' yataH 'yathAkAmaM' yathechCham Ishvaro na svatantraH chetanatvAt devadattavat | jaDa AtmA vastutvAdityAdirUpeNa na tattve atattvespi anumAtuM shakyate | ataH anena pratyakShAdiviruddhasyApi pramANatve chetanatvavastutvAderapi pramANatvaM syAt avisheShAditi vipakShe bAdhakatarka ukto bhavati | sUtre 'kAmAt' ityekadeshotkIrtanena yathAkAmAditi samagrashabdo lakShyate jyotishshabdena jyotiShTomashabdavat ityAshayena yathAkAmamityuktam | hItyanena paJNchamI vyAkhyAtA | 'tattve' ityanenAsminnityasyAkarShosdhyAhAro vA j~nApitaH | 'anumAnam' ityanena 'nAnumA' iti bhinnapadatvaM 'pR^ithak' ityanena naJNo viruddhArthakatvamAshritya 'nAnumA' ityaikapadyaM cha sUchitam | 'nApekShyate' ityanena nashabdaghaTitasamAsa- maN^gIkR^itya 'nApekShA' ityaMsho vyAkhyAtaH | smR^ityanusAreNa sUtre bhAShye cha tattvaj~nAnAsAdhanatvaprakaTanAya parAbhimatA- numAne sAdhanagocharechChAviShayatvaniShedhaH | tathA chAyaM sUtrArthaH - 'anumA' anumAnatvena parAbhimatamabhedasAdhaka- manumAnam 'asmiMstattve' tattvaj~nAnArthaM 'nApekShA' na apekShA yasyAM sA tathAktA tattvaj~nAnakAraNaM na bhavati | kuta etat?  yataH iyamanumA 'nAnumA' pratyakShAdiviruddhAnumA | tadviruddhAspi sadanumA kiM na syAt?  na syAt | kutaH?  'yathAkAmAt' asyAH | kAma ichChA tadanusAripravR^ittimattvAt | tathA cha pratyakShAdiviruddhAyA api prAmANye uktarItyA atattvaviShaye pravR^ittAyA anumAyA api prAmANyaM syAt, avisheShAditi bhAvaH | yata evamato na dvaitashruteranumAnavirodhospIti |
(36) atraiva smR^itisammatimAha - uktaM cheti || chaH samuchchaye | na kevalaM sUtrakR^itA, skAndespyuktamiti | kimuktamityatastatpaThati - yatheti | padArthAnativR^ittyarthosyaM yathAshabdaH | liN^gamArSham | yadvA - nAyamavyayIbhAvaH, kintvanatikrAntaH kAmo yayeti bahuvrIhisamAsaH | pravartata iti sheShaH | apavR^ittaM viruddhaM gaM gamanaM yasyAH sA apagA, na apagA anapagA iti vigrahaH | tathA cha yasmAt 'anumA' 
shrutyAdiviruddhaM pR^ithaganumAnaM 'yathAkAmA' kAmamanatikramya pravartate | puruShechChAnusAreNa pravR^ittimatIti yAvat| tasmAt 'shruteranapagA' shrutyanukUlA tadaviruddhaiva sA 'pUrvAparAvirodhAya' shruteH pUrvottaravAkyavirodhaparihArArtham 'iShyate' apakShyate | na kevalamatIndriyArthatattva- nishchayAyeti chashabdArthaH | kvachidanyathA chet yatra shrutyAdyAnukUlyaM tadavirodhaH, pUrvottarAvirodhAya tattvanishchayAya cha kAraNatayeShyate | nAnyathA nAnyA pR^ithaganumA kvachidvAkyespi | kutaH? yat sA anumA kevalAnumA yathAkAmA tasmAditi yojyam | yathAkAmAnumetyekaM padaM vA | yathAkAmA cha sAnumeti vigrahaH | tathAtve - yasmAdeShAsnapagA na tasmAtsA noktaphalArthamapekShyate | 'anyathA' yuktiM vinA netyAvR^ittyAsnvayaH | ata eva sudhAyAM 'yathAyogyA- khilaj~natA' ityekaM padamityuktam | itishabdasya skAnda ityanenAnvayaH |
(37) spaShToktitvAtprathamaM smR^itimupanyasyAtraiva arthe shrutisammatiM chAha - naiSheti | Aspaneyetyatra A apeti vichChedaH | viruddhArthayorupasargayoH krameNa sambandhaH | tathA cha 'eShA' parabrahmaviShayA 'matiH' shuShkatarkeNa 'AneyA' utpAdyA 'apaneyA' nirAkAryA cha na bhavatItyarthaH | 'proktAsnyena suj~nAnAya preShTha' iti vAkyasheShaH | preShTheti nachiketasaM prati yamasya sambuddhiH | 'anyena' anyatvaj~nAninA jIveshvarAdibhedaj~nAninA bhagavadbhaktyAdimateti yAvat| AchAryeNa 'proktA' tadupadesAjjAtA 'suj~nAnAya' syAdityarthaH | iti cheti chaH samuchchaye | tathA cha iti kaThashrutau choktamiti sambandhaH |
(38) nanvastvAnandamayena brahmaNA hiraNyagarbhAdijIvAnAM bhedaH | tathApi saH vyAvahArikaH saMsAra evAsti, na pAramArthiko muktAvapi | udAhR^itashrutInAM sAMsArikabhedaparatvopapatterityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtraM paThati - asminniti| atrAsyeti nAnandamayaparAmarshaH | kintu netara ityuktajIvasyetyAha - asyeti | asyAnyasya cheti pratItinirAsAya chashabdaM vyAkhyAti yuktIti | astIti sheShaH | kiM tadyogashAsanamityata Aha - sosshnuta iti | kriyA- visheShaNametat | luptavibhaktiko vA nirdeshaH | tathA cha 'ityAdi shAsti' ityAdinA shAstIti vAsnvayaH | anena na kevalaM bhedavyapadeshAdAnandamayena jIvAnAM bhedaH siddhaH | kiM nAma? yatossmin prakaraNe asya jIvasyAnenAnandamayena saha 'asmiMshcha' mokShespi 'yogaM' sambandhaM shrutiH shAsti atospi | ato na tadaikyaM jIvAnAM nApi sAMsArika eva bhedaH | na chaitAvatA kathaM bhedasiddhiH | sambandhasya bhedasApekShatvAt | yadvA - yasmAt 'asmin' prakaraNadvayespi 'asya' jIvasya 'tadyogaM' tairAnandamayAdyairyogaM sambandhaM 'shAsti' pratipAdayati phalatvena shrutiriti sheShaH | tasmAdAnandamayo na jIvakoshAdiriti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | 'saH' brahmaj~nAnI 'vipashchitA' sarvaj~nena 
j~nAtenaiva 'parabrahmaNA' chaturmukhena cha saha 'sarvAn' svayogyakAmAn 'ashnute' muktau prApnotIti shrutyarthaH | 'adR^ishyesnAtmye' iti vAkyaM tu prAgeva vyAkhyAtam | dehAdutkrAnto jIvaH 'etam' 'AndamayaM' pUrNAnandaM paramAtmAnaM 'upasaN^krAmati' tatsamIpaM prApnotItyanuvAkAntaragatatR^itIyavAkyasyArthaH ||
|| ityAnandamayAdhikaraNam ||
|| 7. antassthatvAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe adhidaivagatAnyatraprasiddhendrAdinAmasamanvasiddhyarthaM dehAntasthatvarUpaliN^gasamanvayaH kriyata iti shAstrAdhyAyapAdasaN^gatayaH siddhA ityAshayena pUrvAdhikaraNatadviShayavAkyasaN^gatI darshayati - adR^ishya iti || pUrvAdhikaraNodAhR^ite 'adR^ishye anAtmye' iti vAkye Anandamayasya kArtsnyenAj~neyatvarUpamadR^ishyatvamuktamityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha - tachcheti | chashabda evArthe| tathA cha yatpUrvoktamadR^ishyatvaM tadeva 'antaHpraviShTam' iti vAkye na vijAnantItyanena kasyachidantasthasyochyate | devAj~neyatvAtkaimutyena pratipAdyata ityarthaH | anenAntasthatvamukhenA- dR^ishyatvAnandamayatvayoranyaniShThatvAkShepAt pUrvAdhikaraNenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | hR^idayaguhAntaHpraviShTaM jagatkartAraM chandramasyantarmanasA svechChayA charantaM sahaiva sthitam etaM devAstattvAbhimAninaH kArtsnyena na vijAna- ntIti shrutyarthaH | pUrvapakShe tviyamanyaparA | tatra sayuktikaM pUrvapakShamAha - sa cheti | chashabdosvadhAraNe | anya ityAvartate | tathA cha sosntasstho viShNoH 'anyaH' anya eva bhavet, kutaH?  'indro rAjA' ityAdivAkyairyatos- nyosntaHsthatayA pratIyate ata iti yojanA | Adishabdena
apAM netAraM bhuvanasya gopAm |
tvaShTAraM rUpANi vikurvanti vipashchim |
brahmendramagniM jagataH pratiShThAM diva AtmAnaM savitAraM bR^ihaspatim |
chaturhotAraM pradishosnuklR^iptaM vAcho vIryaM tapasAsnvavindat |
ityAdi varuNatvaShTragnyAdiprapakatattachChrutiliN^ghaTitataittirIyavAkyAni gR^ihyante | pUrvapakShaphalamAha - tasmAditi | idaM chAvartate | prasajyata iti sheShaH | tathA cha 'tasmAt' antasthasya viShNvanyatvAt 'saH' adR^ishyosnya eva prasajyate | tasmAdanyasyAdR^ishyatvAt 'sosnya eva' indrAdyanyatamaAnandamayaH prasajyate na viShNuriti yojanA | rAjA ya indro jagataH 'Ishe' IShTe jagadIshvaratvena vartata ityarthaH | yasmAdIshe IShTe tasmAjjagato rAjeti vA | etaduttarasya 'saptahotA' iti padasya sapta buddhIndriyANi viShayeShu jIvena juhotIti saptahotA | viShayAnandriyaiH jIvena vetyarthaH| 'sapta yuà¤¼JNjanti' iti vAkye AdyArdhasya 'sapta' ChandAMsi gAyatryAdIni 
ashvarUpANi 'ekachakraM' sUryarathaM prati svAtmAnaM yuJNjanti rathe yuktAni bhavantItyarthaH | saptachChandosbhimAninA pR^ithagvedAbhimAnI saptachChando nAmA ekaH pradhAnosshvossti | 'ChandosbhimAninA pR^ithagvedAbhimAnI saptachChando nAmA saptasvekossti' iti tattvapradIpokteH | ata eva 'sapta yuJNjanti .... eko ashvo vahati saptanAmA' ityanayorna virodhaH | sUryarathachakrasya sthitimAha - trinAbhIti | trirAvR^ittamAsachatuShTayAtmakanAbhitrayopetam 'ajaraM' sadA dR^iDham arvashabditebhyo vAjibhyo dUrasthatvAdanarvaM chakraM sUryarathasyAstItyarthaH | chakrasya mAnasottaragirishikharavalayaparivartitvAt arvatAM merumAnasottaramadhyAkAsha- gAmitvAddUrasthatvaM yuktam | yena 'yatra' chakre 'imA' imAni vishvAni sarvANi bhuvanAni 'tasthuH' sthitAH ityuttarArdhasyArthaH | jagataH 'pratiShThAm' AshrayaM 'chaturhotAram' antaHkaraNachatuShTaye viShayANAM hotAraM 'pradishaH' pratidisham 'anuklR^iptaM' vyavasthitaM 'vAchaH' vedasya 'vIryaM' sAraM mukhyArtham 'indram agniM' 'divo' devyAH 'AtmAnaM' svAminaM vAyuM 'savitAraM bR^ihaspatiM' 'brahmA' hiraNyagarbhaH tapasA 'anvavindat' labdhavAnityarthaH | siddhAntayati - itIti ||
(2) kuto na mantavyamityatastatra hetutvena sUtramupanyasya vyAchaShTe - antariti || sUtresntarityuddeshyabhAge apekShitaM padamadhyAhR^itya darshayati - shrUyamANa iti | antassthatvena shrutyochyamAna ityarthaH | vidheyasamarpakasyAnuvR^ittasya tattu, ityasyArthamAha - viShNureveti | taittirIyopaniShadgatabhinnabhinnavAkyodAharaNapUrvakaM hetvaMshaM vyAchaShTe - antariti| ityAdIti | tasya dharmAstaddharmAH teShAmupadesho vachanaM ityAdirUpashchAsau taddharmopadeshashcha ityAditaddharmopadeshaH tasmAdityarthaH | yadvA - luptavibhaktikosyaM nirdeshaH | tathA chetyAderupadeshAdityarthaH | samudAyaikavachanametat | anena 'antaHpraviShTam' iti vAkye 'antaHshrUyamANo' hR^idayAntassthatvena shrutyukto viShNureva, na tvanyaH | kutaH?  tasya viShNordharmANAM kShIrapralayAbdhisthatvabrahmaj~neyatvabrahmatapolabhyatvabrahmANDavIyatvAdirUpANAM 'tasmin' antaHshrute tenAnta- rityAdinA 'upadeshAt' uktatvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | upadeshAdityantasya sUtrasya tasmAdanya eveti na mantavyamityanenAnvayaH | 'brahmA' vartamAnachaturmukhaH 'samudre' pralayAbdhau kShIrAbdhau cha 'antararNe' jale kShIre cha 'manasA' svechChayA saJNcharantaM 'dashahotAraM' j~nAnakarmAkhyadashendriyeShu viShayahotAraM tattadviShayasthApakaM dashendriyANi jIvena viShayeShu juhvataM vA viShNum 'anvavindat' vyajAnAt | 'kavayo' j~nAninaH 'samudre' kShIrapralayAbdhyorantaHsthitaM vichakShate jAnanti | 'vedhaso' bhUtabhaviShyadbrahmANaH 'marIchirmitaruktvataH' iti ChAndogyabhAShyokteH | pramitaruktvanimittAt marIchipadoktAnAM jIvAnAM padam AshrayaM viShNum ichChanti prArthayanti | tattvapradIparItyA 'kavayaH' santaH 'vedhaso' vichakShate vichakShaNAya 
j~nAnAya marIchInAM padaM viShNum ichChantItyekAnvayo vA | kavayaH 'aNDakoshaM' brahmANDAkhyasthAnaM 'yasya' viShNoH 'shuShmaM' vIryaM tadupAdAnakamAhuriti shrutyarthaH | viriJNchivAkyasyAsya 'prANa ulbaM tena klR^ipto amR^itenAhamasmi' iti vAkyasheShaH | tasya 'ulbaM' jarAyuH 'prANaH' antaHprAvaraNaM yena sahaiva jAyate | 'tena' amR^itena 'ahaM' klR^iptossmItyarthastattvapradIpesbhihitaH | kShIrasamudrasthatvasya viShNuliN^gatvaM kuta ityata Aha - sa hIti | 'saH' viShNuH hishabdena lokaprasiddhatvAditi hetu sUchitaH |
(3) astu viShNoH kShIrAbdhisthatvaM liN^gaM prasiddhatvAt, tathAspi pralayArNavasthatvasya brahmANDavIryatvasya cha kuto viShNudharmatvamityatastayorviShNudharmatve pramANaM vaktuM pratijAnIte - tasyeti | 'aNDakosho' brahmANDAkhyasthAnaM 'tasya' viShNorvIryamityarthaH | chashabdAtsaH pralayasamudrashAyIti pratij~nA sUchyate | tasyaivetyavadhAraNe vA chashabdaH | tathAtve pratij~nAntaramupalakShaNIyam | ata eva pralayAbdhishAyitve 'Apo nArAH' iti pashchAtpramANopanyAsaH shrutAvaNDakoshashabdashravaNespi pratyayasya svArthikatvAttattyAgenANDakosha ityevAnUditam | shrutAvapi tathaiva Chedo vA | 'saH' vAsudevAt jAto viShNuH 'svAt' svakIyAchCharIrAt vividhAH prajAH 'sisR^ikShuH' sraShTumichChuH 'abhidhyAya' vichintya 'Adau' aNDasR^iShTeH pUrvameva 'apaH' tadAvaraNarUpAH sasarja | tAsvapsu vIryam 'avAsR^ijat' nyadhAt mAyAdvAreti sheShaH | 'haimaM' hiraNyAtmakaM 'sahasrAMshusamaprabhaM' sUryasamaprakAshaM 'tat' vIryaM brahmANDAkhyamabhavat | 'yasmin' aNDe 'sarvalokapitAmaho' brahmA chaturmukhaH 'svayaM' svatantrAt hareH sAkShAjjaj~ne ityarthaH | yataH Apo 'narasUnavaH' narasya viShNossUnavaH | 'viShNurnaro nAshAtparo yataH' iti bhAgavatatAtparyokteH | ato nArAH proktAH yena kAraNena 'pUrvaM' pralaye 'tAH' ApaH tasya viShNoH ayanaM 'tena saH nArAyaNaH smR^itaH' tachChabdavAchyatvena smR^ityukta ityarthaH | yadyapi -
puruShosNDaM vinirbhidya yadAdau sa vinirgataH |
AtmanosyanamanvichChannapossrAkShIchChuchiH shuchIH ||
iti bhAgavate |
aNDaM praviShTo yo viShNuH sosNDaM bhittvA prakAshitaH |
sospossR^ijattato nArA .... |
iti bhAgavatatAtparye chANDasR^iShTyanantaram apsR^iShTiruchyate | tathAspi sA bahiHsR^iShTeranyAssntareti na virodhaH | itItyasya 'tasya cha vIryamaNDakoshaH, sa hi pralayasamudrashAyI yataH' iti pUrveNAnvayaH |
(4) itashcha brahmANDajanakavIryatvaM pralayasthatvaM cha tasyaiva j~nAyata ityAha - ahamiti | 'tripuruShaM 
mAyAbIjamajAyata' iti vAkyasheShaH | taditi vyAptivachanossarvanAmashabdaH | athavA sarvanAmashabdaH, ata eva TIkAyAM tadaheyamiti vyutkramaH kR^itaH | tathA cha tatprasiddhaM vyAptaM vA 'aham' aheyaM ratiH shaM cha mitamasyeti rashmirjIvaH tamindayati prerayatIti rashmIt jIvaprerakaM, inda preraNe iti dhAtoH ayaM dakArAntaH shabdaH | anukR^ityadhikaraNe tu - indhI dIptAviti dhAtuvyAkhyAnAt rashmIt bhagavadapekShayA rashmirUpANAm alpAnAM sUryAditejasAM prakAshakamiti vyAkhyAtam, tatra dhakArAntosgnIchChabdavadayaM shabdo j~nAtavyaH |  'tejaH' jagatprakAshakaM 'puruShaM' pUrNaShaDguNaM nArAyaNaM tadAkhyaM brahma teja iti vA | 'agrataH' pralaye 'jAtaM' sthitaM tasmAnnArAyaNAkhyapuruShAt 'agrataH' prathamaM 'prakR^itiH' chetanA jAyate gachChatIti jagat jIvasamudAyaH, jAtamityasyobhayatra yathAyogyaM sambandhaH | janishcha yathA yogyA grAhyA | pashchAt 'aNDaM cha' 'tripuruShaM' brahmavAyurudrAkhyapuruShatrayayuktaM 'mAyAbIjaM' prakR^ityupAdAnakam ajAyateti tattvapradIpadishA shrutyarthaH | chaturvedashikhAyAm ityasya vachanAdityadhyAhAreNa tasyetyanenAnvayaH |
(5) yadyevaM samudrasthatvAdiliN^gAdantasstho viShNuH, tarhi tenAntassthena viShNunA indrAdInAmabhedostra vivakShitosstu | indrAdiprApakakashrutyAderapi sadbhAvAt | shrutyAdeshcha svabhAvato liN^gasya niravakAshatayA balavattve- nAnyatarabAdhenAnyatarapakShanirNayAyogAt | evaM cha pUrvottarapakShadvaye anyonyaM bAdhyabAdhakabhAvashUnye sati tadanyathA- nupapattyA antaHsthena viShNunendrAdInAmabhedaH prApta ityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtraM paThitvA vyAchaShTe - bhedeti | taittirIye - 'indrasya' ityeko bhedavyapadeshaH | 'vAyoH' ityanyaH | 'antaH' ityaparaH | 'devAnAm' iti chetaraH | Adishabdena 'amR^itaM devAnAmAyuH prajAnAmindraM rAjAnaM savitAram' ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | vyapadeshAdityasyAnya iti sautrapratij~nayAnvayaH | anena sUtre vidheyasamuchchayArthakachashabdasya bhinnakrameNa anvayena na kevalamantashshrUyamANo viShNuH, kintvindrAdibhyosnyashcha | kutaH?  tasyendrAdyantaryAmitvadantassthatvakathanena tebhyo bhedokteriti sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | atra shrutAvindrashabdosnyaparaH; ShaShThIshravaNAt | 'indro rAjA' ityAdau tu indrAdishabdAH paramamukhyavR^ittyA viShNuparA eva, bAdhakAbhAvAt | tathA cha mano vihAya paJNchasu j~nAnendriyeShu shabdAdiviShayahotA tairviShayAnubhAvakaH | indrasyAtmA antaryAmI AdAnAdikartA vA | sarvahR^idayeShu 'nihitaH' sannihitaH 'kavayo' j~nAninaH 'vAyorAtmAnaM nichikyuH' dadR^ishuH AdityesntaH 'manasA' svechChayA saà¤¼JNcharantaM viShNuM kavayaH anvavindan | 'brahmA' chaturmukhaH devAnAM hR^idyayanAt sthiteH pravartanAdvA hR^idayaM viShNum 'anvavindat' apashyaditi shrutyarthaH |
|| ityantassthatvAdhikaraNam || 7 ||
||  8.AkAshAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe bhagatavi lokatosnyatraprasiddhAkAshapadopalakShitAdhibhautikAsheShashabdasamanvayaH 
kriyate | phalakathanena pUrvapakShaH sUchito bhavatItyAshayena pUrvapakShaphalamAha - ko hIti || itIti | ityAnandamayAdhikaraNodA- hR^itavAkyenetyarthaH | tushabdasyAkAshasya tviti sambandhaH | tathA cha Chandogashrutyu- ktAkAshAbhinnAkAshasyaivetyarthaH | 'Anandamayatve' pUrNAnandatvena nimittena AnandamayashabdavAchyatve 'hetuH' lokacheShTakatvarUpaH | tushabdArthaivakAra- vyAvartyamAha - neti | anena viShNubhinnabhUtAkAshasyaiva Chandoga- shrutyuktAkAshashabdavAchyatvamiti pUrvapakShe 'ko hi' iti taittirIyashrutyuktospi sa eveti taduktahetunA tasyaivAnandamayatvaM sidhyati, na viShNoriti phalamuktaM bhavati | pUrvasaN^gatistvadhikAshaN^kAM kR^itvAstra pUrvanyAya evAtidishyata ityAtideshikI draShTavyA |
(2) siddhAntayati - itIti || kuto na mantavyamityAshaN^kAyAM tatra hetutayA sUtramupAdatte | yata iti | idaM chAvartate | tatrAdyasya 'yatashchodeti' itivat kuta ityarthaH | 'yachChabdastu parAmarshe prashnArthespi bhaNyate' iti bhAgavatatAtparyokteH | dvitIyastu na mantavyamiti pratij~nAyAM sUtrArthasya hetutvadyotakaH | viShayAdeH pUrvapakShaphalakathanena sUchanespi mukhatosnukteH tadanuvAdapUrvakaM sUtraM vyAchaShTe - asyeti | 'ityatra' vAkye pratipAdyatvasyeti sheShaH | chospyarthaH | yadyapi tathApItyarthe | 'asau' AkAshostra vAchya iti sheShaH| sUtresnuvR^ittasya 'tattu' ityasyArtho viShNureveti | ityAdIti | luptavibhaktiko nirdeshaH AdishabdAt 'sarvANi bhUtAni' ityAdijagatkAraNatvapratipAdakaM vAkyaM gR^ihyate | yathoktaM tattvapradIpe - "sarvANi bhUtAni' ityAdinA udIryamANaM jagadutpAdakatvAdikamAdishabdA- dupAdadIta" iti | liN^gapadaM shrutyupalakShakam | tathA chetthaM yojanA-yadyapi 'asya lokasya' iti ChandogavAkye bhUtAkAshasya shrutyAdibalAdasti pratipAdyatvasya prAptiH | tathAspi nAsAvatra vAkye AkAshapadena vAchyo yujyate, kintu - viShNureva | kutaH?
