'sa eShaH' ityAdivAkye 'talliN^gAt' tasya viShNorliN^gamasAdhAraNadharmaH parovarIyastavAdiH | tasya tasminnAkAshe shravaNAduktatvAt | yata evaM talliN^gAt asau ChandogashrutyuktAkAsho viShNureva, tata eva 'ko hi' iti taittirIyavAkyespyasAveva pratipAdyata iti tasyaivAnandamayatve heturukto na tu bhUtasya| ato bhUtAkAshasyAnandamayatve heturuktaH, na tu viShNoriti na mantavyamiti | anena sUtrayojanA darshitA| asyetyAderayamarthaH - 'asya' pratyakShasiddhasya pR^ithivIlokasya tadabhimAninashchaturmukhasya 'kA gatiH' Ashraya iti shilakena pR^iShTaH pravAhaNo rAjA AdIptatvAdAkAshanAmako viShNuriti pratyuvAcha | kathamityA- kAN^kShAyAM tadupapAdanAya tasyAkAshasya mahimAnamAha - 'sarvANi havA imAni bhUtAnyAkAshAdeva samutpadyante AkAshaM pratyastaM yanti AkAsho hyevaibhyo jyAyAnAkAshaH parAyaNaM sa eSha paro varIyAnudgIthaH sa eShosnantaH' iti | atra vaishabdasya prasiddhidyotakasya sannihitasarvabhUtAnvaye vA, 'syurevaM tu punarvaivetyavadhAraNavAchakAH' ityabhidhAnAdavadhAraNArthatvaM vA draShTavyam | bhUtashabdo bhUtAkAsha evAtrochyate iti pUrvapakShe AkAshavyatiriktabhUtaparaH | siddhAnte tu sarvabhUtaparaH | brahmAdisarvajagatparo vA | tathA cha 'sarvANImAni' pramitAni AkAshAdibhUtAni brahmAdijagadvA AkAshAdeva samutpadyante | 'havai' prasiddhaM hi | 
AkAshaM 'pratyastam' adarshanaM 'yanti' tatraiva pralaye muktau cha lInAH bhavanti | kutaH?  'hi' yasmAdAkAsha eva 'ebhyo' brahmAdibhyo 'jyAyAn' adhikottamaH | kuta etat?  yata AkAshaH 'parAyaNam' uttamAshrayaH naitasmAduttamaM vastvAshaN^kyamiti bhAvenAha - sa iti | 'sa eShaH' AkAshanAmA bhagavAn 'parovarIyAn' atra -
parasmAduttamaM proktaM paro iti tataH param |
parovaraM paraM tasmAtproktaM pArovarIyakam ||
iti sAmasaMhitAvachanAnusAreNAdau para iti shabdAntarasya madhye varashabdAntarasya cha AvApena vR^ittivAkye subAdeshasya sorulopena rutvotvaguNeShu samAne pare optashabdadvayasya lope chottamottamottama ityartho j~nAtavyaH | 'udgIthaH' uchchatvena gIta ukto vedena | takArasya thakAro vyatyayAt | 'sa eShaH' AkAshaH 'ananto' deshakAlaguNairaparichChanna iti | ChAndogyabhAShye tu 'uchchatvAdgIthatvAtsarvasthAna- sthatvAdudgItho bhagavAn' iti vyAkhyAtam |
(3) 'sa eShosnantaH' ityuktAnantatvasyAparimitatvasya viShNuniShThatvaM kuto j~nAyata ityata Aha-viShNoriti| viShNorvIryANi 'kaM' kosnu ko vA 'pravocham' prAvochat | sAkalyena pravakti na kospi | 'yaH' kaH kavirbahmA 'pArthivAni rajAMsi' pArthivaparamANUn 'vimame' gaNayati | sospi na pravaktIti shrutyarthaH| 'parovarIyAn' ityuktasarvottamatvasya viShNudharmatvaM kuta ityata Aha - para iti | atra 'na te mahitvamanvashnuvanti' iti uttaravAkyAduktArtho j~nAyate | ata evAdishabda ubhayAnvayI | tatrAdyo 'viShNornu vIryagaNanAM katamosrhatIha yaH parthivAnyapi kavirvimame rajAMsi' iti smR^itigrAhI | vyAkhyAteyaM shrutirjanmanaye | ityAdinA vAkyeneti sheShaH | yadyapi shrutyanusArAtsarvottamatve prathamaM pramANaM vaktavyaM na tu anantatve | ata eva TIkAyAmAdau sarvottamatvaM gR^ihItam| tathAspi anantatvasya sAvakAshatvashaN^kA- viShayatvAtprathamaM tatra pramANopanyAsaH | ata eva tatraivottaratra smR^ityA sAvakAshatvashaN^kAparihAraH | 'tasya' viShNoH hishabdo yata ityarthe | 'tat' anantatvAdi 'liN^gaM' dharma ityavagatam| ato na hetuvisheShaNAsiddhiriti vAkyasheShaH | evakArapAThe nAnaikAntyamiti sheShaH | uttaratrAnvayo vA| yadyapi 'anantaH' iti shrutiH; vAchakashabdatvAt | tathAspi tatpadapravR^ittinimittasya liN^gatvamapyaviruddham |
(4) nanvanantatvam 'anantAkAshavatpashyan' ityAkAshasyApi smaryate, ataH sAvakAshatvAtkathaM viShNoreva talliN^gamityataH smR^itimAha - ananta iti | Anandeti luptavibhaktiko nirdeshaH| viShNurevaiko mukhyatayA prochyata iti sambandhaH | 'pareShAM' viShNoranyeShAm 'upachArataH' svasvasamIpagataparamAtmasambandhAdeva vAchyateti sheShaH | iti brAhma ityasya tasyaiva talliN^gamityuktamiti pUrveNAnvayaH | anenaivakAro liN^gasya niravakAshatvaj~nApaka iti sUchitam |
(5) nanu shrutyA pUrvapakShite kathaM liN^gena nirNayaH | liN^gasya shrutito durbalatvAdityataH AkAshashrutirviShNau sAvakAsheti shrutyA darshayati - nAmAnIti | 'cho' yato 'nAmAni sarvANi' iti vAkyena viShNorAkAshAdisarvashabda- vAchyatvamuktam, ato liN^gena shruterbAdhayA nirNayo yukta iti yojanA |
|| ityAkAshAdhikaraNam || 8 ||
|| 9. prANAdhikaraNam || 
(1) atrAdhikaraNe lokatosnyatra prasiddhAdhyAtmikAsheShashabdopalakShakapraNashabdasya brahmaNi samanvayaH kriyate | sarvatrAdau sUtraM pAThyam | pashchAtsaN^gatyAdikaM vaktavyamiti sUchayitumatra sUtramAdAveva paThati - ata eveti |
(2) viShayavAkyodAharNapUrvakaM pUrvAdhikaraNena saN^gatiM viShayasaMshayau cha sUchayati - taditi || atra yattadorAvR^ittiH | bhujyata iti bhogaH AnandaH | tena tadvAnupalakShyate, dharmAdharmiNorabhedavivakShA vA | tathA cha he viShNo 'yat' yasmAt 'prajApateH' hiraNyagarbhasya tadupakShitAnAM sakalajIvAnAM 'bhujaH' bhogAn yogyA- nandAn 'kariShyamANaH' upalakShaNametat - kurvANoskArShIshcha | 'tasmAttvaM' 'mahAn bhogaH' pUrNAnandavAnabhavaH| svasya mahAbhogAbhAve parasmai taddAnAnupapatteH | yasmAchcha pAyuguhyaikyena navendriyAbhimAnino devAn tvaM 'prANayaH' acheShTayaH| idamapyupalakShaNaM - cheShTayasi cheShTayiShyasi cha | tasmAttvaM prANaH prANashabdavAchyosbhava iti siddhAntarItyA shrutyarthaH | pUrvapakShe tvetatsarvaM mukhyaprANe yojyam | itIti | 'iti' taittirIyashAkhAgatavAkye 'paramAnandatvaM' pUrNAnandatva- paryavasitaM 'tadvai tvam' iti vAkye 'mahAbhogashabdena' 'mahAn bhogaH' iti padadvayAtmakavAkyena cha prANasyoktamiti yojanA | anena prANAkhyo viShayaH | tasya viShNvanyatvAkShepamukhenAnandamayatvasyApyanyaniShThatvAkShepAdAnandamayA- dhikaraNenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiH | saH vAyuruta viShNuriti saMshayashcha sUchito bhavati |
(3) sayuktikaM pUrvapakShaM darshayati - sa cheti || tachChabda Avartate | chashabdosvadhAraNe | vAyurityanena sambadhyate | Anandamayashcheti samuchchaye vA | tathA cha paramAnandatvaM yasya prANasyoktaM saH 'prANaH' tachChabdavAchyo mukhyavAyureveti 'Apatati' prApnoti | ata evAnandamayospi sa evetyApatati | kutaH? prasiddheH prANashruteH tasyAshcha tasminvAyau prasiddhe rUDhatvAt | prANapadapravR^ittinimittasya jIvanADihetutvasya cha sharIre sati mukhye jIvanAdikaM sambhavati nAsatItyanvayavyatirekAbhyAM svasharIragatavAyuvikAradvArA mukhyavAyAveva prasiddherdarshanAditi yojanA |
(4) siddhAntayati - na cheti || evaM prANasya vAyutvaM AnandamayatvaM cha na yuktamityarthaH | kuto 
naivamityA- shaN^kAyAM tatra hetutayA sUtraM vyAchaShTe - yata iti | sUtrArthasya hetutvadyotakosyaM yatashshabdaH | sUtresnuvR^ittasya tattvityasyArtho viShNureveti | tathA cha yatosyaM prANo viShNoreva ato naivamityanvayaH | kutosyaM prANo viShNurevetyataH sautraM hetumanUdya vyAchaShTe - ata eveti | ityAdIti | ityAdinoktaM yadviShNuliN^gaM tasmAdevetyarthaH | kathaM shrutyA pUrvapakShite liN^gena nirNaya ityato liN^gasya niravakAshatvaj~nApanAyaivakAraH | tathA cha sAvakAsha- shruterniravakAshaliN^gena bAdha iti bhAvaH | he viShNo 'te' tava shrIshcha lakShmIshcheti dve patnyau staH | vakShasthalAshritA shrIH aN^kasthitA lakShmIriti sampradAyavidaH | tattvapradIpe tu - aN^kasthitA shrIH vakShasi lakShmabhUtA lakShmIrityuktam|  'ahorAtre' tadabhimAnisUryachandrau 'pArshve' pArshvasthitAvityarthaH | divArAtramete pArshvagate iti vA | yadyapIdam 'adbhyaH' iti pUrvAnuvAkagatam | 'tadvai tvaM prANaH' ityetachcha 'bhartA san bhriyamANaH' ityuttarAnuvAkagatam | tathA cha nAnayorliN^galiN^gibhAvo yujyate | tathAspi 'shrIshcha te' iti yuShmachChabdenoktasya 'tadvai tvaM prANaH' ityatrApi yuShmachChabdena pratyabhij~nAnAttadupapattiH | niravakAshatvAdbhinnAnuvAkasthasyApi mukhato grahaNaM yuktam | Adishabdena 'hariM harantamanuyanti devAH | vishvasyeshAnaM vR^iShabhaM matInAm' (tai.A. 3-15.) iti tattvapradIpodAhR^itamanuvAkAntarasthaM gR^ihyate | sarvabuddhiniyantAraM jagatpatiM sarvasaMhartAraM hariM devAH anugachChantItyarthaH | chandrikAyAM tu - 'bhartA san' ityuttarAnuvAkagataM 'tamevamR^ityumamR^itantamAhustaM bhartAraM tamugoptAramAhuH' (tai.A. 3-14.) ityAdikamAdipadena grAhyamityuktam | yadyapi taittirIyashAkhAyAM 'hrIshchate' iti pAThaH | tathAspi vAjasaneyashAkhAbhiprAyeNa evamudAhR^itamiti dhyeyam | sUtrArtastu spaShTaH |
|| iti prANAdhikaraNam || 9 ||
|| 10. jyotiradhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe tattatsUktagatAsheShashabdopalakShakasya lokatosnyatraprasiddhasya jyotirnAmno brahmaNi samanvayaH kriyate | pUrvAdhikaraNatadviShayasaN^gatI viShayavAkyodAharaNapUrvakaM viShayasaMshayau cha darshayati - yo vedeti || tataH kimityata Aha - tachcheti | chosvadhAraNe | tathA cha yatpUrvaM mAntravarNikapadopAttamantravarNagatena 'yo veda' iti vAkyena guhAnihitaM vastUktaM tadevAnandamayAdyAkhyamityuktam | tadeva 'vime karNA' iti vAkye 'jyotiruktaM' jyotishshabdenoktamityarthaH| anena vakShyamANapUrvapakShaparyAlochanayA jyotiSho viShNvanyatvasAdhanamukhenAnandamayatvasyAnya- niShThatvAkShepAdAnandamayAdhikaraNenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiH sUchitA bhavati | jyotirviShayaH kimagniruta viShNuriti sandehashcha sUchito bhavati | 'vi me' iti R^iN^mantre vItyupasargANAM kriyApadenAnvayaH | tatra 
dhAtoreva vicharaNAbhidhAyakatvam | upasargAstu dyotakAH na vAchakAH | ata eva sUtre charaNAbhidhAnAt ityevoktam| bhAShye tu 'vicharaNAbhidhAnAt' iti spaShTArthamuktam | ata eva tattvapradIpe 'spaShTatvAya vicharaNAbhidhAnAt ityuktam' ityuktam| 'me' ityasmachChabdena mantradraShTA R^iShiruchyate | 'dUra AdhIH' ityasya ekapadatvespi avagrahadarshanena dvikhaNDatvAdvibhajyAnvayaH | AN^ IShadabhivyAptyubhayArthakaH | vartata iti sheShaH | tathA cha yato me karNau jyotiSho viruddhaM patayataH patataH | svArthe Nich | chakShushcha viruddhaM patatIti vipariNAmenAnvayaH | yathA karNAderjyotirvidUratvaM evaM jyotiShospi karNAdividUratvamityAha - vIdamiti | kampostyantamityarthe | tathA cha yadidaM hR^idaye 'Ahitam' A samantAt sthitaM jyotistadatyantaM karNAdiviruddhaM vartate | evaM me manaH jyotiSho dUre vicharati atIva taddarshanaviruddhaM vartate | manashcharaNasya tattvaniShThAvirodhitvaM 'chaJNchalaM hi manaH kR^iShNa' iti gItAyAmuktam | ataH kAraNAt 'AdhIH' IShadbuddhirahaM vyAptabuddhirapIti vA 'kiM svit' kiM nu vakShyAmi | kimu kiM vA nu idAnIM 'maniShye' chintayAmIti mantrArthaH | tattvapradIpe tu - A samantAddUrasthabuddhirahamityekAnvayena vyAkhyAtam |
(2) atha sayuktikaM pUrvapakShayati - tachcheti | chassamuchchaye | taditi chAvartate | agnishabdo bhUtataddeva- tAparaH|  dvitIyachashabdo bhinnakramaH | tathA cha tajjyotirguhAnihitaM chAgnireva bhavediti prAptaM, kutaH?  'prasiddheH' jyotishshrutestasyAshcha tasminnagnAveva prasiddheH rUDhatvAt | na kevalaM shruterevedaM jyotiragniH, kintu tasya jyotiShaH 'agnisUktatvAt' agniprakaraNagatatvAchcheti yojanA | ata eva pUrvapakShopasaMhAraTIkAyAM shrutiprakaraNayo- rbalavatvAditi prasiddhapadalakShitAyAH shruteH prathamamuktiH | ata eva chandrikAyAM bhAShye agnisUktasthatvAchcheti chashabda- prayogAdityuktam | tathA cha shrutiprakaraNAbhyAM guhAnihitatvaliN^gamAtrasya bAdhAt agnirevedaM jyotirguhAnihitaM cheti bhAvaH |
(3) siddhAntayatsUtramavatArayati - ata iti || yataH pUrvapakShaH prAptostaH uttaraM sUtramAha bhagavAnbAdarAyaNa ityarthaH | tadeva sUtraM paThati jyotiriti | sUtre tattvityasya anuvR^ittiM vipariNAmaM chAbhipretya pratij~nAMshaM vyAchaShTe - viShNureveti | 'jyotiH' tachChabdavAchyo viShNureva bhavediti yojanA | kuta ityataH prAptaM 'charaNAbhidhAnAt' iti hetvaMshaM charaNashabdasya vicharaNArthatvaM karNAdInAmityasya adhyAhAraM chAbhipretya vyAchaShTe - karNAdInAmiti | atra vAkye karNAdInAmetajjyotiHprati viruddhacharaNokteH karNAdividUratvaliN^gashravaNAdityarthaH | atra karNAdividUratvaM nAma tairiyaditi parichChedAyogyavaibhavatvaM, na tu karNAdividUratvamAtram | tadviShaye tasyAsambhavAt | abhidhAnaparyantadhAvanaM hetvasiddhiparihArAyeti draShTavyam | 
(4) nanvastu jyotiShaH karNAdividUratvoktiH, tAvatA tasya viShNutvaM kuta ityataH karNAdividUratvasya viShNvekaliN^gatve shrutimudAharan tatpratijAnIte - sa hIti || evetyanuShajyate | Adishabdena 'na te viShNo' ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | tathA cha 'hi' yasmAt 'saH' viShNureva 'paro mAtrayA' ityAdivAkyena karNAdividUra iti pramitaH tasmAnnAprayojakatA, na vA hetuvisheShaNAsiddhirityadhyAhAreNa yojanA | anena 'jyotiH' tachChabdavAchyaM brahmaiva | kutaH?  atra  karNAdInAmetajjyotiH prati sAkalyena tadaviShayIkaraNarUpaviruddha 'charaNAbhidhAnAt' karNAdividUratva- liN^gashravaNAt ittyAvR^ittyadhyAhArAbhyAM sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | mApayati j~nApayati viShayAniti vA mIyante viShayA aneneti vA mAtrA indriyagaNaH tayA tatastvaM 'paro' dUrossIti he viShNo anyamahimnaH paramantaM sImAnaM te mahimAnaM kospi shrotrAdinA nApeti cha prakR^itAnuguNyena shrutirvyAkhyeyA | atra tattvapradIpasannyAyaratnAvalIkArayoH jyotirityAdichatussUchI ekamevAntarbhedAdhikaraNamityabhipretam | agnisUktachChAndogyagataviShayavAkyabhedAdanayorbhedaH | TIkAkR^ita- stujyotissUtramekamadhikaraNaM 'ChandaH' ityAditrisUtrI adhikaraNAntaramiti j~nAtavyam || 10 ||
|| iti jyotiradhikaraNam || 10 ||
|| 11. ChandosbhidhAnAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe adhivedagatagAyatryAdyasheShashabdasamanvayaH kriyate | saN^gatyAdijij~nAsAjananAya sUtramevAdau paThati - Chanda iti || atra Chanda ityAvartate | tachcha vyastaM samastaM cha | tathA cha 'ChandosbhidhAnAt' 'gAyatrI vA idam' iti vAkyasthagAyatrIshabdena chaturviMshatyakSharamantravisheShAtmakaChandasaH pratipAdanAt, tachChabdasya tatra rUDhatvAt, gAyatrIshabdavAchyo na viShNuH, kintu Chanda eva | yato gAyatrI na viShNuH, api tu ChandaH, ato jyotirapi na viShNuH kintu ChandaH | kutaH?  'ChandosbhidhAnAt' ChandasA gAyatryA tadaikyAbhiprAyeNa jyotiShosbhidhAnAt upakramAditi chet - na, viShNureva jyotiH | kutaH? 'nigadAt' gAyatrIpadena viShNorevAbhidhAnAt | gAyatryAdi- padairviShNorevAbhidhAnaM cha tadabhedavidhAnArthaM kintu tathopAsanArthamevetyAha - tatheti | 'tathA' gAyatryAdishabdA- rthaguNasvarUpatvena 'chetaso' manasaH 'arpaNAya' brahmaNyAdhAnAyopAsanArthameva viShNornigadAdityarthaH | upAsanetyanuktvA 
chetorpaNetyuktirupAsanAsvarUpa- kathanArthA | anena prasiddhagAyatryAdipadena viShNorabhidhAnaM vyarthamiti shaN^kA parihR^itA| nanu bhavedgAyatrIshabdavAchyatvena viShNorjyotishshabdavAchyatvasAdhanam, yadi gAyatrIshabdavAchyatvaM viShNoH pramitaM syAt | tadeva kuta ityata Aha - tathA hIti | 'hi' yasmAt 'tathA' gAnatrANakartR^itvanimittena viShNo- rgAyatrIshabdavAchyatvasAdhakaM 'darshanaM' dR^ishyate j~nAyatesrtho yayeti vyupattyA 'gAyati cha trAyati cha' (shAkhAntaram) ityAdirUpA shrutirasti tasmAditi sUtrArthaH |
(2) shrutyAdisaN^gativiShayavAkyaviShayasaMshayapUrvapakShatatphalAni sUchayan sUtre pUrvapakShAMshaM vyAchaShTe - atheti || uktasyetyAvartyate | tathA cha 'hR^idaya AhitaM yat' iti guhAnihitatvena yaduktaM tasyaiva 'jyotiShaH' punaH 'atha yadataH paro divo jyotirdIpyate vishvataH pR^iShTheShu sarvataH pR^iShTheShu anuttameShUttameShu lokeShu | idaM vAva tadyadidamasminnantaHpuruShe jyotiH' iti ChAndogyespyuktasya 'gAyatryA' itthaMbhUtalakShaNe tR^itIyA | gAyatrItvena tadrUpatayA 'samArambhaH' pAThaH kR^itaH | kutosyaM vij~nAyate?  yato 'gAyatrI vA idaM sarvaM vAgvai gAyatrI vAgvA idaM sarvam' iti vAkye 'gAyatryA' gAyatrIshabdena tadaikyatAtparyeNa 'samArambhaH' upakramaH kR^itaH ata iti yojanA | tataH kimityata Aha - tasmAditi| idaM chAvartate | jyotirgAyatrIti cha sheShaH | Chanda iti chAnuShajyate | tathA cha yasmAdgAyatryA samArambhaH kR^itaH, sa cha yasmAdanupasaJNjAtavirodhitvena balavAn, tasmAdidaM jyotirgAyatryeva bhavet | sA cha gAyatrI virNasamAvesha- lakShaNamantrAtmakaChanda eva bhavet, na viShNuH | kutaH?  tasmAt gAyatrIshabdasya Chandasyeva rUDhatvAdvAktvA- bhidhAnAchcheti yojanA | anena 'gAyatrI vA idaM sarvam' iti pUrvavAkyasthagAyatrIshabdasya viShNvanyaparatve tata evottaravAkyasthajyotiSho viShNvanyatvApattyA  tata eva agnisUktagatajyotiShospi tadanyatvameva bhavet | ata evAnandamayatvamapi anyasyaiva bhavenna viShNoriti pUrvoktAkShepeNa etadadhikaraNotthAnAtpUrveNAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiH | evaM gAyatrI viShayaH | kiM ChandovisheShaH uta viShNuriti sandehaH | tathA gAyatrI ChandovisheSha eva bhavet; tachChabdasya tatra rUDhatvAditi sayuktikaH pUrvapakShaH | tathA tasmAt jyotirapi Chanda eveti tasyaiva guhAnihitatvamAndamayatvaM cheti pUrvapakShaphalaM cha sUchitaM bhavati | atra pUrvapakShe gAyatryAdishabdAH mantraparAH, sarvamapi vAkyaM tanmAhAtmyaparatayA yojanIyam| siddhAnte tu 'atha' ityAderayamarthaH - bhagavanmAhAtmyAntarArambhesthashabdaH 'yat' shvetadvIpAnantAsa- navaikuNThagataM nArAyaNavAsudevavaikuNThAkhyaM rUpatrayaM tat 'ataH' etasmAdvivakShitAdbuddhisthAt 'divaH paraH' paraM tadapekShayochchasthAnasthitamityarthaH | 'jyotiH' tejomayaM evaMbhUtaM tat 'vishvataH pR^iShTheShu' 
pR^ithivyAM brahmaNo merau vaijayantesntarikShagam |
tR^itIyaM satyaloke cha sadanaM trividhaM matam ||
iti vachanAdantarikShagavaijayantamerusatyalokagatebhyo brahmasadanebhyaH krameNochcheShu 'sarvataH pR^iShTheShu' antarikShapR^ithivI- svarAtmakalokebhyaH krameNochcheShu 'anuttameShu' na vidyate uttamo loko yebhyasteShu pratyavareShviti vA | 'uttameShu' svayamevottameShu 'lokeShu' shvetadvIpAnantAsanavaikuNTheShu 'dIpyate' prakAshate 
'tat' dIpyamAnaM tejaH 'idaM vAva' idaM khalu| idaM cha kim?  'yadidamasmin puruShe' hR^idaye 'antarjyotiH' tachChabditaM brahmAsti tattenaikIbhUtamityarthaH | yo gAyatrInAmA gAyatrIsaMsthaH strIrUpo hayashIrShAkhyo bhagavAn tadidaM prathamaM rUpamityAshayena tasya dvitIyaM rUpaM vaktuM gAyatrItyAdivAkyaM pravR^ittam | 'yadidaM kiJNcha bhUtaM' pUrNaM matsyAdyavatArarUpaM yachcha 'sarvaM' sarvAntaHsthitaM rUpaM tatsarvaM 'gAyatrI' gAyatrInAmA bhagavAneva | vai prasiddham | tasyaiva tR^itIyaM rUpamAha - vAgiti | gAyatrInAmA bhagavAn 'vAgvai' vAN^nAmako viShNureva | kutossya viShNutvamityatastallakShaNayogAdityAha - vAgvA iti | 'idaM sarvaM bhUtaM' prANijAtaM 'vAgvai' vAN^nAmakabhagavadadhInameva | ataH sarvasvAmitvAdvAcho viShNutvamiti | siddhAntasUtrAMshamanukaroti - neti | nigadyata ityatrApi sambadhyate | tathA cha jyotiHshabdena viShNureva nigadyata ityarthaH | kuta ityato nigadAditi hetuM yojayati - hi nigadyata iti | gAyatrIshabdeneti sheShaH | tathA cha 'hi' yasmAdgAyatrIshabdenApi viShNureva 'nigadyate' abhIdhIyate tasmAdityarthaH | viShNorgAyatryAdishabdairabhidhAnaM cha na tadabhedavidhAnArthaM, kintu tathopAsanArthamevetyAha - tatheti | chetosrpaNetyuktiprayojanaM pUrvavat | bhAShyatvaj~nApanAya tathetyAdisvapadAni tathAshabdArthakathanena vivR^iNoti - agnIti | atra jyotishshabdopalakShakAgnipadaM jyotissUtrasya bhinnAdhikaraNatvapakShe anyatra prasiddhasya gAyatrIpadasya viShNau prayoge prayojanamatra vadatA sUtrakR^itA pUrvatrottaratra chAgnyAdipadasya viShNau prayoge prayojanaM sUchitamiti darshayitum | na cha gAyatryAdipadAbhyAmeva gAyatrIpadasamanvayaphalasya pUrvatrottaratra choktasamanvayaphalasya cha sUchanasambhavAdagnipadaM vyarthamiti vAchyam | phalIbhUtasamanvayaviShayatvenAsyApi avashyopA- deyatvAt | samAnaprakaraNasthavAgAdigrAhakatvena AdishabdasyApyAvashyakatvAt | avashyApekShitAbhyAmubhAbhyAmapyAnanda- mayAdyadhikaraNeShu uttaratra choktaprayojanasyApi sUchanasambhavAdubhayamapyAvashyakam | jyotirityAdichatuHsUtryA ekAdhika- raNatvapakShe tu sAkShAtsamanvetavyapashabdatvenaiva shabdadvayopAdAnaM, na tu phalatvenAgnishabdasyAdhikaraNAntarespyeta- nnyAyasUchanaM tu Adishabdenaiva, na tUbhAbhyAm | bhinnajAtIyAnekashabdagrahaNArthaM shabdadvayottarAdipadam | ata eva tattvapradIpe AdishabdasyobhayatrAnvayaM prathamAdishabdena tejaHshabdAnAM dvitIyena ChandashshabdAnAM cha grahaNamabhipretya 'agnyAditejaHshabdAnAM gAyatryAdiChandashshabdAnAM cha' ityuktam| kechittu bhAShyagatahishabdo j~nAnArthamatha dhyAnArthamiti pramANaprasiddhidyotakaH, adhikaraNAntarespyasya nyAyasyAnusandheyatvaj~nApakashchetyAhuH | chetosrpaNArthamiti sAvadhAra- Nam | tathA cha 'asau' bhagavAnagnigAyatryAdishabdairagnigAyatryAdishabdArthaguNasvarUpa iti | tatra 'chetosrpaNArthaM' budhyavatAraNArtham upAsanArthameva nigadyate, na tadabhedavidhAnArthamityarthaH | itItyantena tathAshabdArtha uktaH| anenAprasiddhagAyatryAdipadena viShNorabhidhAnasya vaiyarthyashaN^kA parihR^itA |
(3) nanu bhavedgAyatryAdishabdavAchyatvena viShNorjyotishshabdavAchyatAsAdhanaM yadIyaM gAyatrI viShNuH syAttadeva kuta ityato gAnatrANakartR^itvaliN^gAdityAshayena tasyAsiddhiparihArAya pravR^ittaM tathAhIti sUtrasheSham 
anukR^itya darshanapadoktAM shrutiM darshayati - tatheti || 'hi' yasmAt 'ityAdi darshanaM' shrutirastItyanvayaH | yadyapi 'gAyati trAyate cha' iti pAThaH ChandogAnam, tathAspi shAkhAntara- mevedamityadoShaH | Adipadena 'yA vai sA gAyatrI iyaM vAva sA yeyaM pR^ithivyasyAM hIdaM sarvaM bhUtaM pratiShThitametAmeva nAtishIyate' (ChAM. 3-12.2.) ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | shrutyarthastu - yato gAyatrIvAchyo bhagavAn vedAn 'gAyati' mukhAnnissArayati prathamo vakteti yAvat | yasmAchcha 'trAyate' akhilamiti sheShaH| ato gAyatrIshabdenochyate | 'yA' prasiddhA gAyatrI tannAmA viShNuH 'sA iyaM vai' iyaM khalu | kimiyam?  'yeyaM pR^ithivI' tannAmA bhagavAn | kathaM pR^ithivI viShNurityataH tallakShaNayogAdityAha - asyAM hIdamiti | 'asyAM' pR^ithivyAM 'bhUtaM' prANijAtamAshritamiti | sudhAyAM tu pUrvapakShAnuguNatayA gAyatrI 'gAyati' arthaM pratipAdayati, adhyetR^in 'trAyate' pAlayati pApAt rakShatItyartha uktaH |
(4) nanu gAyatryAdishabdasya anyatra rUDhatvAtkathaM liN^gamAtreNa viShNutvanishchaya ityato gAyatryAdishruteH sAvakAshatvAditi bhAvena gAyatryagnipR^ithivyAdishabdAH na kevalaM shrutyuktayogena viShNau sAvakAshAH, api tu paurANikarUDhyA gAyatryAH bhagavadadhInatvAdapItyAshayena tatra smR^itimAha - sarveti | 'eShaH' viShNuH 'sarvaChandosbhidhaH' sarvaChandasAm abhidhevAbhidhA yasyeti bahuvrIhiH | ChandovAchaka- gAyatryAdisarvashabdavAchyaH | 'evamasau' viShNuH sarvadevatAvAchakAgnyAdishabdavAchyaH | tathA 'eShaH' viShNuH sarvalokavAchakapR^ithivyAdishabdavAchya ityarthaH | kuta ityataH Chanda AdInAM bhagavadadhInatvAditi pratyekaM hetutrayasUchanAya hishabdatrayaM, vedaprasiddhij~nApAnAya vA | ChandasAM lokAnAM cha  pratyakShatvAt devAnAM cha parokShatvAdeShossAviti vichitroktiH | kathaM tarhyanyatra vyavahAra ityata Aha - teShAmiti | ChandodevalokAnAmityarthaH | 'tat' tachChabdabodhyatvam 'upachArato' viShNusamIpe charaNAttadadhInatvAda- mukhyata evetyarthaH| vAmana ityasya 'hi' yato vAmane iti 'darshanaM' pratipAdanamastyataH shrutermukhyavR^ityA  viShNAveva sAvakAshatvAt liN^gasyAmukhyatospyanyatrAnavakAshatvAttena tadbAdhopapatterbhavatyeva gAnatrANakartR^itvaliN^gamAtreNAyaM nirNaya ityupaskareNAnvayaH |
(5) hetvantareNApi gAyatryAH viShNutvaM sAdhayatsUtramupanyasya tadgR^ihItAM shrutimudAharati - bhUtAdIti| itishabdasya bhUtAdItyanenAnvayaH | sUtre bhUtaM vishvamAdiH prathamoddiShTaM yeShu te bhUtAdayaH, te pAdAH yasya gAyatrIpadArthasya sa bhUtAdipAdaH, tasya vyapadeshaH tatpratipAdakaM vAkyaM tasyopapatteH yuktatvAditi vigrahaH | pAdashabdo bhAvapradhAnaH | ata eva bhUtAdipAdatvasyetyuktaM TIkAyAm | evamityasya chobhayatrAnvayaH | tathA cha 'pAdossya sarvA bhUtAni | tripAdasyAmR^itaM divi' ityevaM gAyatryAH 
bhUtAdishabdagR^ihItAmR^itAkhyAMshachatuShTavattvopadeshAt tasya cha viShNAvevopapatteranyatrAnupapattereva gAyatrIshabdavAchyo viShNureva bhavedityarthaH | chashabdasya vyapadeshapadenAnvaye gAyatryA viShNutve sAdhye pUrvasUtre darshanapadoktahetoH etatsUtroktahetudvayasya cha samuchchaye saH | yathAshrutAnvaye tu bhUtAdipAdatvasya viShNuliN^gatvaM na kevalaM viShNorevopapatteH siddham, kintu puruShasUktoktatvAchcheti hetusamuchchaye sa iti j~neyam | ChAndogye  hi 'saiShA chatuShpadA ShaDvidhA gAyatrI' (ChA. 3-12-5.) iti vAkyena yaiShA ShaDvidhA gAyatrI sA chatuShpadetyevaM gAyatrInAmakasya bhagavataH prAguktagAyatrIbhUtavAkpR^ithivIsharIrahR^idayalakShaNaShaDvidhatvamanUdya aMshachatuShTayavattvarUpaM chatuShpAdatvaM vidhAya svoktArtha eva puruShasUktamantraH samAkhyArUpatvenodAhR^ito brAhmaNena 'tadetadR^i- chAsbhyanUktam' (ChAM. 3-12-5.) iti 'tadetat' bhagavatashchatuShpAdatvaM 'R^ichA' R^iN^mantreNa 'abhi' nishshaN^kaM spaShTam 'anu' AnukUlyenoktamityarthaH |
(6) kimuktamityatastanmantraM paThati - tAvAniti ||  yadyapi R^ichi 'etAvAn' iti 'vishvA' iti cha pAThaH | tathAspi shAkhAntarapAThosyamityadoShaH | 'asya' puruShasya 'puruSha evedaM sarvam' (tai.A. 3-12.) ityR^ichA yassarveshAnatvAdirUpaH tAvAnmahimoktaH, na kevalametAvAn, kintu, puruShaH 'tataH' pUrvoktadapi mahimno 'jyAyAn' adhikamAhAtmyopeta ityarthaH | jyAyastvameva darshayati - pAdossyetyAdinA | 'sarvA bhUtAni' sarvaM vishvam 'asya' viShNorekaH 'pAdaH' pAdavatpAdo bhinnAMshaH | yadyapi tattvapradIpe - vishvabhUvidhirbhAti | tathApi TIkAyAM sarvANi bhUtAnyasyaikaH pAda iti pAdavidhAnadarshanAt; chandrikAyAM 'pashvekatvavat vidheyagatatvAtpAdaikatvaM vivakShitam' ityuktatvAchcha, tattvapradIpospyevameva vyAkhyeyaH | asya 'amR^itaM' nAsharahitam ata eva svarUpabhUtaM 'tripAt' trayANAM pAdAnAm aMshAnAM samudAyo nArAyaNavAsudevavaikuNThasaMj~naM triShu rUDhyA dyotamAnatvAchcha dyushabdavAchyeShu shvetadvIpAnantAsanavaikuNTheShu tiShThatIti R^ichoktamityarthaH | yadyapi bhUtashabdo 'bhinnapAdassarvajIvAH' iti ChAndogyabhAShye jIvaparatayA vyAkhyAtaH | tathAspi 'suvarNam' iti shrutyanusAreNa atra vishvArthatayA vyAkhyAtavyaH |
(7) nanu gAyatryAmiva viShNAvapi bhUtAdipAdatvoktiranupapannA | tasya bhUtabhinnatvAdityata Aha - suvarNamityAdi || 'suvarNam' ityArabhya 'bhinnaM cha' ityantamekavAkyatayAsrthakrameNa vyAkhyeyam | yaj~nadattasya, devadattaH, ityuchyate, vishvamiti cha sheShaH | pAda iti chAvartate | chashabdaevArthe hetau cha | ekadeshaparimitamiti hetu- garbhamAvartanIyam | tathA cha 'cho' yataH shrutisthena pAda iti shabdena na bhUtAnAmityamR^itapAdatrayavatsvarUpAMshatvamuchyate| yenAnupapattiH syAt | kintu, yaj~nadattasya chaturbhAgabalo devadatta iti vadbhinnameva vishvam | yataH 'parimitam' viShNupAdaparimitasAmarthyam ataH pAda iti viShNupAdatvenochyate ityarthaH | asyAto viShNau bhUtAdipAdavyapadeshopapatteshchaivamiti pUrveNAnvayaH | tarhi vishvachatuShTayasamo harirityAgatamityatospyAha - pAda itIti| tathA cha yataH shrautapAda iti padena 
chaturbhAgabala itivat na vishvaM viShNusAmarthyasya chaturthAMsha- parimitamityuchyate | kintu, 'ekadeshaparimitaM' viShNusAmarthyaikadeshaparimitamiti ato noktadoSha ityarthaH | kuta etat j~nAyata ityata Aha - suvarNaM koshamiti | 'shruteH' taittirIyashruteH | shrutau tR^itIyArthe ShaShThI, samudAyaikavachanaM chaitat | ata eva 'muktaiH pUrNAm' ityuktaM TIkAyAm | evaM cha tattpradIpaTIkayorekavAkyatayA | pAdamityAvartate | tatraikaM bhAvasAdhanam | na kileti dIrghaH sAMhitikaH | tathA cha ekasmin kapAle 'suvarNaM' tanmayaM 'rajasA parIvR^itaM' rajoguNopalakShitabagnIranabhoshaMkR^inmahattattvaguNatrayaiH parivR^itaM 'virAjaM' brahmaNaH sharIraM, tattvapradIparItyA visheSheNa rAjantamiva 'koshaM' liN^gavyatyayaH, brahmANDAkhyaM yadasti | devAnAM 'vasudhAnIM' dravyanidhAnamaJNjUShAm 'amR^itaiH' muktaiH pUrNAM tAM 'ShaDDhotuH' ShaDindriyeShu viShayAn juhvataH, ShaDindriyANi viShayeShu jIvena juhvato vA, ShaDindriyaiH sArAdanakarturvA, viShNoH 'kalAmu' ekadeshaparimitAmeva 'pAdaM vichakShate' pAdashabdenAchakShate vadanti puruShasUktAdyAgamA iti sheShaH | na kila atra pAdashabdenAN^ghri vadanti, nApi chaturthAMshamityevArthaH | kutaH? yataH sA maJNjUShA 'pAdaM' pAdatvaM chaturthabhAgasAmyaM 'na vivitse' na lebhe kileti shrutyarthaH | sattarkadIpAvalyAm - pAdaM na vivitse iti | pAdasAmyaM na lebhe ityuktam | atra pakShadvayespi puruShavyatyayastulyaH | TIkAkR^itpakShe lakAravyatyayashcha | yadvA - liN^gavyatyayasya ChAndasatvaM koshamityasya dvitIyAntatvaM chopetya strIliN^gapadAnAmapi koshavisheShaNatvenaika evAnvayaH|
(8) syAdetadevaM yadi 'tAvAn' ityasyAmR^ichi viShNurabhidhIyate ityatra pramANaM syAt, tadeva nAsti, ato liN^gamanyaniShThaM bhaviShyatItyataH sautrachashabdena bhUtAdipAdatvasya viShNuliN^gatve sAdhye puruShasUktoktatvAditi yadanumAnaM sUchitaM tasyAprayojakatvamAshaN^kya pariharati - sa hIti || 'hi' yasmAt 'saH' viShNureva 'puruShasUktA- bhidheyaH' tatpratipAdyaH tasmAtsa eva puruShasUktoktabhUtAdipAdospIti yojanA | anyathA bhUtAdipAdatvasya viShNudharmatvAbhAve puruShasUktapratipAdyatvaM na syAditi bhAvaH | yadvA - gAyatryA viShNutve sAdhye sUtre bhinnakrameNA- nvitachashabdasUchitayuktyantaramAha - sa hIti | asya tasmAdgAyAtrI viShNureveti pradhAnapratij~nAvAkyenAnvayaH | chatuShpadetyuktagAyatrIchatuShpAdatvasya puruShasUktamantreNopapAdanAt tatpratipAdyatve tadupapAdyagAyatrIshabdArthatAspi tasyaiva prApnotIti bhAvaH | puruShasUktoktasya viShNutvaM kuta ityata Aha - yaj~neneti | devAH 'yaj~nena' j~nAnakarmAtmakena rudrAkhyapashunA vA 'yaj~naM' viShNum 'ayajanta' apUjayanniti shrutyarthaH | iti yaj~nashabdAditi | iti vAkye yaj~nashabdashravaNAdityarthaH | yaj~nashabdaH kathaM viShNutvanishchAyaka ityato vidvadrUDhyetyAha - yaj~na iti | 'hi' yataH yaj~na iti padena viShNvAkhyA devatAchyata ityarthaH | yadyapi 'yaj~no vai viShNuH' ityadhvaryUNAM shrutiH | tathAspi shrutyantaramidamityadoShaH |
(9) nanu puruShasUktaM na viShNuprakaraNaM, kintvanyaprakaraNameva | na cha yaj~nashrutivirodhaH | pashurUpAnyaprakaraNe tadanyaviShNushruteH ayogAditivAchyam | tasyAH prAsaN^gikatvasambhavAt | na cha tata eva bhUtAdipAdatvasya viShNuliN^gatvanishchayaH | tathAspyasiddhiH | 'pAdossya vishvA bhUtAni' iti shruterbhUtAdipAde yaj~nashruterabhAvAdtyataH puruShasUktoktasya viShNutve smR^itiJNchAha - tasminniti || mahArAjeti kasyachitsambodhanaM rAmavisheShaNaM vA | tathAtve dIrghassyAt | tathA cha he mahArAja 'tasmin' tretAyuge sarvaiH puruShanAmabhI rAma evAbhidhIyate ityarthaH | ata evAMshAdhikaraNe -
nakShatramAnagaNitaM trayodashasahasrakam |
brahmalokasamaM chakre samastaM sarveShAmabhavattadA ||
rAmorAma iti hyAkhyA sarveShAmabhavattadA |
sarvo rAmamayo loko yadA rAmastvapAlayat ||
iti skAnde ityuktaM tattvapradIpe | atra dR^iShTAntamAha - yatheti | yathA kR^itsne pauruShe sUkte viShNureva na tvanyaH | pashuH naraH prAsaN^gikatayAsbhidhIyate ityarthaH | anena siddhasyaiva dR^iShTAntatvAtpuruShasUktasya viShNuparatvaM siddhamiti bhAvaH | skAnda ityantaraM etaduktamiti sheShaH | asya sa hIti purvavAkyenAnvayaH|
(10) uktamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtramupanyasyati - upadesheti || 'upadeshayoH' saptamIpaJNchamIyutavAkyayoH 'upadeshena' gAyatrIjyotiShoH dyusthatvadivaHparatvarUpaviruddhadharmoktyA 'bhedAt' virodhAt na dvayorviShNvAkhyam ekaM vastu pratipAdyaM, kintu bhinnameveti chet - na, kintu 'ubhayasmin' ubhayatrApyupadeshe ekameva pratipAdyaM, katham?  avirodhAt | trisaptalokApekShayA saptamIpaJNchamyoH ekArthatvena virodhAbhAvAditi sUtrayojanAmabhiprayannAkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - tripAditi | 'pUrvopadeshaH'  pUrvoktiH | 'pashchimaH' pashchAttanaH uttara upadeshastadbhinnosstIti sheShaH| virodhasphoraNAya paJNchamyanta ityAdyuktiH | upakramagatasya prAbalyopapAdanAya pUrva ityuktiH | tataH kimityata Aha - tasmAditi | yasmAdevaM bhinnopadeshadvayamasti tasmAdatropadeshadvaye gAyatrIjyotishshabdAbhyAM naikaM vastu viShNvAkhyamuchyate | kutaH?  yatostra 'naikam' anekaM vastu dyusthatvadivaHparatvarUpaM dharmadvayamuchyate | kintvatra 'naikam' anekaM vastudvayamuchyate iti yojanA | siddhAntayatsUtrAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti | nAtra vastudvayamuchyate ityarthaH | kiM tvitisheShaH, ekaM vastUchyate iti anuShajyate | ubhayasminniti sAdhyAntargatam | apishabdo na kevalamekatra, kintUbhayatrApIti samuchchaye | tathA cha kintUbhayasmin apyupadeshe ekameva viShNvAkhyaM vastUchyate iti yojanA | virodhAtkathametadyujyate ityata Aha - trisaptalokApekShayeti | trilokavivakShayA saptalokavivakShayA cha 'avirodhAt' ubhayatrApyekavastvabhidhAne virodhAbhAvAdityarthaH | ayaM bhAvaH - yadA bhUrbhuvassvariti lokatrayavivakShA, 
tadA lakShayojanochChritAntarikShAkhyabhuva uparitanasya sarvasyApi dyutvAt shvetadvIpAnantasanavaikuNaà¥ThAnAM chAntarikShAdupari- tanatvAttatratyaM nArAyaNavAsudevavaikuNThAkhyaM tripAchChabdoktaM rUpatrayaM divitiShThatItyuchyate iti na saptamyantopadesha- virodhaH | na cha 
pR^ithivIstheShu sarvochcho lokosnantAsanAtmakaH |
antarikShAtmakebhyashcha shvetadvIpasthito hariH ||
ityukteranantAsanasya nAntarikShAduparitanateti shaN^kyam | tasya pR^ithivIsthatvespi bahulakShayojanochChritatvenaika- lakShayojanochChritAntarikShAduparitanatvopapatteH | sarvapR^ithivIsthochchatvoktyA tu na pR^ithivIsthAnyochchatvayogovyAvartyate | kintu pR^ithivIsthochchatvAyogaH | yadA tu bhUrbhuvassvarmaharjanaspassatyamiti saptalokavivakShA |  tadendrasadanasya dyutvAt taduchchasyApyuparisthitatvena tatsajAtIyasyavaikuNThasya divaH paratvam |
pR^ithivyAM dyaurmahAmerurAkAshe sUryamaNDalam |
divIndrasadanaM chaiva tatpare tu divaH pare ||
iti smR^itermerorapi dyutvAttaduchchasya bhUspR^iShTatvena tatsajAtIyasyAnantAsanasyApi divaH paratA | evaM sUryamaNDalasyApi dyutvAttaduchchasyoparisthatvena tatsajAtIyasya bhUmeH kiJNchidantaritasya sarvargasamonnatasya shvetadvIpasyApi divaH paratvamastIti na paJNchamyantopadeshavirodhospIti | dyuparatvaM cha sambhAvitasajAtIyadyuparatvamiti na yAvattvayatkiJNchi- ttvamukhena dUShaNAvakAshaH | vaikuNThasya svargalokAtparatvenaiva divaH paratvasiddhAvapi tasya 'sarvataH pR^iShTheShu' ityanenaiva uktatvAt svargatyAgenendrasadanasya dyutvoktiH | na cha lokatrayavivakShayaivAnantAsanAdInAmapi mervAdiparatvena divaH paratvasyApi siddheH saptalokavivakShA vyartheti vAchyam | tathA sati vaikuNThasyApi dyushabdArthaniviShTatvena tasya sarvadyuparatvAsiddhyApatyA 'dvyAtmakebhyashcha sarvebhyo vaikuNThashchochcha uchyate' iti pramANavirodhApAtAt | ChAndogyabhAShye tu -
anantashayanaM chaiva tathAnantAsanaM hareH |
bahulakShochChrite nitye vimAne saMsthitaM yataH ||
chitprakR^ityAtmani yato divIti kathitaM shrutau |
iti pramANabalena chitprakR^ityAtmakAnantAsanashvetadvIpavaikuNThAkhyasthAnatraye saptamyanto dyushabdo dyotamAnatvanimittena yaugikaH, svargAdau tu rUDha iti upadeshayoravirodha iti prakArAntareNa virodha- 
parihAraH kR^itaH || 11 ||
|| iti ChandosbhidhAnAdhikaraNam || 11 ||
|| 12. pAdAntyaprANAdhikaraNam ||
(1) atrAdhikaraNe lokatosnyatra prasiddhaprANanAmno viShNau samanvayaH pratipAdyate | shrutyAdi- saN^gativiShayavAkyaviShayasaMshayasayuktikapUrvapakShAn darshayati - prANa iti || AdyaprANAdhikaraNe 'tadvai tvam' (tai.A. 3-14.) iti vAkyoktaprANo viShNurityuktamityarthaH | tataH kimityata Aha - tatreti | uktamityanuShajyate | tasyAvR^ittivipariNAmau | evaM tatretyapyAvartanIyam | tathA cha 'tatra' tadvai tvamiti vAkye uktasya prANasya viShNutvaM na vidyate na yujyate | kutaH?  yatastatra 'tadvai tvam' iti vAkyoktaprANaviShaye 'ukte' shrute 'tA vA etAH' ityaitareyavAkye uktasya shrutasya prANasya viShNutvaM na vidyata iti yojanA | kuto na vidyate ityata Aha - indriyaissahAbhidhAnAditi | indriyaissaha paThitatvAt indriyagaNe gaNitatvAt ityarthaH | anenaitareyaprANasya viShNvanya- tvAkShepamukhena prAchInataittirIyoktaprANasyApyanyatvAkShepAttenAsyAkShepikI saN^gatiruktA bhavati | aitareyaprANAkhyo viShayaH |  prANosnya uta viShNuriti saMshayashcha sUchitaH | tathA vAyvAdiranya eveti pUrvapakShaH | indriyagaNe gaNita- tvAkhyatatsAdhakaliN^gaM cha sUchitam | 'tA vA etAH' ityetachcha chaturmukhashirasi shirashshabdapravR^ittinimittakathanAya pravR^ittam | vaishabdaH prasiddhau | tathA cha yataH 'tA etAH' chakShuH shrotraM manovAkprANa ityetachChabdavAchyAstadabhimAninyo devatAH | 'shIrShan' shIrShNi shiraHsaMj~nikamUrdhni shritAH | ata eva shrayaNAchChriya iti siddhAnte shrutyarthaH | anena chakShurAdibhiH shritatvaM shiraHpadapravR^ittinimittamityuktaM bhavati | pUrvapakShI tu prANashabdamanyamAtraparaM manyate | siddhAntaya- tsUtramavatArayati - ata iti | yataH pUrvapakShaH prAptaH ata uttaraM sUtramAha bhagavAn bAdarAyaNa ityarthaH |
(2) sUtraM paThitvA tatrAnugamAditi hetvaMshaM shrutyudAharaNena vyAchaShTe - prANa iti || ityAdIti | evamAdi- vAkyoktAnAM devatopadeshyatvAdiliN^gAnAmatrAsmin prakaraNe bahuShu sthaleShu 'anugamAt' anuvR^itterabhyAsAdityarthaH | Adipadena 'prANo hyevaiSha ya eSha tapati' iti sUryamaNDalasthatvapratipAdakavAkyaM gR^ihyate | tathA 'sarvANi bhUtAnyApi- pIlikAbhyaH prANena bR^ihatyA viShTabdhAni' ityAdi vAkyaM cha gR^ihyate |
(3) sautraM tathAshabdaM vyAchaShTe - atrApIti || shruta iti sheShaH | na kevalaM 'tadvai tvam' ityatra, kintvaitareyespIti samuchchayespishabdaH | sUtre anuvR^ittasya tattvityasyArthamAha - viShNureveti | anena yathA 
'tadvaitvam' iti shrutyuktaprANo viShNuH tathaitareyoktospi viShNureva, na tvanyaH | kutaH?  viShNuliN^gAnAM devatopadeshyatvA- dInAmasmin prakaraNe 'anugamAt' anuvR^itterabhyAsAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
aitareye 'taM devAH prANayanta' iti ekakhaNDasthavAkyam | 'taM' nArAyaNaM vAyuM cha devAH 'prANayanta' prakarSheNa shiShyaprashiShyadiShu nItavantaH upadidishurityarthaH | anena viShNoH sarvadevopAsyatvamuktaM bhavati |
'sa eShossuH sa eSha prANaH sa eSha bhUtiH' ityAdyanyakhaNDagataM vAkyam | anena bhUtitvAdinA devAdyupAsyatvamuchyate | 'sa eShaH' bhagavAn duShTanirasanAdasuH prakR^iShTAnandarUpatvAtprANaH devAnAM bhUtishabditaj~nAnA- dyaishvaryapradatvAdasurANAm aj~nAnAdyanaishvaryahetutvAchcha bhUtyabhUtishabdavAchya ityarthaH |
tatraiva 'tA vA etAH sarvA R^ichaH sarve vedAH sarve ghoShA ekaiva vyAhR^itiH | prANa eva prANa R^icha ityeva vidyAt' iti anyadvAkyam | atra prANasyasarvavedoktatvamuchyate | yAstAH etAH sarvA R^ichastAsAM 'ekaiva vyAhR^itiH' ekameva vyAhartavyaM pratipAdyam | tachcha kim?  prANo viShNureva | kiJNcha ye sarve vedAH teShAmapi prANa eva pratipAdyaH| api cha ye samudrAdighoShAH teShAmapi, kimu vedAnAm | tatra R^ichastu visheShata indrAdinAmavato viShNorguNAn alpaj~nAnAmapi prakAshayantIti, prANe nArAyaNe tadviShayA eva 'vidyAt' tatpratipAdikA eveti jAnIyAdityarthaH | aitareyabhAShye tu - prathamaprANapadamapi viShayasaptamyantatayA vyAhR^itishabdaM cha vyAharaNaparatayA vyAkhyAya ekameva vyAharaNaM nirdoShaguNapUrtivAchakatvAdeka- prakArameva nAmetyarthaH uktaH | tattvapradIpespyayamevoktaH |
atha devarathaH 'tasya vAguddhiH shrotre pakShasI chakShuShI yukte manaH saN^gR^ihItA tadayaM prANosdhitiShThati' iti vAkyAntaraM atra prANasya deharathatvamuchyate | prameyAntarakathanArambhArthosthashabdaH | uchyata iti sheShaH| tathA cha devasya viShNoH vAyoH adhyAtmamadhidaivataM cha ratha uchyate ityarthaH | tasyAdhyAtmaM dehAkhyarathasya 'vAk' vAgAkhyA umA uddhiH dhAraNarajjurUpA adhidaivaM viShNurathasya prasiddhasyandanasya cha nAgAkAromA uddhiH 'shrotre' dakShavAmapArshvagatachandratadbhArye 'pakShasI' pArshvayuktAshvau anyatrAshvarUpau pArshvayoryuktau 'chakShuShI' ubhayapArshvagatasUryatadbhArye cha 'yukte' agrato niyuktAshvau 'mano' manosbhimAnI rudraH 'saN^gR^ihItA' sArathiH evam adhidaivaM prasiddhasyandanasyApi rudraH sArathiH | sa chAsAvayaM cha tadayamityekaM padam | tattvapradIparItyA bhinnapadatvespi taditi rathatayoktaM sharIraM parAmR^ishyate | liN^gavyatyayena taM rathamiti vA | ayaM prANo viShNuH vAyushchAdhitiShThatItyarthaH | liN^gena pUrvapakShite kathaM tenaiva siddhAnta ityAshaN^kA- nudayAya liN^gabAhulyoktiH | 
(4) nanu bAhulyena balavataH saiddhAntikaliN^gAdapi pUrvavAdyuktaliN^gameva balavat | niravakAshatvena svabhAvato balavattvAt | na chAvisheSheNanirNayaH, bAhulyena balavatospi svAbAvabalinaH prAbalyAt | yadAhuH -
dvividhaM balavattvaM cha bahutvAchcha svabhAvataH |
tayossvabhAvo balavAn upajIvyadikashcha saH ||
iti | ataH kathaM tairviShNutvanishchaya ityato devatopadeshyatvAdiliN^gAnAM niravakAshatvamapi smR^ityA sAdhayati 
- viShNumiti | devAH viShNumeva prAdhAnyena shiShyAdiShu j~nAnasampradAyapravartanena 'Anayan' upAdishan | bhUtimuddishya viShNumevopAsate | bhUtimiti vidheyavisheShaNaM vA | tathA cha viShNuM bhUtiM bhUtirj~nAnAdyaishvaryarUpa ityupAsate ityarthaH | 'saH' viShNurmukhyavAchyatayeti sheShaH, tenaivakAropapattiH | 'tadratho' viShNoreva rathaH | atraivakArasya dvirgrahaNAtsarvatrAnuShaN^gaH sUchitaH | tena sarvaliN^gAnAmapi niravagakAshatvamuktaM bhavati | skAnde ityanantaraM liN^gAnAmananyathAsiddhatvamuktamiti vAkyasheShaH | tathA chaikaprakAreNa prabalAtpUrvapakShiliN^gAtprakAradvayenApi prabalasya saiddhAntikaliN^gasyAdhikyena nirNayopa- pattiriti bhAvaH | abhyupetya chedamuditam | vastustu pUrvapakShiliN^gasya na niravakAshatvenApi prAbalyamasti, prANaiH sahagaNitatvasyAntaryAminiShThatAsambhavAt |
(5) yadA bahutvaniravakAshatvAkhyaprakAradvayenApi durbalaliN^gasyobhayathAprabalaliN^gato bAdhasambhavena tainaiva prANasya viShNutvasiddhiH, tadA kimu vAchyaM niravakAshabrahmashabdAbhyAsAditi bhAvenAnugamapadaM prakArAntareNa vyAchaShTe - brahmeti || asmin prakaraNe 'etadbrahma' (ai.A. 2-1-1.) 'brahmaNo lokaH' (ai.A. 2-1-3.) 'brahmemaM puruSham' (ai.A. 2-1-4.) 'udaraM brahmetyAchakShate' (ai.A. 2-1-4.) 'a iti brahma' (ai.A. 2-3-8.) ityAdi niravakAsha- brahmashabdAbhyAsAchchetyarthaH | etadviShNusvarUpaM brahma guNapUrNam | ayaM jIvo brahmaNaH parasyAshrayaH | imaM puruShaM chaturmukhaM parabrahma prApadyata | vAyuryatra sthita urveva garaNaM stavanaM chakre tatsthAnamudaraM tadgatamityarthaH |
(6) uktamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtraM paThitvAsskShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - neti || prANa ityanuvartate | tathA cha prANo viShNuriti na yuktam | kutaH?  'prANo vA ahamasmyR^iShe' iti vAkyena bR^ihatIsahasravakturvishvAmitrasyendreNa prANatayA AtmanaH svasyaivopadeshAdityarthaH | prANa indra eveti phaloktiH | na tUktahetoH sAdhyoktiH | 'prANo vAshamasmyR^iShe' iti vAkyaM tu 'tamindra uvAcha R^iShe priyaM vai me dhAmopAgAH varaM te dadAmIti | sa hovAcha tvAmeva jAnIyAmiti | tamindra uvAcha' iti pUrvavAkyena saha vyAkhyeyam| tatprakArastu - 'taM' vishvAmitraM 'indraH' tadantaHstho bhagavAnuvAcha | kimiti?  he R^iShe me priyaM dhAmopAgAH prApnuhi | te varaM dadAmIti | vaishabdosvadhAraNe prasiddhau vA|  evaM trivAraM shaMsanena dhAmashabditasAlokyaprAptibhagavatpuraprAptisAdhanabhagavatprasAdaM prAptaH 'saH' vishvAmitraH indrAviShTena hariNA varaM te dadAnIti punaruktassan uvAcha | kimiti?  tvAM sAmAnyataH pUrvam ahaM jAne | adhunA kIdR^ishastvamiti visheShato jAnIyAmiti | evamuktaH 'indraH' tadantargato hariH R^iShiM pratyuvAcha | kimiti?  he R^iShe ahaM prakR^iShTAnandarUpatvAtprANashabdavAchyossmIti | atra vAkyasamanvayapakShessmadAdiShUpapadeShu vihitAnAmasmItyAdi- tiN^antapadAnAM tadvR^itteH sulabhatvAditi tattvanirNayaTIkArItyA ahamitIndrAntaHsthena hariNA svAtmano nirdeshAdasmIti uttamapuruShopapattiH | pUrvapakShirItyA shrutyarthastu spaShTaH | ahaM prANossmIti padAnAM aheyatvaprakR^iShTAnandatvasaMhartR^itva- j~nAtR^itvanimittaiH bhagavati samanvayapakShe tu na tadanupapattiriti dhyeyam | naJNadhyAhAreNa siddAntAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti | anugamAdityanuvartate | netyAvartate | hishabdo yata ityarthe | asyoktamiti sheShaH | tathA chetthaM tattvapradIpaTIkoktA yojanA - nAyaM prANa indraH, kintu viShNureva | kutaH?  'anugamAt' prAguktaprabalatamaliN^gAdeH | tathA satyupadesha- virodha iti 
chet - na, kutaH?  yatostra prakaraNe svasthitasyaiva prathamaM 'prANo vA ahamasmyR^iShe' iti vAkyena paramAtmatvamuktamindreNa | tarhyaikyoktivirodha ityapi na | yatostra tasyaiva prANAkhyaparamAtmanaH 'prANastvaM prANaH sarvANi bhUtAni' ityevamAdivAkyena 'bahvadhyAtmasambandhaH' indrAdijIvarUpabahudehasambandhaH sarvagatatvameva R^iShiM prati indreNoktaM 'vidyate' asti natvaikyamata iti | sUtroktasambandhabAhulyaM sambandhini paryavasyatItyAshayena bahvityuktam | bhUmashabdasya bhAvavAchitvespi bhAvabhavitrorabhedAt bhavitari prayogaH | sUtre tu paranipAta ArShaH | athavA - adhikashchAsAvAtmA chAdhyAtmA tasya sambandhaH bahushchAsAvadhyAtmasambandhashcheti vigrahaH | tathA cha 'hi' yataH 'atra' indre 'bahuH' bahulaH paramAtmasambandhaH sannidhivisheSho vidyata ityarthaH | vidyata ityanantaraM tadapekShayAsyam upadesho na svApekShayeti sheShaH | tathAchendre tAtkAlikeshvarasannidhAnavisheShAbhiprAyA 'prANo vA aham' ityuktiH, na svApekShayeti nopadeshavirodha iti bhAvaH | kuto na svApekShayetyataH prANastavamityAdyAha | yojanA tu - hi yasmAt 'prANastvam' ityAdi vAkyenAsya prANasya 'bahvadhyAtmasambandhaH' adhyAtmatvenAntaryAmitvena indrAdirUpabahudehasambandhaH sarvagatatva- muktaM vidyate na chaitadatra jIvavisheShendre vidyate yujyate tasmAditi | prathamapakShe 'yasyAtmA sharIram' (mAdhyandina) iti shruterindrAdInAM viShNudehatvAdaikyavyapadeshaH sharIrasharIribhAvanibandhana iti j~nApanAyAdhyAtmetyuktiH | anena bR^ihatI- sahasravakturvishvAmitrasya taM pratIndreNa prANatayAsstmopadeshAdayaM prANo na viShNuH, kintu indra eveti chet - nendrosyaM prANaH, kintu viShNureva | kutaH?  anugamAt  prAguktabalatamaliN^gAdeH | na chopadeshavirodhaH | yatosyamindragatA- dhyAtmaviShaya eva | kutaH?  hi yasmAdasmin prakaraNesdhyAtmasambandhabhUmA | atrAdhyAtmasambandhashabdenAtmAdhikAre vartamAnamiti | adhishchAsau AtmA cheti dehaH paramAtmA chochyate | tathA cha yasmAdadhyAtmano viShNorindravishvA- mitrAdidehasambandha uktossti tasmAt | athavA - hi yasmAt asminnindre adhyAtmasambandhabhUmA - adhirIshvare - adhikasyAtmanaH paramAtmanaH sambandhasyAveshasya bhUmA bAhulyaM vidyate tasmAdupadeshasya sannihitaparamAtma- viShayatvopapteriti bhAvaH | tadapi kutaH?  hi yasmAt asmin prakaraNesdhyAtmasambandhabhUmoktaH tasmAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati |
(7) nanu yadi prANashabdenendreNApi viShNureva svAtmAdisarvagatatayochyate tarhi mayi prANa iti nirdeshaH syAt | na tvahamiti | viShNAvahamityAdirUpopadeshAyogAdityAshaN^kAM pariharatsUtraM paThati - shAstreti || turevArthospyarthaH, yatha ityarthe smR^itisUchakashcha | yujyata iti sheShaH | tathA cha yatospi prANasya viShNutvespyupadeshaH prANo vAsham ityevaMrUpo yujyate, ato na tadanupapattiH | kathamayaM yujyate? yatosyamupadeshaH 'shAstradR^iShTyA' shAsti sarvamiti shAstraM antaryAmI bhagavAn, taddR^iShTyA tadapekShayaiva pravR^itto na tvaikyena | na chAntaryAmiNi ahamAdiprayogAdarshanAt tadayogaH | yato 'vAmadevavat' tatkartR^ikaprayoga- vat | yathA vAmadevo nAma R^iShiH antaryAmivivakShayA 'ahaM manurabhavam' iti svasmin ahaMmanvAdishabdAn prayuyuje | tathA ayamapyupadesho yujyate ata iti sUtrayojanAmabhiprayan sautrashAstrapadaM vyAchaShTe - shAstramiti | viShNuriti sheShaH | tathAchAntaryAmI viShNariha shAstrapadenokta ityarthaH | antaryAmIti prakR^itAbhiprAyeNa | yadvA - shAsti prerayati sarvAniti vyutapattyA antaryAmItyetadeva shAstramityasya vyAkhyAnaM bhavatIti 
nApadArthatvashaN^kAvakAshaH | ata eva bhAgavate dhyeyesntaryAmiNyeva shAstrashabdaprayogaH| aitareyabhAShye 'shAsturantaryAmiNaH' iti shAstR^ishabdaM mUlIkR^itya vyAkhyAnespi, tadanusAreNa cha tattvapradIpe shAsturantaryAmiNo viShNoriti vyAkhyAnepi nAsya tadvirodhaH shaN^kyaH, yatastatparyAyashabdavyAkhyAnenaiva shAstrashabdo vyAkhyAto bhavatItyAshayena shAstrashabdaparyAyashAstR^ishabdo vyAkhyAyate | yadvA - shAstrashabde shAstR^i a ityavayavavibhAgamabhipretya shAstrityaMshasyAntaryAmiNa ityanena ashabdasya viShNorityanena cha vyAkhyAtattvAt, atra tu avayavavibhAgamavivakShitvA shAstramityakhaNDapadasyAntaryAmiti vyAkhyAnAt tadanukUlatayA 'saMvichChAstram' iti vachanopanyAsAchcha na virodhaH |
(8) antaryAmiNo viShNoH shAstrapadavAchyatve pramANamAha - saMviditi || prathamaskandhe vyAsaM prati nAradavAkyamidam |
svapno mAyAsgrahaH shayyA jAgradAbhAsa AtmanaH |
nAmarUpakriyAvR^ittiH saMvichChAstraM paraM padam || iti |
asyArthaH - Atmano jIvasya mAyAvAsanAkhyasaMskAropAdAnakavastuj~nAnarUpaH svapnaH | agrahaH jAgratsvapnaviShaya- j~nAnarahitA shayyA suShuptiH nAmarUpakriyAsu shabdArthakarmasu vR^ittirvyAvR^ittiryanyAH sA | AbhAsaH pratyayaH saMj~nAdiviShayaj~nAnarUpo jAgrachcha | AhatyaitadavasthAtrayaM yasmAdAtmanaH parabrahmaNo bhavati, tatsaMvit sarvaviShayaka- yathArthaj~nAnarUpaM sarvaj~naM vA | shAstraM sarvaniyantR^i, paraM uttamaM padaM sadbhiH prApyaM brahma aham achintayamiti | bhAgavata ityanantaraM 'prayogAt' iti sheShaH | asyAntaryAmItyanenAnvayaH |
(9) nanvantaryAmiNi ahamAdiprayogaH kathaM sambhavatItyAshaN^kyAM tatra tushabdasUchitAM smR^itimevAha - tattaditi| viShNuH 'tattannAtmA' anyaparatvena prasiddhAhamAdinAmnochyate iti | anena tasyAntaryAmiNi viShNau vidvadrUDhirdarshitA | 'sarvashAstR^itvahetutaH' sarvaniyantR^itvanimitteneti | anena mahAyogo darshitaH | tatra tasya svAtantryanimittokteH | anena paramata ivAsmanmatespi lAkShaNikatvaM parihR^itam 'puruShottamam' antaryAmiNaM viShNuM 'R^ite' vinA, anyatra 'kvApi' jIvAdau 'kiM chit' ahamAdirUpaM 'nAma' vAchakatayA nAstIti | anena harau paramamukhyatA anyatra kevalamukhyatA choktA | anyathA na kvApIti sAmAnyaniShedhAyogAt | atrAhamAdishabdAH pratyagAdivAchitvena prasiddhAH, pratyagAdayashcha sarvadA piNDIbhUtAH, tAnavivekenAj~nAH kevalajIvAdau prayuJNjate dahati shabdamiva kAShThe | prAj~nAstu mukhyAmukhyavivekavanto hyamukhmarthamanAdR^itya mukhyArthe harau prayuJNjataiti tattvanirNaTIkoktamanusandheyam | 'pAdme' ityanantaram 'antaryAmiNyahamAdipadAnAM mukhyatvokteH shAstradR^iShTyA ahamAdyupadesho yukta eva' iti vAkyasheShaH |
(10) nanvantaryAmiNi ahamAdiprayogAdarshanAt tadayoga ityAshaN^kAM sUtroktadR^iShTAntavivaraNena pariharati - ahamiti || 'ahaM' vAmadevasaMj~nakaR^iShyantaryAmI tattadantaryAmitayA manuH sUryashchAbhavamiti R^iN^mantrArthaH | Adipadena 'ahaM kakShIvAnR^iShirasmi viproshaM kutsam' (R^i.4-26-1.) ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | 'ityAdivat' evamAdiprayogavadityasya 'shAstradR^iShTyopadeshaH' ityanenAnvayaH |
(11) punaruktamAkShipya samAdadhatsUtramupanyasya AkShepAMshaM tAvadvyAchaShTe - jIveti || anusandhIyate 
uktamiti cha sheShaH | saMvAdo vivAdaH kalahaH prANasya prANaissaha saMvAda iti vigrahaH | tathA cha yasmAdatra prakaraNe 'taM shataM varShANyabhyArchat tasmAchChataM varShANi puruShAyuSho bhavanti' (ai.A. 2-2-1.) ityanena yachChatasaMvatsaraparyantaM prANasya jIvadehesvastAnahetukaM shatAyuShTvarUpaM jIvaliN^gamuktaM tat 'tAvanti shatasaMvatsarasyAhnAM sahasrANi bhavanti' ityAdinA bahuShu sthaleShu anusandhIyate | yasmAchcha 'tA ahiMsantAhamukthamahamukthamasmi' (ai.A. 2-1-4.) iti vAkyena prANasya prANairindriyaiH saha saMvAdarUpa- mukhyaprANaliN^gamuktam | yasmAchchAdipadagR^ihItaM 'prANo vaMsha iti sthaviraH shAkalyastadyathA shAlAvaMshe sarvesnye vaMshAH samAhitAssyuH evamasmin prANe chakShushshrotraM mano vAgindriyANi sharIraM sarva AtmA samAhitaH' (ai.A. 3-2-1-1.) iti vAkyena sarvajIvendriyadehadhArakatvarUpaliN^gaM choktamasti tasmAdayaM prANo na viShNuH, kintu jIvamukhyaprANAveveti yojanA | yadyapi 'tasmAchChataM varShANi puruShAyuSho bhavanti' (ai.A. 2-2-1.) iti shatAyuShTvaliN^gapratipAdakavAkyamevodAharaNIyaM, na tu 'tAvanti' iti vAkyam | tathAspi liN^gasya bahuShu sthaleShu anugamosstIti j~nApanAyopaniShado jIvaliN^ge tAtparyamastIti j~nApayitum anusandhivAkyamevodAhR^itam | siddhAnte shrutyarthastu - puruShAyuShaH shatasaMvatsarasyAhnAM sahasrANi shatasaMvatsarAntaH- praviShTAharniyAmakasUryagatabhagavatpuruSharUpANi tAvanti sahasrANi | kiyanti?  bR^ihatIsahasragatAkSharANAM vAchyAni puMrUpANi yAvanti sahasrANi tAvanti | tathA cha tAni ShaTtriMshatsahasrANi sampannAni bhavanti | 'tAH' chakShurAdi- devatAH 'ahiMsanta' vivAdamakurvan | kinviti? ahamasya chaturmukhadehasyokthossmi utthApakossmIti |
(12) parihArAMshaM vyAchaShTe - neti || prANo viShNurneti na, kintu viShNurevAyaM, na jIvAdirityarthaH | kuto netyatastatra prAguktAnugamahetvanuShaN^gaM, na choktajIvamukhyaprANaliN^gavirodha ityatastatrahetutvena yataH shAstradR^iShTyA tvayamupadeshaH ityasyAnuShaN^gaM, kimarthamantaryAmIti prashnasyAntarupAstyarthamiti parihAraM chAbhipretya na chopAsanes- vAntarabhedAbhAva iti chodyottaratvena pravR^ittam 'upAsA' iti sUtrAMshaM vyAchaShTe - antariti | gatatvenetyasyAntarbahi- ssarvashabdaiH pratyekaM sambandhaH | itishabdaH prakArArthaH | tathA cha dehAntargatatvena tadbahirgatatvena sarvagatatveneti prakAreNa 'upAsAtraividhyAt' bhagavadupAsanasya trividhatvAdityarthaH| nanu tathApi kathanaM vyarthaM vastuta upAsanAtraividhya- syehAnuktasyAntaryAmikathanAprayojakatvAdityataH pravR^ittam 'AshritatvAt' ityaMshaM chashabdAdhyAhAreNa vyAchaShTe - iheti | etatprakaraNe uktatvAdityarthaH | upAsAtraividhyasyeti vipariNAmenAtrAnvIyate | cho hetUpapAdakahetusamuchchaye | tathA cha atroktatraividhyAntargatAntaropAsanArthamantaryAmikathanaM yuktamiti bhAvaH |
(13) atropAsanAtraividhyamuchyata ityatrApi kiM liN^gamityata Aha - sa iti | 'saH' vAsudevo bhagavAn 'etameva sImAnaM' shiromadhyaM vidAryaiva 'etayA dvArA' suShumnAnADyA 'prApadyata' prAptaH | chaturmukhahR^idayamiti sheShaH | anena bhagavato dehAntaHpraveshokteH ukteshchopAsanArthatvAt antarupAstiruktA bhavati | 'saH' chaturmukhadehe prAkprapadAbhyAmantaH praviShTo nArAyaNaH 'etameva puruShaM' vyAsakR^iShNakapilAdirUpamAtmAnam AtataguNaM svasvarUpa- bhUtamAdAnAdikartAraM vA | tatamaM 'lopaH samAne' iti sUtrAttalopaH | tamabarthe mapratyayo vA | tathA cha tatamaM atishayena vyAptaM niravadhikavyAptimantaM 'brahma' 
guNapUrNam 'apashyat' tadguNakatayA tadrUpaM dadarshetyarthaH | kechittu - takAra eva vyAptyabhidhAyaka ityAhuH | anena sarvagatatvaM tathopAsanArthamuktam | 'tadetat' prakR^itaM sarvaM 'vidvAn' jAnannaitareyaH itarAyA apatyaM pumAn vishAlasaMj~nAt R^iSheH utpannaH aitareyaH | 'mahidAso' mahino mahAtmAno devAH dAsabhUtAH yasyAsau bhagavAnAhetyarthaH | hasmavaishabdAH prasiddhidyotakAH | atra bahirupAstyarthaM mahidAsa Aheti bahirupAstiruktA bhavati | na cha vAchyamatra svarUpamAtramuchyate, nopAsanArthamiti | upAsanAM vinoktiprayojanA- bhAvAt | ityAdinetyasyetyAdinAvAkyenopAsanAtraividhyasyAshritatvAdarthAduktatvAdi- tyanvayaH | Adishabdena 'taM prapadAbhyAM prApadyata brahmemaM puruShametasyAmetam' (ai.A. 2-1-4.) ityAdikaM gR^ihyate | nanu 'etaddhasmavai tadvidvAnAha hiraNyadanvaidaH' (ai.A. 2-1-5.) itivanmahidAsospi R^iShitvenochyatAmiti chenna | asyAH upaniShadaH aitareyasaMj~na- yaivetarAputrasya mahidAsasya R^iShitvasiddhyA taduktervyarthatvAt |
(14) tathAspi mahidAsasya viShNutvaM kuto j~nAyata ityata Aha - mahidAseti || 'jaj~ne' vyakto babhUva | 'sa cha' mahidAsaH -
mahidAsastvaitareyo bahvR^ichopaniShadgataH |
sAkShAtsa bhagavAnviShNustannAmaiko munirhyabhUt ||
iti ChAndogyabhAShye anantaroktabhagavadanyaH tatsaMj~naketarAputraH R^iShiratra na vivakShitaH, kintu | yo 'vaiShNavaM' viShNuviShayaM 'tantraM' granthaM 'vyadhAt' nirmame | yadvA - 'tantraM' paJNcharAtraM vyadhAt nAradAdibhyo vyAchakhyau | yashcha 'sAkShAt' svayaM 'bhagavAn' pUrNaj~nAnAdimAn 'viShNuH' tadavatArabhUtaH pUrvoktaH sa evAtra vivakShita ityAha - sAkShAditi| brahmANDe purANa ityasyAshritatvAdityanenAnvayaH | mahidAsasya viShNutvoktiriti tadarthaH | tena chashabdAnvayaH |
(15) nanvekavidhopAsanayA sarveShAM brahmAparokShasambhavAtkimupAsAtraividhyena ityataH pravR^ittaM 'tadyogAt' iti sUtrasheShaM vyAchaShTe - tattaditi || upAsanetyanena puruShANAmityanena cha tadityasyAvR^ittiH sUchitA | chaH samuchchaye | tathA cha teShAM puruShANAM manuShyarShigandharvadevAkhyAdhikAriNAM teShu trividhopAsaneShu madhye tattadupAsane yathAkramaM bahirantarvyAptirUpaikaikopAsana eva yogyatayA yogyatvena hetunetyarthaH | asyopAsAtraividhyAdityanenAnvayaH | tathA chAnekavidhopAstiyogyatAvatAmadhikAriNAM naikavidhopAsanayA brahmaj~nAnamiti tattraividhyamAvashyakamiti bhAvaH |
(16) puruShANAmuktAnekavidhopAsanayogyatA kuto j~nAyata ityataH kartR^ivisheShAnanupAdAya sAmAnyataH upAsakatraividhyapratipAdikAM smR^itiM paThati - keShAJNchiditi || 'puruShottamo' hariH 'keShAJNchit' devAnAM devaiH sarvagatatvena prakAreNopAsyaH | 'keShAJNchit' R^iShigandharvAdInAM 'hR^idaye' svasvahR^idayAkAshe upAsyaH | 'keShAJNchit' manuShyottamAnAM tu bahirevopAsya ityarthaH | prAchuryAdevamuktiH | iti brAhma ityasya tattadupAsanayogyatayA tadvishiShTatvena puruShANAmAshritatvAduktatvAditi pUrveNAnvayaH |
(17) atraivAdhikaraNe kartR^ivisheShapratipAdakaM visheShapramANamAha - agnAviti || viShNuH 'kriyAvatAM' 
yaj~nAdikriyAnuShThAtR^iNAm 'agnau' gArhapatyAdau upAsyaH hariH | 'yoginAm' R^iShINAM hR^idaye upAsyaH | 'aprabuddhAnAM' mandamatInAM atyalpapratibhAnAM manuShyottamAnAM 'pratimAsu' kR^iShNarAmAdivigraheShu upAsyaH | 'viditAtmanAM' visheShato j~nAtabhagavadrUpANAm ashrutapratibhAnAM devAnAM tu 'sarvatra' sarvasthAneShUpAsya ityarthaH | atrAgnau pratimAsviti vAkyadvayena bahirmAtropAsanopalakShyate | ata eva sthAnadvayoktiH | yathAshruteH sUryAdau viShNUpAsterbahirupAstitvaM na syAt | yoginAmityanenAntarupAstiruktA | 'R^iShayosntaHprakAshAH' () iti shruteH | sarvatreti sarvagatopAstiriti j~nAtavyam | na chAtra "yeShAM bahirupAsanena mokShasteShAmapi hR^idyupAsanaM kiJNchitkAryameva" iti bR^ihadbhAShyeNa "bhagavAn bimbadarshanenainaM mochayati" iti nyAyavivaraNena cha virodhashshaN^kyaH | agnAviti vAkyesnyaniShedhAbhAvena bimbashabditasvasvayogyAtmAparokShArthaM hR^idyupAsanasyApi sarvaiH kAryatvAbhyupagamAt | mochakayogyAparokShadvArAbhUtA- vatArAdyaparokShasAdhanopAsanAya eva taistaiH prAchuryeNa prakaraNasyAgnAviti vAkyena vyavasthayA pratipAdanAchcha | iti cheti | chaH samuchchaye | vachanadvayasyApyekArthasAdhakatvAdasyApi brAhme AshritatvAditi pUrveNAnvayaH | tattadupAsana- yogyatAvattvena puruShavisheShANAmuktatvAditi tadarthaH | ato na tadyogAditi hetvasiddhiH shaN^kyeti bhAva |
anena nAtroktaprANo viShNuH, kintu jIvamukhyaprANAveva | kutaH? 'jIvamukhyaprANaliN^gAt' shatAyuShTvarUpa- jIvaliN^gasyaprANasaMvAdAdirUpamukhyaprANaliN^gasya cheha shravaNAditi chet - na, viShNurevAyaM prANaH, na jIvAdiH | kutaH? 'anugamAt' hetoreva, na chAnyashrutiliN^gavirodhaH | uktarItyA 'tadyogAt' teShAmantaryAmiviShayatvopapatteH | yatashshAstradR^iShTyAsyam upadesha iti vA | kimarthamatrAntaryAmikathanamiti chet, antarupAstyarthamiti brUmaH | na chopAsanesvAntarabhedAbhAvaH | 'upAsAtraividhyAt' antarAdibhedena bhagavadupAsanasya trividhatvAt | na cha tathApi kathanamayuktam | vAstavatraividhyasyehAnuktasya kathanAprayojakatvAditi vAchyam | 'iha' prakaraNe tatraividhyasyA- shritatvAduktatvAt | na chaikavidhopAsanayA sarveShAM brahmAparokShasambhavAt kimupAsAtraividhyeneti vAchyam | 'tadyogAt' teShAM puruShANAM tasmin tadupAsana eva yogyatvAt | anekavidhopAstiyogyatAvatAM cha puruShANAM ekavidhapAsanayAsparokShAsambhavena yogyatAbhedA- dupAsAtraividhyasyAvashyakatvAditi sUtrArtha ukto bhavati | na cha vivAdakartR^itvaliN^gasyAntaryAmiviShayatve 'udAsInau cha tAvAstAM keshavashchAbjasambhavaH' iti vachanavirodhaH shaN^kyaH | tasyAntaryAmiviShayabhinnabAhyarUpaviShayatvAt | atosnyaliN^gAnAM tattadantaryAmiviShayatvopapatteH tadvirodhAbhAvAt | viShNurevAyaM prANaH Anandamayashcheti yuktA tajjij~nAseti siddham |
|| iti pAdAntyaprANAdhikaraNam ||
iti shrImatparamahaMsaparivrAjakAchAryANAM sarvatantrasvatantrANaAM
shrImadraghunAthatIrthapUjyapAdAnAM shiShyeNa
shrImajjagannAthayatinA kR^itAyAM
shrImadbrahmasUtrabhAShyadIpikAyAM
prathamAdhyAyasya prathamaH pAdaH 
|| om ||
